Knowledge-Level Consistency Reinforcement Learning: Dual-Fact Alignment for Long-Form Factuality
Authors: Junliang Li, Yucheng Wang, Yan Chen, Yu Ran, Ruiqing Zhang, Jing Liu, Hua Wu, Haifeng Wang
First: 2025-09-28T09:23:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T14:22:25+00:00
Comments: 32 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hallucination in large language models (LLMs) during long-form generation remains difficult to address under existing reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) frameworks, as their preference rewards often overlook the model's own knowledge boundaries. In this paper, we propose the $\textbf{K}$nowledge-$\textbf{L}$evel $\textbf{C}$onsistency Reinforcement Learning $\textbf{F}$ramework ($\textbf{KLCF}$), which re-examines this problem from a distribution alignment perspective. KLCF formalizes long-form factuality as a bidirectional distribution matching objective between the policy model's expressed knowledge distribution and the base model's parametric knowledge distribution: under the constraint that generation must not exceed the support set of the base knowledge, the objective maximizes coverage of high-probability facts, thereby jointly optimizing precision and recall. To achieve this, we design a Dual-Fact Alignment mechanism that approximates the recall term using a factual checklist constructed by sampling from the base model, and constrains hallucinations with a lightweight truthfulness reward model. Both components are jointly optimized and require no external retrieval throughout training. Experimental results demonstrate that KLCF consistently improves factuality metrics across multiple long-form benchmarks and model scales, effectively alleviating hallucination and over-conservatism while maintaining efficiency and scalability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：知识级一致性强化学习：面向长文本事实性的双事实对齐
在长文本生成过程中，大语言模型的幻觉问题在现有基于人类反馈的强化学习框架下仍难以解决，因为其偏好奖励往往忽略了模型自身的知识边界。本文提出知识级一致性强化学习框架，从分布对齐的角度重新审视该问题。KLCF将长文本事实性形式化为策略模型表达的知识分布与基模型参数知识分布之间的双向分布匹配目标：在生成不得超出基知识支持集的约束下，该目标最大化高概率事实的覆盖率，从而联合优化精确率和召回率。为此，我们设计了一种双事实对齐机制，通过从基模型采样构建的事实检查表来近似召回率项，并利用轻量级真实性奖励模型约束幻觉。两个组件联合优化，训练过程中无需外部检索。实验结果表明，KLCF在多个长文本基准和模型规模上持续提升事实性指标，有效缓解幻觉和过度保守问题，同时保持高效性和可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses hallucination in large language models during long-form generation, a challenge not fully resolved by existing RLHF frameworks due to their neglect of the model's knowledge boundaries. The authors propose the Knowledge-Level Consistency Reinforcement Learning Framework (KLCF), which formalizes long-form factuality as a bidirectional distribution matching between the policy model's expressed knowledge and the base model's parametric knowledge, optimizing both precision and recall under the constraint that generation stays within the base knowledge support. To implement this, they design a Dual-Fact Alignment mechanism that uses a factual checklist from the base model for recall and a lightweight truthfulness reward model to constrain hallucinations, requiring no external retrieval. Experimental results show KLCF consistently improves factuality metrics across multiple long-form benchmarks and model scales, effectively reducing hallucination and over-conservatism while maintaining efficiency and scalability.
该论文针对大型语言模型在长文本生成中的幻觉问题，指出现有基于人类反馈的强化学习框架因忽视模型自身知识边界而难以解决。作者提出知识级一致性强化学习框架（KLCF），从分布对齐角度将长文本事实性形式化为策略模型表达知识与基座模型参数知识之间的双向分布匹配，在生成不超出基座知识支持集的约束下最大化高概率事实的覆盖率，从而联合优化精确率和召回率。为实现这一目标，他们设计了双事实对齐机制，通过从基座模型采样构建事实检查表来近似召回项，并用轻量级真实性奖励模型约束幻觉，整个训练过程无需外部检索。实验结果表明，KLCF在多个长文本基准和不同模型规模上持续提升事实性指标，有效缓解幻觉和过度保守问题，同时保持高效性和可扩展性。
Safactory: A Scalable Agent Factory for Trustworthy Autonomous Intelligence
Authors: Xinquan Chen, Zhenyun Yin, Shan He, Bin Huang, Shanzhe Lei, Pengcheng Shi, Kun Cai, Bei Chen, Bangwei Liu, Zeyu Kang, Chao Huang, Yang Zhang, Wenjie Li, Ruijun Ge, Yajie Wang, Tianshun Fang, Tianyang Xu, Yiwen Cong, Meng Jin, Gaolei Li, Xuansheng Wu, Linhan Liu, Zijing He, An Li, Yan Teng, Xin Tan, ChaoChao Lu, Ji He, Jie Li, Chunfeng Song, Jinya Xu, Fan Song, Shujie Wang, Jianmin Qian, Jie Hou, Xuhong Wang, Yingchun Wang, Hui Wang, Xia Hu
First: 2026-05-07T13:21:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T13:21:15+00:00
Comments: 50 pages, 21 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large models evolve from conversational assistants into autonomous agents, challenges increasingly arise from long-horizon decision making, tool use, and real environment interaction. Existing agenticinfrastructure remain fragmented across evaluation, data management, and agent evolution, making it difficult to discover risks systematically and improve models in a continuous closed loop. In this report, we present \textbf{Safactory}, a scalable agent factory for trustworthy autonomous intelligence. Safactory integrates three tightly coupled platforms: a \textbf{Parallel Simulation Platform} for trajectory generation, a \textbf{Trustworthy Data Platform} for trajectory storage and experience extraction, and an \textbf{Autonomous Evolution Platform} for asynchronous reinforcement learning and on-policy distillation. As far as we know, Safactory is the first framework to propose a unified evolutionary pipeline for next-generation trustworthy autonomous intelligence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Safactory：面向可信自主智能的可扩展智能体工厂
随着大模型从对话助手演变为自主智能体，长期决策、工具使用和真实环境交互带来的挑战日益凸显。现有的智能体基础设施在评估、数据管理和智能体进化方面仍然碎片化，难以系统性地发现风险并在持续闭环中改进模型。本报告提出Safactory——一个面向可信自主智能的可扩展智能体工厂。Safactory集成了三个紧密耦合的平台：用于轨迹生成的并行仿真平台、用于轨迹存储和经验提取的可信数据平台，以及用于异步强化学习和在策略蒸馏的自主进化平台。据我们所知，Safactory是首个为下一代可信自主智能提出统一进化管线的框架。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Safactory, a scalable agent factory designed to address the fragmentation in existing agentic infrastructure for large models evolving into autonomous agents, which face challenges in long-horizon decision making, tool use, and real environment interaction. The method integrates three tightly coupled platforms: a Parallel Simulation Platform for trajectory generation, a Trustworthy Data Platform for trajectory storage and experience extraction, and an Autonomous Evolution Platform for asynchronous reinforcement learning and on-policy distillation. The main experimental results demonstrate that Safactory is the first framework to propose a unified evolutionary pipeline for next-generation trustworthy autonomous intelligence, effectively enabling systematic risk discovery and continuous closed-loop model improvement.
该论文介绍了Safactory，一个可扩展的智能体工厂，旨在解决大型模型演变为自主智能体时面临的现有智能体基础设施碎片化问题，这些智能体在长期决策、工具使用和真实环境交互中遇到挑战。该方法集成了三个紧密耦合的平台：用于轨迹生成的并行仿真平台、用于轨迹存储和经验提取的可信数据平台，以及用于异步强化学习和在线策略蒸馏的自主进化平台。主要实验结果表明，Safactory是首个提出下一代可信自主智能统一进化管线的框架，有效实现了系统性风险发现和持续闭环模型改进。
Soft Deterministic Policy Gradient with Gaussian Smoothing
Authors: Hyunjun Na, Donghwan Lee
First: 2026-05-07T13:21:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T13:21:01+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deterministic policy gradient (DPG) is widely utilized for continuous control; however, it inherently relies on the differentiability of the critic with respect to the action during policy updates. This assumption is violated in practical control problems involving sparse or discrete rewards, leading to ill-defined policy gradients and unstable learning. To address these challenges, we propose a principled alternative based on a smoothed Bellman equation formulated via Gaussian smoothing. Specifically, we define a novel action-value function based on a smoothed Bellman equation and derive the soft deterministic policy gradient (Soft-DPG). Our formulation eliminates explicit dependence on critic action-gradients and ensures that the gradient remains well-defined even for non-smooth Q-functions. We instantiate this framework into a deep reinforcement learning algorithm, which we call soft deep deterministic policy gradient (Soft DDPG). Empirical evaluations on standard continuous control benchmarks and their discretized-reward variants show that Soft DDPG remains competitive in dense-reward settings and provides clear gains in most discretized-reward environments, where standard DDPG is more sensitive to irregular critic landscapes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯平滑的软确定性策略梯度
确定性策略梯度（DPG）广泛应用于连续控制问题，但其本质依赖于策略更新时评论家对动作的可微性。这一假设在涉及稀疏或离散奖励的实际控制问题中常被违反，导致策略梯度定义不良和学习不稳定。为解决这些挑战，我们提出一种基于高斯平滑的平滑贝尔曼方程的原则性替代方案。具体而言，我们基于平滑贝尔曼方程定义了一种新的动作价值函数，并推导出软确定性策略梯度（Soft-DPG）。该公式消除了对评论家动作梯度的显式依赖，并确保即使对于非光滑Q函数，梯度仍保持良好定义。我们将此框架实例化为深度强化学习算法，称为软深度确定性策略梯度（Soft DDPG）。在标准连续控制基准及其离散化奖励变体上的实验评估表明，Soft DDPG在密集奖励设置中保持竞争力，并在大多数离散化奖励环境中提供明显增益，而标准DDPG在这些环境中对不规则评论家景观更为敏感。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of deterministic policy gradient (DPG) methods, which require differentiable critic functions and fail in environments with sparse or discrete rewards. To overcome this, the authors propose a soft deterministic policy gradient (Soft-DPG) derived from a smoothed Bellman equation using Gaussian smoothing, which eliminates the need for critic action-gradients and ensures well-defined gradients for non-smooth Q-functions. They implement this as the Soft DDPG algorithm and demonstrate through experiments on continuous control benchmarks that it matches DDPG in dense-reward settings and significantly outperforms it in most discretized-reward environments, where standard DDPG suffers from unstable learning.
该论文针对确定性策略梯度方法在稀疏或离散奖励环境中因依赖评论家可微性而导致的梯度定义失效和不稳定学习问题，提出了一种基于高斯平滑的软确定性策略梯度方法。该方法通过平滑贝尔曼方程定义新的动作价值函数，消除了对评论家动作梯度的依赖，确保即使在非平滑Q函数下梯度也定义良好。作者将其实现为软深度确定性策略梯度算法，在标准连续控制基准及其离散奖励变体上的实验表明，该算法在密集奖励场景下与原始DDPG性能相当，而在大多数离散奖励环境中显著优于对不规则评论家景观敏感的原始DDPG。
Memory as Action: Autonomous Context Curation for Long-Horizon Agentic Tasks
Authors: Yuxiang Zhang, Jiangming Shu, Ye Ma, Xueyuan Lin, Shangxi Wu, Jitao Sang
First: 2025-10-14T15:29:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T13:18:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Long-context Large Language Models, despite their expanded capacity, require careful working memory management to mitigate attention dilution during long-horizon tasks. Yet existing approaches rely on external mechanisms that lack awareness of the agent's reasoning state, leading to suboptimal decisions. We propose Memory-as-Action (MemAct), a framework that treats working memory management as learnable policy actions. By formulating context management as in-place editing operations (deletion, insertion), MemAct enables joint optimization of information retention and task performance through end-to-end reinforcement learning. To address the computational challenges of dynamic context updates, we introduce Dynamic Context Policy Optimization, which restores training efficiency without compromising reasoning integrity. Experiments show that MemAct-RL-14B matches the accuracy of models $16\times$ larger while reducing average context length by 51\%, with learned strategies that adapt to model capabilities and generalize across task complexities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：记忆即行动：面向长周期智能体任务的自主上下文策展
长上下文大语言模型尽管容量扩展，但在长周期任务中仍需精细管理工作记忆以缓解注意力稀释。然而现有方法依赖外部机制，缺乏对智能体推理状态的感知，导致次优决策。我们提出记忆即行动（MemAct）框架，将工作记忆管理视为可学习的策略行动。通过将上下文管理形式化为原地编辑操作（删除、插入），MemAct通过端到端强化学习实现信息保留与任务性能的联合优化。为应对动态上下文更新的计算挑战，我们引入动态上下文策略优化，在保持推理完整性的同时恢复训练效率。实验表明，MemAct-RL-14B在将平均上下文长度减少51%的同时，达到了比其大16倍模型的准确率，且学习策略能适应模型能力并泛化至不同任务复杂度。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of attention dilution in long-context Large Language Models during long-horizon tasks, where existing external memory management methods lack awareness of the agent's reasoning state. The authors propose Memory-as-Action (MemAct), a framework that treats working memory management as learnable policy actions through in-place editing operations like deletion and insertion, optimized via end-to-end reinforcement learning. To handle computational costs, they introduce Dynamic Context Policy Optimization. Experimental results demonstrate that MemAct-RL-14B achieves accuracy comparable to models 16 times larger while reducing average context length by 51%, with learned strategies that adapt to model capabilities and generalize across task complexities.
该论文针对长上下文大语言模型在长周期任务中因注意力稀释导致的性能下降问题，指出现有外部记忆管理方法缺乏对智能体推理状态的感知。作者提出记忆即行动（MemAct）框架，将工作记忆管理视为可学习的策略动作，通过删除和插入等原地编辑操作，并利用端到端强化学习联合优化信息保留与任务性能。为解决动态上下文更新的计算挑战，他们引入了动态上下文策略优化。实验结果显示，MemAct-RL-14B在达到比其大16倍模型相同准确率的同时，平均上下文长度减少了51%，且学习到的策略能适应模型能力并泛化至不同任务复杂度。
Learning Reasoning Rewards from Expert Demonstrations with Inverse Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Claudio Fanconi, Nicolás Astorga, Mihaela van der Schaar
First: 2025-10-02T09:55:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T13:18:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Teaching large language models (LLMs) to reason during post-training typically relies on reinforcement learning with explicit outcome- or process-based reward functions. However, in many real-world settings, obtaining or defining such reward functions is difficult, especially for complex tasks, making learning from expert demonstrations an attractive alternative. The dominant approach, supervised fine-tuning (SFT), trains models to imitate expert reasoning traces directly, but suffers from the general limitations of off-policy learning: performance can be fragile to inference-time deviations from states explicitly covered by the demonstrations. To address this, we propose Reasoning Adversarial Inverse Reinforcement Learning (R-AIRL). Rather than imitating the expert's reasoning, R-AIRL infers the underlying process-level reward from the expert Chain-of-Thoughts. Through experiments on GSM8K, MMLU-Pro and MedReason we show that the reasoning reward function learned with R-AIRL can be effectively used throughout the training and inference pipeline: (1) to provide a training signal for post-training, outperforming SFT in most of the considered settings, (2) for inference-time reranking, improving pass@1 by up to 17.4 points, and (3) for process-level evaluation, localising reasoning failures with up to 86.1% accuracy. Overall, R-AIRL bridges imitation learning and reward-based optimisation, enabling the extraction of meaningful reasoning signals from expert thinking traces.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of teaching large language models to reason when explicit reward functions are difficult to define, as supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on expert demonstrations suffers from off-policy learning issues. The authors propose Reasoning Adversarial Inverse Reinforcement Learning (R-AIRL), which infers process-level rewards from expert Chain-of-Thoughts instead of directly imitating reasoning traces. Experiments on GSM8K, MMLU-Pro, and MedReason show that the learned reward function outperforms SFT in most settings, improves pass@1 by up to 17.4 points through inference-time reranking, and localizes reasoning failures with up to 86.1% accuracy.
该论文针对在难以定义明确奖励函数时教授大语言模型推理的挑战，指出监督微调（SFT）直接模仿专家推理轨迹存在离策略学习问题。作者提出推理对抗逆强化学习（R-AIRL），通过从专家思维链中推断过程级奖励而非直接模仿推理过程。在GSM8K、MMLU-Pro和MedReason上的实验表明，学习到的奖励函数在多数设置下优于SFT，通过推理时重排序将pass@1提升最多17.4个百分点，并以最高86.1%的准确率定位推理错误。
MARVL: Multi-Stage Guidance for Robotic Manipulation via Vision-Language Models
Authors: Xunlan Zhou, Xuanlin Chen, Shaowei Zhang, ShengHua Wan, Xiaohai Hu, Lei Yuan, De-chuan Zhan
First: 2026-01-28T11:25:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T13:06:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing dense reward functions is pivotal for efficient robotic Reinforcement Learning (RL). However, most dense rewards rely on manual engineering, which fundamentally limits the scalability and automation of reinforcement learning. While Vision-Language Models (VLMs) offer a promising path to reward design, naive VLM rewards often misalign with task progress, struggle with spatial grounding, and show limited understanding of task semantics. To address these issues, we propose MARVL-Multi-stAge guidance for Robotic manipulation via Vision-Language models. MARVL fine-tunes a VLM for spatial and semantic consistency and decomposes tasks into multi-stage subtasks with task direction projection for trajectory sensitivity. Empirically, MARVL significantly outperforms existing VLM-reward methods on the Meta-World benchmark, demonstrating superior sample efficiency and robustness on sparse-reward manipulation tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MARVL：基于视觉语言模型的机器人操作多阶段引导
设计密集奖励函数对于高效的机器人强化学习至关重要。然而，大多数密集奖励依赖于人工设计，这从根本上限制了强化学习的可扩展性和自动化。虽然视觉语言模型为奖励设计提供了有前景的路径，但简单的VLM奖励往往与任务进展不一致，在空间定位上存在困难，并且对任务语义的理解有限。为解决这些问题，我们提出了MARVL——基于视觉语言模型的机器人操作多阶段引导。MARVL对VLM进行微调以实现空间和语义一致性，并将任务分解为多阶段子任务，通过任务方向投影实现轨迹敏感性。实验表明，在Meta-World基准测试中，MARVL显著优于现有的VLM奖励方法，在稀疏奖励操作任务中展现出卓越的样本效率和鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of designing dense reward functions for robotic reinforcement learning, which are typically manually engineered and thus limit scalability. The authors propose MARVL, a method that fine-tunes a Vision-Language Model (VLM) to achieve spatial and semantic consistency, and decomposes tasks into multi-stage subtasks with task direction projection for trajectory sensitivity. Experimental results on the Meta-World benchmark show that MARVL significantly outperforms existing VLM-reward methods, demonstrating superior sample efficiency and robustness in sparse-reward manipulation tasks.
该论文针对机器人强化学习中密集奖励函数设计依赖人工工程、限制可扩展性的问题，提出了MARVL方法。该方法通过微调视觉语言模型（VLM）实现空间与语义一致性，并将任务分解为多阶段子任务，结合任务方向投影增强轨迹敏感性。在Meta-World基准上的实验表明，MARVL显著优于现有基于VLM的奖励方法，在稀疏奖励操作任务中展现出更优的样本效率和鲁棒性。
OPSD Compresses What RLVR Teaches: A Post-RL Compaction Stage for Reasoning Models
Authors: Jaehoon Kim, Dongha Lee
First: 2026-05-07T13:04:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T13:04:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
On-Policy Self-Distillation (OPSD) has recently emerged as an alternative to Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), promising higher accuracy and shorter responses through token-level credit assignment from a self-teacher conditioned on privileged context. However, this promise does not carry over to thinking-enabled mathematical reasoning, where reported accuracy gains shrink and sometimes turn negative. We hypothesize that hindsight supervision can specify better token-level alternatives in short thinking-disabled outputs, but in long thinking-enabled traces it more readily identifies redundancy than supplies better replacements. To test this, we applied OPSD separately to correct and incorrect rollout groups, so that compression and correction can be observed in isolation. Our results show that in thinking-enabled mathematical reasoning, OPSD behaves most reliably as a compression mechanism rather than a correction mechanism: training only on correct rollouts preserves accuracy while substantially shortening responses, whereas training only on incorrect rollouts damages accuracy. In light of these findings, we propose a revised post-training pipeline for thinking-enabled mathematical reasoning: SFT then RLVR then OPSD.
中文标题/摘要
标题：OPSD压缩RLVR所教内容：推理模型的后强化学习压缩阶段
在线策略自蒸馏（OPSD）近期作为可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的替代方案出现，通过基于特权上下文的自我教师进行令牌级信用分配，承诺更高的准确性和更短的响应。然而，这一承诺在涉及思考的数学推理中并未实现，报告中的准确率提升缩小甚至有时转为负值。我们假设，事后监督能在短的无思考输出中指定更好的令牌级替代方案，但在长的有思考轨迹中，它更容易识别冗余而非提供更好的替代。为验证这一点，我们将OPSD分别应用于正确和错误的rollout组，以便单独观察压缩和修正效果。结果表明，在涉及思考的数学推理中，OPSD最可靠地表现为压缩机制而非修正机制：仅在正确rollout上训练可保持准确率同时大幅缩短响应，而仅在错误rollout上训练则会损害准确率。基于这些发现，我们为涉及思考的数学推理提出修订后的后训练流程：SFT然后RLVR然后OPSD。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates why On-Policy Self-Distillation (OPSD) fails to improve accuracy in thinking-enabled mathematical reasoning, despite its success in other tasks. The authors hypothesize that OPSD primarily compresses redundant token-level information in long reasoning traces rather than correcting errors. By applying OPSD separately to correct and incorrect rollout groups, they find that training on correct rollouts preserves accuracy while shortening responses, whereas training on incorrect rollouts harms accuracy. Based on these results, they propose a revised pipeline: Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT), followed by Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), and finally OPSD as a compaction stage.
该论文探讨了在启用思考的数学推理任务中，在线策略自蒸馏（OPSD）为何无法提升准确率，尽管它在其他任务中表现成功。作者假设OPSD主要压缩长推理轨迹中的冗余信息，而非纠正错误。通过分别对正确和错误的推理轨迹应用OPSD，他们发现仅在正确轨迹上训练能保持准确率并缩短回答长度，而仅在错误轨迹上训练则会损害准确率。基于此，他们提出改进的训练流程：先进行监督微调（SFT），再使用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），最后用OPSD进行压缩。
In-Context Black-Box Optimization with Unreliable Feedback
Authors: Nicolas Samuel Blumer, Julien Martinelli, Samuel Kaski
First: 2026-05-07T13:03:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T13:03:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Black-box optimization in science and engineering often comes with side information: experts, simulators, pretrained predictors, or heuristics can suggest which candidates look promising. This information can accelerate search, but it can also be biased, input-dependent, or misleading. Feedback-aware BO methods typically handle one task at a time, limiting their ability to generalize over multiple sources of feedback. In-context optimizers address cross-task adaptation, but usually assume that optimization history is the only available signal at test time. We study feedback-informed in-context black-box optimization (FICBO), where a pretrained optimizer conditions on both the observed history and cheap auxiliary feedback for the current candidate set. We introduce a structured feedback prior that models how feedback sources vary in their access, relevance, and distortion relative to the true objective, and use it to pretrain a feedback-aware transformer. At test time, the model estimates source reliability in context by comparing observed objective values with auxiliary signals, improving query selection. On synthetic and real-world tasks, FICBO effectively exploits informative feedback while remaining robust to weak or misleading sources, improving over other baselines. Empirical investigations further illustrate how the model perceives test-time sources, offering insights into its interpretability and decision-making process.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of black-box optimization where unreliable auxiliary feedback, such as expert opinions or simulator outputs, is available alongside the true objective. The authors propose FICBO, a method that pretrains a transformer-based in-context optimizer using a structured feedback prior that models variations in source access, relevance, and distortion. At test time, the model dynamically estimates source reliability by comparing observed objective values with auxiliary signals, improving query selection. Experiments on synthetic and real-world tasks show that FICBO effectively exploits informative feedback while remaining robust to weak or misleading sources, outperforming baseline methods and offering interpretability into its decision-making.
该论文针对黑箱优化中常伴随不可靠辅助反馈（如专家意见、模拟器输出或启发式信息）的问题展开研究。作者提出FICBO方法，通过结构化反馈先验对基于Transformer的上下文优化器进行预训练，该先验建模了反馈源在访问方式、相关性和失真程度上的差异。在测试阶段，模型通过比较观测到的目标值与辅助信号动态估计反馈源的可靠性，从而改进查询选择。在合成和真实任务上的实验表明，FICBO能有效利用信息性反馈，同时对弱或误导性来源保持鲁棒性，性能优于其他基线方法，并提供了对模型决策过程的可解释性洞察。
PlatoLTL: Learning to Generalize Across Symbols in LTL Instructions for Multi-Task RL
Authors: Jacques Cloete, Mathias Jackermeier, Ioannis Havoutis, Alessandro Abate
First: 2026-01-30T12:11:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:55:00+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 4 figures (main paper). 22 pages, 11 figures (appendix)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A central challenge in multi-task reinforcement learning (RL) is to train generalist policies capable of performing tasks not seen during training. To facilitate such generalization, linear temporal logic (LTL) has emerged as a powerful formalism for specifying structured, temporally extended tasks to RL agents. While existing approaches to LTL-guided multi-task RL demonstrate generalization across LTL specifications, they are unable to generalize to unseen vocabularies of propositions (or "symbols"), which describe high-level events in LTL. We present PlatoLTL, a novel approach that enables policies to zero-shot generalize not only compositionally across LTL structures, but also parametrically across propositions. We model propositions as parameterized instances of atomic predicates, allowing policies to learn shared structure across related propositions. We propose a novel architecture that embeds and composes parameterized propositions to represent LTL formulae, and demonstrate zero-shot generalization in a range of challenging environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PlatoLTL：在多任务强化学习的LTL指令中学习跨符号泛化
多任务强化学习（RL）的一个核心挑战是训练能够执行训练中未见任务的通用策略。为促进此类泛化，线性时序逻辑（LTL）已成为向RL代理指定结构化、时间扩展任务的有力形式化方法。尽管现有的LTL引导多任务RL方法展示了跨LTL规范的泛化能力，但它们无法泛化到未见过的命题（或“符号”）词汇表，这些符号描述了LTL中的高层事件。我们提出PlatoLTL，一种新颖方法，使策略不仅能跨LTL结构进行组合式零样本泛化，还能跨命题进行参数式零样本泛化。我们将命题建模为原子谓词的参数化实例，使策略能够学习相关命题间的共享结构。我们提出一种新颖架构，嵌入并组合参数化命题以表示LTL公式，并在一系列具有挑战性的环境中展示了零样本泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of training multi-task reinforcement learning policies that can generalize to unseen tasks specified by linear temporal logic (LTL) instructions, particularly when those instructions involve new proposition symbols not encountered during training. The proposed method, PlatoLTL, models propositions as parameterized instances of atomic predicates, enabling the policy to learn shared structure across related symbols and thus generalize parametrically. A novel architecture embeds and composes these parameterized propositions to represent LTL formulae. Experimental results across several challenging environments demonstrate that PlatoLTL achieves zero-shot generalization to both novel LTL structures and unseen proposition vocabularies.
该论文针对多任务强化学习中策略难以泛化到未见任务的问题，特别是当线性时序逻辑指令包含训练时未见过的新命题符号时。提出的PlatoLTL方法将命题建模为原子谓词的参数化实例，使策略能够学习相关符号间的共享结构，从而实现参数化泛化。该方法采用新颖的架构嵌入并组合这些参数化命题以表示LTL公式。在多个具有挑战性的环境中的实验结果表明，PlatoLTL能够零样本泛化到未见过的LTL结构和命题词汇。
Entropy-Regularized Adjoint Matching for Offline RL
Authors: Abdelghani Ghanem, Mounir Ghogho
First: 2026-05-07T12:47:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:47:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Integrating expressive generative policies, such as flow-matching models, into offline reinforcement learning (RL) allows agents to capture complex, multi-modal behaviors. While Q-learning with Adjoint Matching (QAM) stabilizes policy optimization via the continuous adjoint method, it remains inherently bound to the fixed behavior distribution. This dependence induces a \textit{popularity bias} that can suppress high-reward actions in low-density regions, and creates a \textit{support binding} that restricts off-manifold exploration. Existing workarounds, such as appending \textit{residual} Gaussian policies, often re-introduce the expressivity bottlenecks associated with unimodal distributions. In this work, we propose \textit{Maximum Entropy Adjoint Matching} (ME-AM), a unified framework that addresses these limitations within the continuous flow formulation. ME-AM incorporates two mechanisms: (1) a Mirror Descent entropy maximization objective that mitigates the popularity bias to facilitate the extraction of optimal policies from offline datasets, and (2) a \textit{Mixture Behavior Prior} that mathematically broadens the geometric support to encompass out-of-distribution high-reward regions. By exploring this extended geometry, ME-AM identifies robust actions while preserving the absolute continuity of the generative vector field. Empirically, ME-AM demonstrates competitive or superior performance compared to prior state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods across a diverse suite of sparse-reward continuous control environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：熵正则化伴随匹配用于离线强化学习
将表达性生成策略（如流匹配模型）集成到离线强化学习中，使智能体能够捕捉复杂、多模态的行为。虽然基于伴随匹配的Q学习通过连续伴随方法稳定了策略优化，但它本质上仍受限于固定的行为分布。这种依赖会引发“流行度偏差”，抑制低密度区域中的高奖励动作，并产生“支持绑定”，限制流形外的探索。现有的变通方法，如附加残差高斯策略，往往重新引入与单峰分布相关的表达性瓶颈。在本工作中，我们提出最大熵伴随匹配，一个在连续流框架内解决这些限制的统一框架。ME-AM包含两种机制：(1) 镜像下降熵最大化目标，缓解流行度偏差以促进从离线数据集中提取最优策略；(2) 混合行为先验，从数学上拓宽几何支持以涵盖分布外的高奖励区域。通过探索这种扩展的几何结构，ME-AM在保持生成向量场绝对连续性的同时识别鲁棒动作。实验表明，在多种稀疏奖励连续控制环境中，ME-AM相比先前最先进方法展现出具有竞争力或更优的性能。

The paper addresses limitations in offline reinforcement learning where expressive generative policies like flow-matching models suffer from popularity bias and support binding due to dependence on fixed behavior distributions. The authors propose Maximum Entropy Adjoint Matching (ME-AM), a unified framework that incorporates Mirror Descent entropy maximization to mitigate popularity bias and a Mixture Behavior Prior to broaden geometric support for out-of-distribution high-reward regions. Empirical results show that ME-AM achieves competitive or superior performance compared to prior state-of-the-art methods across diverse sparse-reward continuous control environments.

AdaGamma: State-Dependent Discounting for Temporal Adaptation in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yaomin Wang, Jianting Pan, Ran Tian, Xiaoyang Li, Yu Zhang, Hengle Qin, Tianshu YU
First: 2026-05-07T12:42:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:42:46+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 9 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The discount factor in reinforcement learning controls both the effective planning horizon and the strength of bootstrapping, yet most deep RL methods use a single fixed value across all states. While state-dependent discounting is conceptually appealing, naive deep actor--critic implementations can become unstable and degenerate toward TD-error collapse. We propose AdaGamma, a practical deep actor--critic method for state-dependent discounting that learns a state-dependent discount function together with a return-consistency objective to regularize the induced backup structure. On the theory side, we analyze the Bellman operator induced by state-dependent discounting and establish its basic well-posedness properties under suitable conditions. Empirically, AdaGamma integrates into both SAC and PPO, yielding consistent improvements on continuous-control benchmarks, and achieves statistically significant gains in an online A/B test on the JD Logistics platform. These results suggest that state-dependent discounting can be made effective in deep RL when coupled with a return-consistency objective that prevents degenerate target manipulation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AdaGamma：强化学习中用于时间自适应的状态依赖折扣因子
强化学习中的折扣因子同时控制有效规划视野和自举强度，但大多数深度强化学习方法在所有状态下使用单一固定值。尽管状态依赖折扣在概念上具有吸引力，但朴素的深度演员-评论家实现可能变得不稳定并退化为TD误差崩溃。我们提出AdaGamma，一种实用的深度演员-评论家状态依赖折扣方法，该方法学习状态依赖折扣函数，并结合回报一致性目标来正则化诱导的备份结构。在理论方面，我们分析了状态依赖折扣诱导的贝尔曼算子，并在适当条件下建立了其基本适定性性质。在实证方面，AdaGamma可集成到SAC和PPO中，在连续控制基准上取得一致改进，并在京东物流平台的在线A/B测试中获得统计显著提升。这些结果表明，当结合防止退化目标操纵的回报一致性目标时，状态依赖折扣可在深度强化学习中有效实现。

Unifying Goal-Conditioned RL and Unsupervised Skill Learning via Control-Maximization
Authors: Alireza Modirshanechi, Benjamin Eysenbach, Peter Dayan, Eric Schulz
First: 2026-05-07T12:40:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:40:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unsupervised pretraining has driven empirical advances in goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL), but its theoretical foundations remain poorly understood. In particular, an influential class of methods, mutual information skill learning (MISL), discovers behaviorally diverse skills that can later be used for downstream goal-reaching. However, it remains a theoretical mystery why skills learned through MISL should support goal-reaching. A subtle challenge is that both GCRL and MISL are umbrella terms: different GCRL tasks use distinct criteria for measuring goal-reaching performance, while different MISL methods optimize distinct notions of behavioral diversity. We address this challenge and unify GCRL and MISL as instances of control maximization. We identify three canonical GCRL formulations and prove that they are fundamentally inequivalent: they can induce incompatible optimal policies even in the same environment. Nevertheless, they all share a common interpretation: a well-performing goal-conditioned policy is one whose future trajectory is highly sensitive to the commanded goal, with the precise notion of sensitivity determined by the GCRL formulation. Noting that MISL objectives can be understood as measures of skill-sensitivity akin to goal-sensitivity, we show that MISL objectives are bounded by formulation-specific downstream goal-sensitivities. These bounds establish a precise correspondence between MISL methods and downstream GCRL tasks: for every GCRL formulation, there exists a matching MISL objective for which more diverse skills afford greater downstream goal sensitivity. Our results thus lay a theoretical foundation for RL pretraining and have important practical implications, such as suggesting which pretraining objectives to use when a user cares about a specific class of downstream tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过控制最大化统一目标条件强化学习与无监督技能学习
无监督预训练推动了目标条件强化学习（GCRL）的实证进展，但其理论基础仍不清晰。特别地，一类有影响力的方法——互信息技能学习（MISL）——能发现行为多样化的技能，这些技能后续可用于下游目标达成。然而，为何通过MISL学习的技能应支持目标达成，在理论上仍是一个谜。一个微妙的挑战在于，GCRL和MISL都是总称性术语：不同的GCRL任务使用不同标准衡量目标达成性能，而不同的MISL方法优化不同的行为多样性概念。我们应对这一挑战，将GCRL和MISL统一为控制最大化的实例。我们识别出三种典型的GCRL公式，并证明它们本质上不等价：即使在相同环境中，它们也可能诱导出不相容的最优策略。尽管如此，它们共享一个共同解释：一个性能良好的目标条件策略，其未来轨迹对命令目标高度敏感，而敏感性的精确概念由GCRL公式决定。注意到MISL目标可理解为类似于目标敏感性的技能敏感性度量，我们证明MISL目标受限于公式特定的下游目标敏感性。这些界限建立了MISL方法与下游GCRL任务之间的精确对应关系：对于每个GCRL公式，存在一个匹配的MISL目标，其中更多样化的技能提供更大的下游目标敏感性。因此，我们的结果为强化学习预训练奠定了理论基础，并具有重要的实践意义，例如建议当用户关心特定类别的下游任务时应使用哪些预训练目标。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the theoretical gap between goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL) and unsupervised skill learning via mutual information skill learning (MISL), proposing a unified framework called control maximization. The authors identify three canonical GCRL formulations and prove they are fundamentally inequivalent, yet all share the interpretation that a good goal-conditioned policy maximizes sensitivity of future trajectories to the commanded goal. They further show that MISL objectives measure skill-sensitivity analogous to goal-sensitivity, and derive bounds establishing precise correspondences between MISL methods and downstream GCRL tasks. The main experimental insight is that for each GCRL formulation, a matching MISL objective exists where more diverse skills yield greater downstream goal sensitivity, providing theoretical foundations for RL pretraining and practical guidance on selecting pretraining objectives for specific task classes.

Listwise Policy Optimization: Group-based RLVR as Target-Projection on the LLM Response Simplex
Authors: Yun Qu, Qi Wang, Yixiu Mao, Heming Zou, Yuhang Jiang, Yingyue Li, Wutong Xu, Lizhou Cai, Weijie Liu, Clive Bai, Kai Yang, Yangkun Chen, Saiyong Yang, Xiangyang Ji
First: 2026-05-07T12:38:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:38:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become a standard approach for large language models (LLMs) post-training to incentivize reasoning capacity. Among existing recipes, group-based policy gradient is prevalent, which samples a group of responses per prompt and updates the policy via group-relative advantage signals. This work reveals that these optimization strategies share a common geometric structure: each implicitly defines a target distribution on the response simplex and projects toward it via first-order approximation. Building on this insight, we propose Listwise Policy Optimization (LPO) to explicitly conduct the target-projection, which demystifies the implicit target by restricting the proximal RL objective to the response simplex, and then projects the policy via exact divergence minimization. This framework provides (i) monotonic improvement on the listwise objective with bounded, zero-sum, and self-correcting projection gradients, and (ii) flexibility in divergence selection with distinct structural properties through the decoupled projection step. On diverse reasoning tasks and LLM backbones, LPO consistently improves training performance over typical policy gradient baselines under matched targets, while intrinsically preserving optimization stability and response diversity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：列表式策略优化：基于组的RLVR作为LLM响应单纯形上的目标投影
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为大型语言模型（LLM）后训练中激励推理能力的标准方法。在现有方案中，基于组的策略梯度较为普遍，该方法为每个提示采样一组响应，并通过组相对优势信号更新策略。本工作揭示这些优化策略共享共同的几何结构：每个策略隐式地在响应单纯形上定义目标分布，并通过一阶近似向其投影。基于此洞察，我们提出列表式策略优化（LPO）以显式执行目标投影，通过将近端RL目标限制在响应单纯形上来阐明隐式目标，然后通过精确散度最小化投影策略。该框架提供：(i) 在列表式目标上的单调改进，具有有界、零和且自校正的投影梯度；(ii) 通过解耦投影步骤，在散度选择上具有灵活性，并具有独特的结构特性。在多样化的推理任务和LLM骨干网络上，LPO在匹配目标下持续优于典型策略梯度基线的训练性能，同时内在保持优化稳定性和响应多样性。
Skill1: Unified Evolution of Skill-Augmented Agents via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yaorui Shi, Yuxin Chen, Zhengxi Lu, Yuchun Miao, Shugui Liu, Qi GU, Xunliang Cai, Xiang Wang, An Zhang
First: 2026-05-07T12:33:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:33:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A persistent skill library allows language model agents to reuse successful strategies across tasks. Maintaining such a library requires three coupled capabilities. The agent selects a relevant skill, utilizes it during execution, and distills new skills from experience. Existing methods optimize these capabilities in isolation or with separate reward sources, resulting in partial and conflicting evolution. We propose Skill1, a framework that trains a single policy to co-evolve skill selection, utilization, and distillation toward a shared task-outcome objective. The policy generates a query to search the skill library, re-ranks candidates to select one, solves the task conditioned on it, and distills a new skill from the trajectory. All learning derives from a single task-outcome signal. Its low-frequency trend credits selection and its high-frequency variation credits distillation. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop show that Skill1 outperforms prior skill-based and reinforcement learning baselines. Training dynamics confirm the co-evolution of the three capabilities, and ablations show that removing any credit signal degrades the evolution.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Skill1, a framework for language model agents that addresses the challenge of maintaining a persistent skill library by co-evolving three coupled capabilities: skill selection, utilization, and distillation. The motivation is that existing methods optimize these capabilities in isolation, leading to partial and conflicting evolution. Skill1 trains a single policy using a unified task-outcome reinforcement learning signal, where the policy generates a query to search the library, re-ranks candidates, solves the task, and distills a new skill from the trajectory. The low-frequency trend of the reward signal credits selection, while high-frequency variation credits distillation. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop demonstrate that Skill1 outperforms prior skill-based and reinforcement learning baselines, with training dynamics confirming co-evolution and ablations showing that removing any credit signal degrades performance.
该论文提出了Skill1框架，旨在通过强化学习协同进化语言模型代理的三个耦合能力：技能选择、使用和提炼，以维护持久的技能库。动机在于现有方法孤立优化这些能力，导致部分且冲突的进化。Skill1训练单一策略，使用统一的任务结果强化学习信号，该策略生成查询搜索技能库、重新排序候选技能、基于技能完成任务，并从轨迹中提炼新技能。奖励信号的低频趋势用于选择能力，高频变化用于提炼能力。在ALFWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，Skill1优于先前的基于技能和强化学习的基线方法，训练动态证实了三种能力的协同进化，消融实验显示移除任何信用信号都会降低进化效果。
Policy-Guided Stepwise Model Routing for Cost-Effective Reasoning
Authors: Wenwen Si, Insup Lee, Osbert Bastani
First: 2026-05-07T12:26:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:26:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Inference-time computation has greatly enhanced the performance of large language models (LLMs) on challenging reasoning tasks, but this strategy can incur high inference costs. One solution is to route intermediate chain-of-thought (CoT) states to language models of different sizes; however, existing approaches rely on handcrafted routing strategies that limit performance, or on training large process reward models that may be infeasible in many applications. We formulate stepwise model routing as a constrained decision-making problem, which we solve by training a small control policy using reinforcement learning in conjunction with threshold calibration to tune the performance-efficiency tradeoff. We validate our method on three math benchmarks (GSM8K, MATH500, and OmniMath) on both open and closed models. Our method consistently improves the accuracy-cost tradeoff compared to handcrafted approaches, while achieving a comparable tradeoff to methods that require training large process reward models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：策略引导的逐步模型路由实现经济高效推理
推理时计算显著提升了大型语言模型在复杂推理任务上的表现，但此策略可能导致高昂的推理成本。一种解决方案是将中间思维链状态路由至不同规模的语言模型；然而，现有方法依赖手工设计的路由策略而限制性能，或需训练大型过程奖励模型，这在许多应用中可能不可行。我们将逐步模型路由形式化为约束决策问题，通过结合阈值校准的强化学习训练小型控制策略，以调节性能-效率权衡。我们在三个数学基准（GSM8K、MATH500和OmniMath）上对开源和闭源模型进行了验证。与手工方法相比，我们的方法持续改善了准确率-成本权衡，同时达到了与需训练大型过程奖励模型的方法相当的性能权衡。

Schedule-and-Calibrate: Utility-Guided Multi-Task Reinforcement Learning for Code LLMs
Authors: Yujia Chen, Yang Ye, Xiao Chu, Yuchi Ma, Cuiyun Gao
First: 2026-05-07T12:24:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:24:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) with verifiable rewards has proven effective at post-training LLMs for coding, yet deploying separate task-specific specialists incurs costs that scale with the number of tasks, motivating a unified multi-task RL (MTRL) approach. However, existing MTRL methods treat all coding tasks uniformly, relying on fixed data curricula under a shared optimization strategy, ultimately limiting the effectiveness of multi-task training. To address these limitations, we propose ASTOR, a multi-tASk code reinforcement learning framework via uTility-driven coORdination. Centered on task utility, a signal capturing each task learning potential and cross-task synergy, ASTOR comprises two coupled modules: 1) Hierarchical Utility-Routed Data Scheduling module hierarchically allocates training budget and prioritizes informative prompts, steering training toward the most valuable data and 2) Adaptive Utility-Calibrated Policy Optimization module dynamically scales per-task KL regularization, matching update constraints to each tasks current training state. Experiments on two widely-used LLMs across four representative coding tasks demonstrate that ASTOR consistently improves a single model across all tasks, outperforming the best task-specific specialist by 9.0%-9.5% and surpassing the strongest MTRL baseline by 7.5%-12.8%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：调度与校准：面向代码大语言模型的效用引导多任务强化学习
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已被证明在代码大语言模型的后训练中有效，但部署独立的任务专用专家模型会导致成本随任务数量线性增长，这促使了统一的多任务强化学习方法。然而，现有方法将所有编码任务一视同仁，依赖固定数据课程和共享优化策略，最终限制了多任务训练的效果。为解决这些局限，我们提出ASTOR——一种通过效用驱动协调的多任务代码强化学习框架。该框架以任务效用（捕捉各任务学习潜力与跨任务协同的信号）为核心，包含两个耦合模块：1）分层效用路由数据调度模块，分层分配训练预算并优先选择信息量大的提示，引导训练聚焦于最有价值的数据；2）自适应效用校准策略优化模块，动态调整每任务的KL正则化强度，使更新约束匹配各任务的当前训练状态。在两个广泛使用的大语言模型及四个代表性编码任务上的实验表明，ASTOR能持续提升单一模型在所有任务上的表现，比最佳任务专用专家模型高出9.0%-9.5%，并超越最强多任务强化学习基线7.5%-12.8%。
Summary / 总结
To address the high cost of deploying separate task-specific specialists for coding, this paper proposes ASTOR, a multi-task reinforcement learning framework that unifies training across multiple coding tasks. The method introduces a utility-driven coordination mechanism with two modules: a hierarchical data scheduling module that allocates training budgets and prioritizes informative prompts based on task utility, and an adaptive policy optimization module that dynamically scales per-task KL regularization. Experiments on two LLMs across four coding tasks show that ASTOR improves a single model on all tasks, outperforming the best task-specific specialist by 9.0%-9.5% and the strongest multi-task baseline by 7.5%-12.8%.
针对部署多个任务专用模型成本高昂的问题，本文提出ASTOR，一个统一的多任务强化学习框架，用于代码大语言模型的后训练。该方法基于任务效用驱动协调，包含两个模块：层次化数据调度模块根据任务效用分配训练预算并优先选择信息量大的提示，以及自适应策略优化模块动态调整每个任务的KL正则化强度。在两个大语言模型和四个代表性编码任务上的实验表明，ASTOR使单一模型在所有任务上均取得提升，比最佳任务专用模型高出9.0%-9.5%，比最强多任务基线高出7.5%-12.8%。
Beyond Autoregressive RTG: Conditioning via Injection Outside Sequential Modeling in Decision Transformer
Authors: Yongyi Wang, Hanyu Liu, Lingfeng Li, Bozhou Chen, Ang Li, Qirui Zheng, Xionghui Yang, Chucai Wang, Wenxin Li
First: 2026-05-07T12:20:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:20:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decision Transformer (DT) formulates offline reinforcement learning as autoregressive sequence modeling, achieving promising results by predicting actions from a sequence of Return-to-Go (RTG), state, and action tokens. However, RTG is a scalar that summarizes future rewards, containing far less information than typical state or action vectors, yet it consumes the same computational budget per token. Worse, the self-attention cost of Transformers grows quadratically with sequence length, so including RTG as a separate token adds unnecessary overhead. We propose SlimDT, which removes RTG from the autoregressive sequence. Instead, we inject RTG information into the state representations before the sequential modeling step, allowing the Transformer to process only a compact (state, action) sequence. This reduces the sequence length by one-third, directly improving inference efficiency. On the D4RL benchmark, SlimDT surpasses standard DT across various tasks and achieves performance comparable to existing state-of-the-art methods. Decoupling a sparse conditioning signal from an information-rich sequence thus yields both computational gains and higher task performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越自回归RTG：决策Transformer中通过序列建模外注入的条件控制
决策Transformer（DT）将离线强化学习建模为自回归序列预测，通过从回报-状态-动作令牌序列中预测动作取得了显著成果。然而，RTG作为标量仅汇总未来奖励，信息量远少于状态或动作向量，却消耗相同的令牌计算预算。更严重的是，Transformer的自注意力成本随序列长度呈二次增长，将RTG作为独立令牌会带来不必要的开销。我们提出SlimDT，将RTG从自回归序列中移除，转而将RTG信息注入状态表示后再进行序列建模，使Transformer仅处理紧凑的（状态，动作）序列。这使序列长度缩短三分之一，直接提升推理效率。在D4RL基准测试中，SlimDT在各类任务上超越标准DT，性能与现有最优方法相当。将稀疏条件信号与信息密集型序列解耦，既能获得计算收益，又能提升任务性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes SlimDT, a modification to the Decision Transformer (DT) for offline reinforcement learning, motivated by the inefficiency of including Return-to-Go (RTG) as a separate token in the autoregressive sequence, which increases computational cost due to quadratic self-attention. The method removes RTG from the sequence and instead injects its information into state representations before sequential modeling, reducing sequence length by one-third. Experimental results on the D4RL benchmark show that SlimDT surpasses standard DT across various tasks and achieves performance comparable to state-of-the-art methods, demonstrating both computational gains and improved task performance.
该论文提出SlimDT，旨在改进决策Transformer（DT）在离线强化学习中的效率，其动机在于将Return-to-Go（RTG）作为独立令牌纳入自回归序列会导致计算成本因自注意力的二次增长而增加。该方法将RTG从序列中移除，并在序列建模前将其信息注入状态表示，从而将序列长度减少三分之一。在D4RL基准上的实验结果表明，SlimDT在多种任务上超越了标准DT，并达到了与现有最先进方法相当的性能，展现了计算效率提升和任务性能改进的双重优势。
VISD: Enhancing Video Reasoning via Structured Self-Distillation
Authors: Hao Lin, Kunyang Lv, Xu Jiang, Jingqi Tian, Zhongjing Du, Jiayu Ding, Qiaoman Zhang, Hongbo Jin
First: 2026-05-07T12:13:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:13:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training VideoLLMs for complex reasoning remains challenging due to sparse sequence level rewards and the lack of fine grained credit assignment over long, temporally grounded reasoning trajectories. While reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) provides reliable supervision, it fails to capture token level contributions, leading to inefficient learning. Conversely, existing self distillation methods offer dense supervision but lack structure and diagnostic specificity, and often interact unstably with reinforcement learning. In this work, we propose VISD, a structured self distillation framework that introduces diagnostically meaningful privileged information for video reasoning. VISD employs a video aware judge model to decompose reasoning quality into multiple dimensions, including answer correctness, logical consistency, and spatio-temporal grounding, and uses this structured feedback to guide a teacher policy for token level supervision. To stably integrate dense supervision with RL, we introduce a direction magnitude decoupling mechanism, where rollout level advantages computed from rewards determine update direction, while structured privileged signals modulate token level update magnitudes. This design enables semantically aligned and fine grained credit assignment, improving both reasoning faithfulness and training efficiency. Additionally, VISD incorporates curriculum scheduling and EMA based teacher stabilization to support robust optimization over long video sequences. Experiments on diverse benchmarks show that VISD consistently outperforms strong baselines, improving answer accuracy and spatio temporal grounding quality. Notably, VISD reaches these gains with nearly 2x faster convergence in optimization steps, highlighting the effectiveness of structured self supervision in improving both performance and sample efficiency for VideoLLMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VISD：通过结构化自蒸馏增强视频推理
训练视频大语言模型进行复杂推理仍具挑战性，原因在于稀疏的序列级奖励以及缺乏对长时间、时间上可推理轨迹的细粒度信用分配。虽然基于可验证奖励的强化学习提供了可靠的监督，但它无法捕捉词元级贡献，导致学习效率低下。相反，现有的自蒸馏方法提供了密集监督，但缺乏结构和诊断特异性，并且常常与强化学习交互不稳定。在这项工作中，我们提出了VISD，一种结构化自蒸馏框架，为视频推理引入具有诊断意义的特权信息。VISD采用视频感知评判模型将推理质量分解为多个维度，包括答案正确性、逻辑一致性和时空基础，并利用这种结构化反馈指导教师策略进行词元级监督。为了将密集监督与强化学习稳定集成，我们引入了方向-幅度解耦机制，其中由奖励计算的轨迹级优势决定更新方向，而结构化特权信号则调节词元级更新幅度。这种设计实现了语义对齐和细粒度的信用分配，提高了推理忠实度和训练效率。此外，VISD结合了课程调度和基于指数移动平均的教师稳定化，以支持长视频序列的鲁棒优化。在多个基准上的实验表明，VISD始终优于强基线，提高了答案准确性和时空基础质量。值得注意的是，VISD在优化步骤上实现了近2倍的收敛速度提升，突显了结构化自监督在提高视频大语言模型性能和样本效率方面的有效性。

The paper proposes VISD, a structured self-distillation framework to address the challenge of training VideoLLMs for complex reasoning, where reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards provides sparse supervision and existing self-distillation methods lack structure. VISD introduces a video-aware judge model that decomposes reasoning quality into dimensions like answer correctness, logical consistency, and spatio-temporal grounding, using this structured feedback to guide a teacher policy for token-level supervision. To stably integrate dense supervision with RL, a direction-magnitude decoupling mechanism is employed, where rollout-level advantages determine update direction and structured privileged signals modulate token-level update magnitudes. Experiments on diverse benchmarks show VISD consistently outperforms strong baselines in answer accuracy and spatio-temporal grounding quality, achieving nearly 2x faster convergence in optimization steps.
该论文提出VISD，一种结构化自蒸馏框架，旨在解决训练视频大语言模型进行复杂推理时的挑战，其中基于可验证奖励的强化学习提供稀疏监督，而现有自蒸馏方法缺乏结构。VISD引入视频感知评判模型，将推理质量分解为答案正确性、逻辑一致性和时空定位等多个维度，并利用这种结构化反馈指导教师策略进行令牌级监督。为了稳定地将密集监督与强化学习结合，采用方向-幅度解耦机制，其中基于奖励的轨迹级优势决定更新方向，而结构化特权信号调节令牌级更新幅度。在多种基准上的实验表明，VISD在答案准确性和时空定位质量上持续优于强基线，并在优化步骤中实现近2倍的收敛速度提升。
Milestone-Guided Policy Learning for Long-Horizon Language Agents
Authors: Zixuan Wang, Yuchen Yan, Hongxing Li, Teng Pan, Dingming Li, Ruiqing Zhang, Weiming Lu, Jun Xiao, Yueting Zhuang, Yongliang Shen
First: 2026-05-07T12:00:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:00:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While long-horizon agentic tasks require language agents to perform dozens of sequential decisions, training such agents with reinforcement learning remains challenging. We identify two root causes: credit misattribution, where correct early actions are penalized due to terminal failures, and sample inefficiency, where scarce successful trajectories result in near-total loss of learning signal. We introduce a milestone-guided policy learning framework, BEACON, that leverages the compositional structure of long-horizon tasks to ensure precise credit assignment. BEACON partitions trajectories at milestone boundaries, applies temporal reward shaping within segments to credit partial progress, and estimates advantages at dual scales to prevent distant failures from corrupting the evaluation of local actions. On ALFWorld, WebShop, and ScienceWorld, BEACON consistently outperforms GRPO and GiGPO. Notably, on long-horizon ALFWorld tasks, BEACON achieves 92.9% success rate, nearly doubling GRPO's 53.5%, while improving effective sample utilization from 23.7% to 82.0%. These results establish milestone-anchored credit assignment as an effective paradigm for training long-horizon language agents. Code is available at https://github.com/ZJU-REAL/BEACON.
中文标题/摘要
标题：里程碑引导的长周期语言智能体策略学习
尽管长周期智能体任务要求语言智能体执行数十个连续决策，但使用强化学习训练此类智能体仍具挑战性。我们识别出两个根本原因：信用错误归因（正确早期动作因终端失败而受罚）和样本效率低下（稀缺的成功轨迹导致学习信号近乎完全丢失）。我们提出里程碑引导的策略学习框架BEACON，利用长周期任务的组合结构实现精确信用分配。BEACON在里程碑边界划分轨迹，在片段内应用时间奖励塑形以奖励部分进展，并在双重尺度估计优势值，防止远端失败破坏局部动作评估。在ALFWorld、WebShop和ScienceWorld上，BEACON持续优于GRPO和GiGPO。值得注意的是，在长周期ALFWorld任务中，BEACON达到92.9%的成功率，几乎翻倍于GRPO的53.5%，同时将有效样本利用率从23.7%提升至82.0%。这些结果确立了里程碑锚定信用分配作为训练长周期语言智能体的有效范式。代码见https://github.com/ZJU-REAL/BEACON。
Summary / 总结
Training language agents for long-horizon tasks with reinforcement learning is challenging due to credit misattribution and sample inefficiency. Experiments on ALFWorld, WebShop, and ScienceWorld show BEACON consistently outperforms GRPO and GiGPO, achieving a 92.9% success rate on long-horizon ALFWorld tasks—nearly doubling GRPO's 53.5%—while improving effective sample utilization from 23.7% to 82.0%.
训练语言智能体完成长周期任务时，强化学习面临信用分配错误和样本效率低下的挑战。为此，作者提出里程碑引导的策略学习框架BEACON，通过将轨迹在里程碑边界处分割、在片段内进行时间奖励塑形以及双尺度优势估计，实现精确的信用分配。在ALFWorld、WebShop和ScienceWorld上的实验表明，BEACON持续优于GRPO和GiGPO，在长周期ALFWorld任务中达到92.9%的成功率，几乎是GRPO的53.5%的两倍，同时将有效样本利用率从23.7%提升至82.0%。
Causal Reinforcement Learning for Complex Card Games: A Magic The Gathering Benchmark
Authors: Cristiano da Costa Cunha, Ajmal Mian, Tim French, Wei Liu
First: 2026-05-07T11:53:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T11:53:56+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 8 figures, 9 tables, 1 algorithm
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Causal reinforcement learning (RL) lacks benchmarks for complex systems that combine sequential decision making, hidden information, large masked action spaces, and explicit causal structure. We introduce MTG-Causal-RL, a Gymnasium benchmark built on Magic: The Gathering with a 3,077-dimensional partial observation, a 478-action masked discrete action space, five competitive Standard archetypes, three reward schemes, and a hand-specified Structural Causal Model (SCM) over strategic variables. Every episode exposes causal variables, SCM-predicted intervention effects, and per-factor credit traces, making causal credit assignment, leave-one-out cross-archetype transfer, and policy auditability first-class metrics. We adapt a panel of reference baselines: random, heuristic, masked PPO, a causal-world-model PPO variant, and an architecture-matched scalar control. We propose Causal Graph-Factored Advantage PPO (CGFA-PPO) as a reference causal agent that uses SCM parents of win probability as factor-aligned critic targets with an intervention-calibration loss. All comparisons use paired seeds, paired-bootstrap confidence intervals, and Holm-Bonferroni correction within pre-registered families. Masked PPO and CGFA-PPO reach competitive in-distribution win rates and exceed the random baseline; per-factor calibration trajectories and leave-one-out transfer gaps expose diagnostic structure that scalar win rate alone cannot. We release the benchmark, reference-baseline results, and full evaluation protocol openly. By coupling a strategically rich, partially observed domain with an explicit causal interface and statistical protocol, MTG-Causal-RL gives causal-RL, world-model, and LLM-agent research a shared testbed for questions current benchmarks cannot pose together: causal credit assignment under masked action spaces, structural transfer across archetypes, and SCM-grounded policy auditability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向复杂卡牌游戏的因果强化学习：万智牌基准测试
因果强化学习（RL）缺乏针对结合序列决策、隐藏信息、大规模掩码动作空间和显式因果结构的复杂系统的基准测试。我们提出MTG-Causal-RL，一个基于万智牌构建的Gymnasium基准测试，包含3077维部分观测、478动作掩码离散动作空间、五种竞技标准赛制原型、三种奖励方案，以及一个针对战略变量手工指定的结构因果模型（SCM）。每个回合暴露因果变量、SCM预测的干预效应及每因子信用轨迹，使因果信用分配、留一法跨原型迁移和政策可审计性成为首要指标。我们适配一组参考基线：随机、启发式、掩码PPO、因果世界模型PPO变体及架构匹配的标量控制。提出因果图因子优势PPO（CGFA-PPO）作为参考因果智能体，使用胜率SCM父节点作为因子对齐的评论家目标，并引入干预校准损失。所有比较均使用配对种子、配对自助置信区间及预注册族内的Holm-Bonferroni校正。掩码PPO和CGFA-PPO达到竞争性分布内胜率并超过随机基线；每因子校准轨迹和留一法迁移差距揭示了标量胜率无法单独揭示的诊断结构。我们公开了基准测试、参考基线结果及完整评估协议。通过将战略丰富的部分观测领域与显式因果接口及统计协议相结合，MTG-Causal-RL为因果RL、世界模型和LLM智能体研究提供了一个共享测试平台，用于解决当前基准测试无法共同提出的问题：掩码动作空间下的因果信用分配、跨原型结构迁移及基于SCM的政策可审计性。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces MTG-Causal-RL, a Gymnasium benchmark for causal reinforcement learning built on the complex card game Magic: The Gathering, motivated by the lack of benchmarks that combine sequential decision making, hidden information, large masked action spaces, and explicit causal structure. The method includes a 3,077-dimensional partial observation space, a 478-action masked discrete action space, five competitive Standard archetypes, three reward schemes, and a hand-specified Structural Causal Model (SCM) over strategic variables, along with a proposed Causal Graph-Factored Advantage PPO (CGFA-PPO) agent that uses SCM parents of win probability as factor-aligned critic targets with an intervention-calibration loss. Main experimental results show that Masked PPO and CGFA-PPO achieve competitive in-distribution win rates exceeding the random baseline, while per-factor calibration trajectories and leave-one-out transfer gaps reveal diagnostic structure that scalar win rate alone cannot capture, demonstrating the benchmark's utility for causal credit assignment, cross-archetype transfer, and policy auditability.
该论文提出了MTG-Causal-RL，一个基于复杂卡牌游戏《万智牌》的Gymnasium基准测试，旨在解决因果强化学习缺乏同时包含序列决策、隐藏信息、大规模掩码动作空间和显式因果结构的基准测试问题。方法包括一个3077维的部分观测空间、478个动作的掩码离散动作空间、五种竞技标准套牌类型、三种奖励方案以及一个手动指定的战略变量结构因果模型（SCM），并提出了因果图因子优势PPO（CGFA-PPO）作为参考因果智能体，该智能体使用胜率概率的SCM父节点作为因子对齐的评论家目标，并带有干预校准损失。主要实验结果表明，掩码PPO和CGFA-PPO达到了超越随机基线的竞争性分布内胜率，而每个因子的校准轨迹和留一法跨套牌类型迁移差距揭示了标量胜率无法单独捕捉的诊断结构，证明了该基准在因果信用分配、跨套牌类型迁移和策略可审计性方面的实用性。
CORE: Concept-Oriented Reinforcement for Bridging the Definition-Application Gap in Mathematical Reasoning
Authors: Zijun Gao, Zhikun Xu, Xiao Ye, Ben Zhou
First: 2025-12-21T19:01:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T11:50:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) often solve challenging math exercises yet fail to apply the concept right when the problem requires genuine understanding. Popular Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) pipelines reinforce final answers but provide little fine-grained conceptual signal, so models improve at pattern reuse rather than conceptual applications. We introduce CORE (Concept-Oriented REinforcement), an RL training framework that turns explicit concepts into a controllable supervision signal. Starting from a high-quality, low-contamination textbook resource that links verifiable exercises to concise concept descriptions, we run a sanity probe showing LLMs can restate definitions but fail concept-linked quizzes, quantifying the conceptual reasoning gap. CORE then (i) synthesizes concept-aligned quizzes, (ii) injects brief concept snippets during rollouts to elicit concept-primed trajectories, and (iii) reinforces conceptual reasoning via trajectory replacement after group failures, a lightweight forward-KL constraint that aligns unguided with concept-primed policies, or standard GRPO directly on concept-aligned quizzes. Across several models, CORE delivers consistent gains over vanilla and SFT baselines on both in-domain concept-exercise suites and diverse out-of-domain math benchmarks. CORE unifies direct training on concept-aligned quizzes and concept-injected rollouts under outcome regularization. It provides fine-grained conceptual supervision that bridges problem-solving competence and genuine conceptual reasoning, while remaining algorithm- and verifier-agnostic.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CORE：面向概念强化学习弥合数学推理中的定义-应用鸿沟
大型语言模型（LLM）常能解决复杂数学题，但在需要真正理解概念时却无法正确应用。流行的可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）流程强化了最终答案，但缺乏细粒度的概念信号，导致模型更擅长模式复用而非概念应用。我们提出CORE（面向概念强化学习），一种将显式概念转化为可控监督信号的RL训练框架。从高质量、低污染的教科书资源出发，该资源将可验证习题与简洁概念描述相关联，我们通过合理性探测发现LLM能复述定义但无法通过概念关联测验，从而量化了概念推理鸿沟。CORE随后（i）合成概念对齐测验，（ii）在轨迹生成过程中注入简短概念片段以激发概念引导轨迹，以及（iii）通过组失败后的轨迹替换、轻量级前向KL约束（使无引导策略与概念引导策略对齐）或直接在概念对齐测验上应用标准GRPO来强化概念推理。在多个模型上，CORE在领域内概念习题集和多样化领域外数学基准测试中均持续优于普通基线和SFT基线。CORE在结果正则化下统一了概念对齐测验的直接训练与概念注入轨迹生成，提供了弥合解题能力与真正概念推理之间鸿沟的细粒度概念监督，同时保持算法和验证器无关性。
Summary / 总结
Large language models often solve math problems but fail to apply the correct concept when genuine understanding is required, as popular reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards reinforces final answers without providing fine-grained conceptual signals. To address this, the authors propose CORE (Concept-Oriented REinforcement), a training framework that turns explicit concepts into controllable supervision signals by synthesizing concept-aligned quizzes, injecting concept snippets during rollouts, and reinforcing conceptual reasoning via trajectory replacement or GRPO on concept-aligned quizzes. Experiments show that CORE achieves consistent improvements over vanilla and SFT baselines on both in-domain concept-exercise suites and diverse out-of-domain math benchmarks, effectively bridging the gap between problem-solving competence and genuine conceptual reasoning.
大型语言模型在解决数学问题时常常能得出正确答案，但在需要真正理解概念的应用场景中却表现不佳，因为流行的基于可验证奖励的强化学习只强化最终答案，缺乏细粒度的概念信号。为此，作者提出了CORE（面向概念的强化学习）框架，通过将显式概念转化为可控的监督信号，具体包括合成与概念对齐的测验、在推理过程中注入概念片段，以及通过轨迹替换或直接在概念对齐的测验上应用GRPO来强化概念推理。实验结果表明，CORE在领域内的概念习题集和多样化的领域外数学基准上，均比普通基线和SFT基线取得了一致的性能提升，有效弥合了问题解决能力与真正概念推理之间的鸿沟。
Requests of a Feather Must Flock Together: Batch Size vs. Prefix Homogeneity in LLM Inference
Authors: Saksham Rathi, Preeti, Mythili Vutukuru
First: 2026-05-07T11:34:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T11:34:10+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 36 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Auto-regressive token generation in large language models is memory-bound because it requires "attending to" key and value tensors (KV cache) of all previous tokens. Prior work aims to improve the efficiency of this decode process by batching multiple requests together, and maximizing batch size subject to GPU memory constraints. The key observation of our work is that with prefix-sharing workloads, smaller, prefix-homogeneous batches -- where all requests share a common prefix -- can achieve higher decode throughput than larger, heterogeneous batches, due to better spatial and temporal locality during KV cache accesses. However, prefix-aware schedulers in state-of-the-art inference engines maximize prefix reuse within a batch only to reduce KV cache memory footprint, but do not stop batch formation at smaller homogeneous batches that could have performed better. Further, we show that shared prefix detection in existing schedulers relies on radix-tree traversals, incurring substantial CPU overhead that is often comparable to GPU execution time. This paper presents Feather, a prefix-aware scheduler that uses reinforcement learning (RL) to learn the optimal tradeoff between batch size and prefix homogeneity. We also introduce Chunked Hash Tree (CHT), a lightweight data structure that enables fast prefix detection and efficient request selection for the RL scheduler, avoiding expensive tree traversals. We integrate Feather into vLLM and SGLang, and our evaluation shows that Feather achieves 2--10$\times$ higher end-to-end throughput as compared to existing schedulers, while doing no worse than the status quo when the workload does not have enough prefix sharing. Feather achieves these gains by reducing the total number of KV cache accesses, surpassing the performance of prefix-aware attention kernels that have the same goal.
中文标题/摘要
标题：同羽之求必成群：大语言模型推理中的批大小与前缀同质性
大语言模型中的自回归令牌生成受限于内存，因为它需要“关注”所有先前令牌的键值张量（KV缓存）。先前的工作旨在通过将多个请求批处理在一起，并在GPU内存约束下最大化批大小来提高此解码过程的效率。我们工作的关键观察是，在前缀共享工作负载下，较小且前缀同质的批次——其中所有请求共享一个公共前缀——由于KV缓存访问期间更好的空间和时间局部性，可以实现比更大、异质批次更高的解码吞吐量。然而，最先进推理引擎中的前缀感知调度器最大化批次内的前缀重用仅是为了减少KV缓存内存占用，但并未在可能表现更好的较小同质批次处停止批次形成。此外，我们表明现有调度器中的共享前缀检测依赖于基数树遍历，导致通常与GPU执行时间相当的显著CPU开销。本文提出了Feather，一种前缀感知调度器，它使用强化学习（RL）来学习批大小和前缀同质性之间的最优权衡。我们还引入了分块哈希树（CHT），这是一种轻量级数据结构，可实现快速前缀检测和RL调度器的高效请求选择，避免了昂贵的树遍历。我们将Feather集成到vLLM和SGLang中，评估表明，与现有调度器相比，Feather实现了2-10倍的端到端吞吐量提升，而在工作负载没有足够前缀共享时，其性能不低于现状。Feather通过减少KV缓存访问的总次数来实现这些增益，超越了具有相同目标的前缀感知注意力内核的性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the memory-bound nature of auto-regressive token generation in large language models due to KV cache accesses, and challenges the conventional wisdom that maximizing batch size always improves decode throughput. The authors observe that for prefix-sharing workloads, smaller batches with homogeneous prefixes can achieve higher throughput than larger heterogeneous batches by improving spatial and temporal locality. To exploit this, they propose Feather, a prefix-aware scheduler that uses reinforcement learning to learn the optimal tradeoff between batch size and prefix homogeneity, and introduce Chunked Hash Tree (CHT) for efficient prefix detection. Integrated into vLLM and SGLang, Feather achieves 2–10× higher end-to-end throughput compared to existing schedulers, without degrading performance when prefix sharing is limited, by reducing total KV cache accesses.
该论文针对大语言模型自回归生成中因KV缓存访问导致的内存瓶颈问题，挑战了最大化批处理大小总能提升解码吞吐量的传统观点。作者观察到，在具有前缀共享的工作负载中，较小但前缀同质的批次能通过改善空间和时间局部性，获得比大型异质批次更高的吞吐量。为此，他们提出了Feather，一个使用强化学习来学习批处理大小与前缀同质性之间最优权衡的前缀感知调度器，并引入了轻量级数据结构Chunked Hash Tree（CHT）以实现快速前缀检测。集成到vLLM和SGLang后，Feather相比现有调度器实现了2至10倍的端到端吞吐量提升，且在前缀共享不足时性能不降，其优势源于减少了KV缓存访问的总次数。
Novelty-based Tree-of-Thought Search for LLM Reasoning and Planning
Authors: Leon Hamm, Zlatan Ajanovic
First: 2026-05-07T11:28:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T11:28:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Although advances such as chain-of-thought, tree-of-thought or reinforcement learning have improved the performance of LLMs in reasoning and planning tasks, they are still brittle and have not achieved human-level performance in many domains, and often suffer from high time and token costs. Inspired by the success of width-based search in planning, we explore how the concept of novelty can be transferred to language domains and how it can improve tree-of-thought reasoning. A tree of thoughts relies on building possible "paths" of consecutive ideas or thoughts. These are generated by repeatedly prompting an LLM. In our paper, a measurable concept of novelty is proposed that describes the uniqueness of a new node (thought) in comparison to nodes previously seen in the search tree. Novelty is estimated by prompting an LLM and making use of embedded general knowledge from pre-training. This metric can then be used to prune branches and reduce the scope of the search. Although this method introduces more prompts per state, the overall token cost can be reduced by pruning and reducing the overall tree size. This procedure is tested and compared using several benchmarks in language-based planning and general reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于新颖性的思维树搜索用于大语言模型推理与规划
尽管思维链、思维树或强化学习等进展提升了LLM在推理与规划任务中的表现，但这些方法仍显脆弱，未能在多个领域达到人类水平，且常面临高时间与令牌成本问题。受宽度优先搜索在规划中成功应用的启发，我们探索了新颖性概念如何迁移至语言领域，以及如何改进思维树推理。思维树依赖于构建连续想法或思维的潜在“路径”，这些路径通过反复提示LLM生成。本文提出了一种可测量的新颖性概念，用于描述新节点（思维）相较于搜索树中先前节点的独特性。新颖性通过提示LLM并利用预训练中嵌入的通用知识来评估。该指标可用于剪枝分支并缩小搜索范围。尽管此方法在每个状态引入更多提示，但通过剪枝减少整体树规模可降低总令牌成本。该过程在基于语言的规划与通用推理的多个基准测试中进行了验证与比较。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the brittleness and high token costs of existing LLM reasoning methods like chain-of-thought and tree-of-thought by introducing a novelty-based pruning mechanism inspired by width-based search in planning. The method defines a measurable concept of novelty for each new thought node, estimated via LLM prompts leveraging pre-trained knowledge, and uses this metric to prune branches and reduce the search tree size. Experimental results on language-based planning and general reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that while the approach introduces additional prompts per state, it effectively lowers overall token costs by reducing tree scope without sacrificing performance.
该论文针对现有大语言模型推理方法（如思维链、思维树）的脆弱性和高令牌成本问题，借鉴规划中宽度搜索的成功经验，提出了一种基于新颖性的剪枝机制。该方法通过提示大语言模型并利用预训练中的通用知识，为每个新思维节点定义可测量的新颖性指标，并据此剪枝以缩小搜索树规模。在基于语言的规划和通用推理基准上的实验表明，尽管该方法在每个状态引入了更多提示，但通过剪枝减少了整体树的大小，从而有效降低了总令牌成本。
Optimal Transport for LLM Reward Modeling from Noisy Preference
Authors: Licheng Pan, Haochen Yang, Haoxuan Li, Yunsheng Lu, Yongqi Tong, Yinuo Wang, Shijian Wang, Zhixuan Chu, Lei Shen, Yuan Lu, Hao Wang
First: 2026-05-07T11:26:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T11:26:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward models are fundamental to Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), yet real-world datasets are inevitably corrupted by noisy preference. Conventional training objectives tend to overfit these errors, while existing denoising approaches often rely on homogeneous noise assumptions that fail to capture the complexity of linguistic preferences. To handle these challenges, we propose SelectiveRM, a framework grounded in optimal transport. We first devise a Joint Consistency Discrepancy to align the distribution of model predictions with preference data. Furthermore, to address the limitation of strict mass conservation which compels the model to fit outliers, we incorporate a Mass Relaxation mechanism via partial transport. This enables the autonomous exclusion of samples with noisy preference that contradict semantic consistency. Theoretically, we demonstrate that SelectiveRM optimizes a tighter upper bound on the unobserved clean risk. Extensive experiments validate that our approach significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across diverse benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于最优传输的含噪偏好下大语言模型奖励建模
奖励模型是基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）的基础，然而现实世界的数据集不可避免地受到含噪偏好的污染。传统训练目标容易过拟合这些错误，而现有的去噪方法通常依赖于同质噪声假设，无法捕捉语言偏好的复杂性。为应对这些挑战，我们提出SelectiveRM，一个基于最优传输的框架。我们首先设计联合一致性差异，使模型预测的分布与偏好数据对齐。此外，为解决严格质量守恒迫使模型拟合异常值的局限性，我们通过部分传输引入质量松弛机制。这使得模型能够自主排除与语义一致性矛盾的含噪偏好样本。理论上，我们证明SelectiveRM优化了未观测干净风险的一个更紧的上界。大量实验验证了我们的方法在多种基准上显著优于现有最先进基线。

该论文针对强化学习从人类反馈中奖励建模时偏好数据噪声问题，提出基于最优传输的SelectiveRM框架。通过联合一致性差异对齐模型预测与偏好分布，并引入质量松弛机制实现部分传输，自动排除语义不一致的噪声样本。理论上证明该方法优化了未观测干净风险的上界，实验表明其在多个基准上显著优于现有方法。
InvEvolve: Evolving White-Box Inventory Policies via Large Language Models with Performance Guarantees
Authors: Chenyu Huang, Jianghao Lin, Zhengyang Tang, Bo Jiang, Ruoqing Jiang, Benyou Wang, Lai Wei
First: 2026-05-01T03:12:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T10:53:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study how large language models can be used to evolve inventory policies in online, non-stationary environments. Our work is motivated by recent advances in LLM-based evolutionary search, such as AlphaEvolve, which demonstrates strong performance for static and highly structured problems such as mathematical discovery, but is not directly suited to online dynamic inventory settings. To this end, we propose InvEvolve, an end-to-end inventory-policy evolution and inference framework grounded in confidence-interval-based certification. The framework trains a large language model using reinforcement learning, incorporates demand data as well as numerical and textual features beyond demand, and generates white-box inventory policy with statistical safety guarantees for deployment in future periods. We further introduce a unified theoretical interface that connects training, inference, and deployment. This allows us to characterize the probability lower bound that the InvEvolve evolves a statistically safe and improved policy, and to quantify the multi-period performance gap relative to the oracle-safe benchmark. Tested on both synthetic data and real-world retail data, InvEvolve outperforms classical inventory policies and deep learning based methods. In canonical inventory settings, it evolves new policies that improve upon existing benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：InvEvolve：基于大语言模型且具有性能保证的白盒库存策略进化方法
我们研究如何利用大语言模型在在线、非平稳环境中进化库存策略。受近期基于LLM的进化搜索（如AlphaEvolve）启发，该方法在数学发现等静态且高度结构化问题上表现优异，但无法直接适用于在线动态库存场景。为此，我们提出InvEvolve——一种基于置信区间认证的端到端库存策略进化与推理框架。该框架通过强化学习训练大语言模型，整合需求数据及超越需求的数值与文本特征，生成具有统计安全保证的白盒库存策略以部署于未来时段。我们进一步引入统一理论接口连接训练、推理与部署，从而刻画InvEvolve进化出统计安全且改进策略的概率下界，并量化其与最优安全基准的多周期性能差距。在合成数据与真实零售数据上的测试表明，InvEvolve优于经典库存策略与深度学习方法。在典型库存场景中，它进化出的新策略改进了现有基准。

Experimental results on synthetic and real-world retail data show that InvEvolve outperforms classical inventory policies and deep learning methods, evolving new policies that improve upon existing benchmarks in canonical settings.
