Democratizing Tool Learning with Environments Fully Simulated by a Free 8B Language Model
Authors: Chenming Tang, Hsiu-Yuan Huang, Weijie Liu, Junqiang Zheng, Saiyong Yang, Yunfang Wu
First: 2026-04-20T02:54:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T10:48:35+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a prevalent paradigm for training tool calling agents, which typically requires online interactive environments. Existing approaches either rely on training data with ground truth annotations or require advanced proprietary language models (LMs) to synthesize environments that keep fixed once created. In this work, we propose TRUSTEE, a cost-friendly method for training tool calling agents with dynamic environments fully simulated by free open-source LMs that can be as small as 8B, including task generation, user simulation, tool simulation and trajectory evaluation, paired with an adaptive curriculum learning mechanism that controls task difficulty during training. Our empirical results show that TRUSTEE outperforms baselines which require extra external resources in most cases. These confirm that, with a sufficiently sophisticated design, even simulated environments with a local 8B LM as the backbone could set a strong baseline for tool learning. We hope our proposed paradigm could democratize tool learning and inspire future research on environment scaling with limited resources.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用免费8B语言模型完全模拟环境，实现工具学习民主化
强化学习已成为训练工具调用代理的主流范式，通常需要在线交互环境。现有方法要么依赖带真实标注的训练数据，要么需要高级专有语言模型来合成固定不变的环境。本文提出TRUSTEE，一种经济高效的方法，通过免费开源语言模型（可小至8B参数）完全模拟动态环境来训练工具调用代理，包括任务生成、用户模拟、工具模拟和轨迹评估，并配备自适应课程学习机制以控制训练任务难度。实验结果表明，TRUSTEE在多数情况下优于需要额外外部资源的基线方法。这证实了，通过足够精巧的设计，即使以本地8B语言模型为骨干的模拟环境也能为工具学习设定强基线。我们希望该范式能推动工具学习民主化，并启发有限资源下环境扩展的未来研究。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces TRUSTEE, a cost-friendly method for training tool-calling agents using reinforcement learning, motivated by the high cost and reliance on proprietary models in existing approaches. TRUSTEE simulates dynamic environments entirely with a free 8B open-source language model, incorporating task generation, user simulation, tool simulation, and trajectory evaluation, along with an adaptive curriculum learning mechanism to control task difficulty. Experimental results show that TRUSTEE outperforms baselines requiring extra external resources in most cases, demonstrating that even simulated environments with a small 8B LM can set a strong baseline for tool learning.
该论文提出了TRUSTEE，一种经济实惠的训练工具调用代理的方法，采用强化学习范式，旨在解决现有方法依赖昂贵专有模型的问题。TRUSTEE完全使用免费的8B开源语言模型模拟动态环境，包括任务生成、用户模拟、工具模拟和轨迹评估，并配备自适应课程学习机制来控制任务难度。实验结果表明，TRUSTEE在大多数情况下优于需要额外外部资源的基线方法，证明即使以小型8B语言模型为骨干的模拟环境也能为工具学习设定强基线。
Teaching Metric Distance to Discrete Autoregressive Language Models
Authors: Jiwan Chung, Saejin Kim, Yongrae Jo, Jaewoo Park, Dongjun Min, Youngjae Yu
First: 2025-03-04T08:14:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T10:25:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) operate as autoregressive predictors over discrete token vocabularies, a formulation that has enabled their adaptation far beyond natural language to vision, robotics, and multimodal reasoning. However, training against one-hot targets disregards metric relationships between tokens and limits effectiveness on tasks where distance is meaningful, such as numerical values, spatial coordinates, or quantized embeddings. We introduce DIST2Loss, a distance-aware objective for discrete autoregressive models that replaces one-hot targets with reward-weighted distributions derived from predefined token distances. DIST2Loss can be interpreted as the closed-form solution to entropy-regularized policy optimization with known per-token rewards, retaining the core mechanism of reinforcement learning while avoiding sampling, rollouts, and instability. Our experiments show that DIST2Loss improves data efficiency and downstream performance across diverse domains. It yields tighter bounding boxes in visual grounding, accelerates robotic manipulation by improving action learning, enhances reward modeling for LLM alignment, and strengthens vector-quantized image generation. These results demonstrate that distance-aware supervision offers a simple and general alternative to one-hot supervision for discrete autoregressive models.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of discrete autoregressive language models that use one-hot targets, which ignore metric relationships between tokens and hinder performance on tasks where distance is meaningful, such as numerical values or spatial coordinates. The authors propose DIST2Loss, a distance-aware objective that replaces one-hot targets with reward-weighted distributions derived from predefined token distances, interpretable as a closed-form solution to entropy-regularized policy optimization. Experiments demonstrate that DIST2Loss improves data efficiency and performance across diverse domains, including tighter bounding boxes in visual grounding, accelerated robotic manipulation, enhanced reward modeling for LLM alignment, and stronger vector-quantized image generation.
该论文针对离散自回归语言模型使用独热目标而忽略词元间度量关系、在数值或空间坐标等距离敏感任务上效果受限的问题，提出了DIST2Loss这一距离感知目标函数。该方法用基于预定义词元距离的奖励加权分布替代独热目标，可解释为熵正则化策略优化的闭式解，避免了采样、展开和不稳定性。实验表明，DIST2Loss在多个领域提升了数据效率和下游性能，包括视觉定位中更紧的边界框、加速机器人操作的动作学习、增强大语言模型对齐的奖励建模，以及改进向量量化图像生成。
BehaviorGuard: Online Backdoor Defense for Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yinbo Yu, Xueyu Yin, Jiadai Wang, Chunwei Tian, Sai Xu, Qi Zhu, Daoqiang Zhang
Venue: IJCAI 2026
First: 2026-05-07T10:21:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T10:21:14+00:00
Comments: 11 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Backdoor attacks pose a serious threat to deep reinforcement learning (DRL). Current defenses typically rely on reward anomalies to reverse-engineer triggers and model finetuning to remove backdoors. However, complex trigger patterns undermine their robustness, and fine-tuning entails high costs, limiting practical utility. Therefore, we shift defense concerns to trigger-agnostic backdoor output behaviors and propose BehaviorGuard, an online behavior-based backdoor detection and mitigation framework for DRL. Specifically, we find that regardless of attacks, backdoored policies induce consistent shifts in action distributions to ensure reliable activation, leaving detectable traces in high-quantile regions and distribution tails, even in the absence of triggers. Based on this, we design a novel metric that captures behavioral drift in action distributions to identify and suppress backdoor actions at runtime. To our knowledge, this is the first online backdoor defense that counters attacks both in single- and multi-agent DRL. Evaluated across diverse benchmarks with different backdoor attacks, BehaviorGuard consistently surpasses prior methods in both efficacy and efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：BehaviorGuard：面向深度强化学习的在线后门防御
后门攻击对深度强化学习构成严重威胁。现有防御通常依赖奖励异常来逆向工程触发器，并通过模型微调移除后门。然而，复杂触发模式削弱了其鲁棒性，且微调成本高昂，限制了实际应用。因此，我们将防御重点转向与触发器无关的后门输出行为，提出BehaviorGuard——一种面向深度强化学习的在线基于行为后门检测与缓解框架。具体而言，我们发现无论攻击方式如何，被植入后门的策略都会导致动作分布发生一致偏移，以确保可靠激活，即使在无触发器情况下，也会在高分位数区域和分布尾部留下可检测痕迹。基于此，我们设计了一种新指标，捕捉动作分布中的行为漂移，以在运行时识别并抑制后门动作。据我们所知，这是首个能同时应对单智能体和多智能体深度强化学习中攻击的在线后门防御方法。在多种基准测试和不同后门攻击下的评估表明，BehaviorGuard在有效性和效率上均持续优于先前方法。
Summary / 总结
Backdoor attacks pose a serious threat to deep reinforcement learning (DRL), and existing defenses relying on reward anomalies and model fine-tuning are often brittle against complex triggers and incur high costs. To address this, the authors propose BehaviorGuard, an online behavior-based defense framework that is trigger-agnostic. It detects and mitigates backdoor attacks by monitoring shifts in action distributions, specifically in high-quantile regions and distribution tails, which consistently occur under backdoored policies even without triggers. Evaluated across diverse benchmarks with various backdoor attacks in both single- and multi-agent DRL, BehaviorGuard consistently outperforms prior methods in both efficacy and efficiency.
后门攻击对深度强化学习构成严重威胁，现有依赖奖励异常和模型微调的防御方法在面对复杂触发器时鲁棒性不足且成本高昂。为此，作者提出BehaviorGuard，一种在线、基于行为且与触发器无关的防御框架。它通过监测动作分布中的高分位数区域和分布尾部变化来检测和抑制后门动作，因为后门策略即使在没有触发器的情况下也会在这些区域留下可检测的痕迹。在多种基准测试和不同后门攻击下的评估表明，BehaviorGuard在单智能体和多智能体深度强化学习中均一致地在有效性和效率上超越了先前方法。
Time Series Reasoning via Process-Verifiable Thinking Data Synthesis and Scheduling for Tailored LLM Reasoning
Authors: Jiahui Zhou, Dan Li, Boxin Li, Xiao Zhang, Erli Meng, Lin Li, Zhuomin Chen, Jian Lou, See-Kiong Ng
First: 2026-02-08T05:42:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T10:16:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Time series is a pervasive data type across various application domains, rendering the reasonable solving of diverse time series tasks a long-standing goal. Recent advances in large language models (LLMs), especially their reasoning abilities unlocked through reinforcement learning (RL), have opened new opportunities for tackling tasks with long Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning. However, leveraging LLM reasoning for time series remains in its infancy, hindered by the absence of carefully curated time series CoT data for training, limited data efficiency caused by underexplored data scheduling, and the lack of RL algorithms tailored for exploiting such time series CoT data. In this paper, we introduce VeriTime, a framework that tailors LLMs for time series reasoning through data synthesis, data scheduling, and RL training. First, we propose a data synthesis pipeline that constructs a TS-text multimodal dataset with process-verifiable annotations. Second, we design a data scheduling mechanism that arranges training samples according to a principled hierarchy of difficulty and task taxonomy. Third, we develop a two-stage reinforcement finetuning featuring fine-grained, multi-objective rewards that leverage verifiable process-level CoT data. Extensive experiments show that VeriTime substantially boosts LLM performance across diverse time series reasoning tasks. Notably, it enables compact 3B, 4B models to achieve reasoning capabilities on par with or exceeding those of larger proprietary LLMs.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces VeriTime, a framework designed to enhance large language models' reasoning capabilities for time series tasks by addressing the lack of curated Chain-of-Thought data, inefficient data scheduling, and insufficient reinforcement learning algorithms. The method comprises three key components: a data synthesis pipeline that creates a time series-text multimodal dataset with process-verifiable annotations, a data scheduling mechanism that organizes training samples by difficulty and task taxonomy, and a two-stage reinforcement finetuning process that uses fine-grained, multi-objective rewards based on verifiable process-level CoT data. Experimental results demonstrate that VeriTime significantly improves LLM performance across diverse time series reasoning tasks, enabling compact 3B and 4B models to achieve reasoning capabilities comparable to or exceeding those of larger proprietary LLMs.
该论文提出了VeriTime框架，旨在通过解决缺乏精心策划的思维链数据、数据调度效率低下以及强化学习算法不足等问题，增强大语言模型在时间序列任务中的推理能力。该方法包括三个关键部分：一个数据合成管道，用于构建带有过程可验证注释的时间序列-文本多模态数据集；一个数据调度机制，根据难度和任务分类法组织训练样本；以及一个两阶段强化微调过程，利用基于可验证过程级思维链数据的细粒度多目标奖励。实验结果表明，VeriTime显著提升了LLM在多种时间序列推理任务上的性能，使紧凑的3B和4B模型能够达到或超越更大规模专有LLM的推理能力。
Beyond Uniform Credit Assignment: Selective Eligibility Traces for RLVR
Authors: Chaoli Mou, Zhan Zhuang, Xinning Chen, Yu Zhang
First: 2026-05-07T10:11:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T10:11:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become a key approach for improving the reasoning abilities of large language models. However, widely used critic-free algorithms such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) necessitate a ``uniform credit assignment'' assumption that indiscriminately broadcast trajectory-level advantages, hindering learning efficiency by failing to distinguish critical reasoning steps. To address this limitation, we propose Selective Eligibility Traces (S-trace). Grounded in the intuition of partial trust region preservation, we initially introduce P-trace as a sample-efficient, critic-free eligibility traces method, upon which we build S-trace, implementing a sparse eligibility traces mechanism to further mitigate variance and achieve fine-grained credit assignment by selectively masking low-entropy tokens. Theoretically, we contextualize the recent Group Sequence Policy Optimization (GSPO) method within the critic-free eligibility traces framework, identifying it as a special instance of the eligibility traces method operating under uniform credit assignment. Experiments demonstrate that S-trace not only outperforms GRPO, showing gains of 0.49\% on Qwen3-1.7B and 3.16\% on Qwen3-4B, and maintaining a robust 2.98\% improvement when scaled further to Qwen3-8B in average pass@16, but notably achieves this with simultaneously higher sample and token efficiency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越均匀信用分配：面向RLVR的选择性资格迹方法
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的关键方法。然而，广泛使用的无评论家算法（如组相对策略优化GRPO）需要“均匀信用分配”假设，即不加区分地广播轨迹级优势，因无法区分关键推理步骤而阻碍学习效率。为解决此局限，我们提出选择性资格迹（S-trace）。基于部分信任域保持的直觉，我们首先引入P-trace作为样本高效的无评论家资格迹方法，并在此基础上构建S-trace，通过选择性掩蔽低熵令牌实现稀疏资格迹机制，以进一步降低方差并实现细粒度信用分配。理论上，我们将近期提出的组序列策略优化（GSPO）方法置于无评论家资格迹框架中，将其识别为在均匀信用分配下运行的资格迹方法的特例。实验表明，S-trace不仅优于GRPO——在Qwen3-1.7B上提升0.49%，在Qwen3-4B上提升3.16%，且当扩展至Qwen3-8B时仍保持2.98%的稳健提升（平均pass@16指标），更值得注意的是，它在实现更高样本与令牌效率的同时达成此效果。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of uniform credit assignment in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for large language models, where methods like GRPO indiscriminately broadcast trajectory-level advantages and fail to distinguish critical reasoning steps. To overcome this, the authors propose Selective Eligibility Traces (S-trace), building on a sample-efficient, critic-free eligibility traces method called P-trace that is grounded in partial trust region preservation, and then implementing a sparse eligibility traces mechanism that selectively masks low-entropy tokens for fine-grained credit assignment and variance reduction. Theoretically, they show that Group Sequence Policy Optimization (GSPO) is a special case of this framework under uniform credit assignment. Experiments demonstrate that S-trace outperforms GRPO, achieving gains of 0.49% on Qwen3-1.7B, 3.16% on Qwen3-4B, and a robust 2.98% improvement on Qwen3-8B in average pass@16, while also achieving higher sample and token efficiency.
该论文针对强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）中均匀信用分配的限制，即GRPO等方法不加区分地广播轨迹级优势，无法区分关键推理步骤，从而阻碍学习效率的问题。为此，作者提出了选择性资格迹（S-trace），基于部分信任区域保留的直觉，先引入样本高效、无评论家的资格迹方法P-trace，再通过选择性掩码低熵令牌实现稀疏资格迹机制，以进行细粒度信用分配并降低方差。理论上，他们将组序列策略优化（GSPO）方法定位为该框架下均匀信用分配的一个特例。实验表明，S-trace不仅优于GRPO，在Qwen3-1.7B上提升0.49%，在Qwen3-4B上提升3.16%，并在扩展到Qwen3-8B时保持2.98%的稳健提升（平均pass@16），而且同时实现了更高的样本和令牌效率。
CAMEL: Confidence-Gated Reflection for Reward Modeling
Authors: Zirui Zhu, Hailun Xu, Yang Luo, Yong Liu, Kanchan Sarkar, Kun Xu, Yang You
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-02-24T08:20:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T09:57:25+00:00
Comments: ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward models play a fundamental role in aligning large language models with human preferences. Existing methods predominantly follow two paradigms: scalar discriminative preference models, which are efficient but lack interpretability, and generative judging models, which offer richer reasoning at the cost of higher computational overhead. We observe that the log-probability margin between verdict tokens strongly correlates with prediction correctness, providing a reliable proxy for instance difficulty without additional inference cost. Building on this insight, we propose CAMEL, a confidence-gated reflection framework that performs a lightweight single-token preference decision first and selectively invokes reflection only for low-confidence instances. To induce effective self-correction, we train the model via reinforcement learning with counterfactual prefix augmentation, which exposes the model to diverse initial verdicts and encourages genuine revision. Empirically, CAMEL achieves state-of-the-art performance on three widely used reward-model benchmarks with 82.9% average accuracy, surpassing the best prior model by 3.2% and outperforming 70B-parameter models using only 14B parameters, while establishing a strictly better accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CAMEL：基于置信度门控的反思机制用于奖励建模
奖励模型在将大型语言模型与人类偏好对齐中扮演着基础性角色。现有方法主要遵循两种范式：标量判别偏好模型（高效但缺乏可解释性）和生成式评判模型（提供更丰富的推理但计算开销更高）。我们观察到，判决令牌之间的对数概率差与预测正确性高度相关，可在不增加推理成本的情况下提供可靠的实例难度代理指标。基于这一发现，我们提出CAMEL——一种置信度门控反思框架，该框架首先执行轻量级的单令牌偏好决策，并仅对低置信度实例选择性调用反思。为诱导有效的自我修正，我们通过反事实前缀增强的强化学习训练模型，使模型暴露于多样化的初始判决并鼓励真正的修正。实验表明，CAMEL在三个广泛使用的奖励模型基准上取得了82.9%的平均准确率，超越先前最佳模型3.2%，并以仅14B参数超越70B参数模型，同时建立了严格更优的准确率-效率帕累托前沿。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces CAMEL, a confidence-gated reflection framework for reward modeling that addresses the trade-off between efficiency and interpretability in aligning large language models with human preferences. The method leverages the observation that the log-probability margin between verdict tokens strongly correlates with prediction correctness, enabling a lightweight single-token preference decision followed by selective reflection only for low-confidence instances, with self-correction induced via reinforcement learning and counterfactual prefix augmentation. Experimental results show that CAMEL achieves state-of-the-art performance on three reward-model benchmarks with 82.9% average accuracy, surpassing the best prior model by 3.2% and outperforming 70B-parameter models using only 14B parameters, while establishing a strictly better accuracy-efficiency Pareto frontier.
该论文提出了CAMEL，一种基于置信度门控的反思框架，用于奖励建模，以解决大型语言模型与人类偏好对齐中效率与可解释性之间的权衡。该方法利用判决令牌的对数概率差与预测正确性高度相关的观察，先进行轻量级的单令牌偏好决策，仅对低置信度实例选择性触发反思，并通过强化学习和反事实前缀增强诱导自我修正。实验结果表明，CAMEL在三个广泛使用的奖励模型基准上取得了82.9%的平均准确率，超越最佳先前模型3.2%，且仅用14B参数就超越了70B参数模型，同时建立了严格更优的准确率-效率帕累托前沿。
Near-Policy: Accelerating On-Policy Distillation via Asynchronous Generation and Selective Packing
Authors: Miao Rang, Zhenni Bi, Hang Zhou, Kai Han, Xuechun Wang, An Xiao, Xinghao Chen, Yunhe Wang, Hanting Chen
First: 2026-05-07T09:50:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T09:50:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Standard knowledge distillation for autoregressive models often suffers from distribution mismatch. While on-policy methods mitigate this by leveraging student-generated outputs, they rely on computationally expensive Reinforcement Learning (RL) frameworks. To improve efficiency, we propose Near-Policy Distillation (NPD), an asynchronous approach that decouples student generation from training. This reformulation enables Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) with sequence packing. However, asynchronous updates inevitably introduce policy lag and sample noise, which can cause the behavior to drift from near-policy toward off-policy. To counteract this without sacrificing efficiency, NPD integrates sparse student updates and the $Δ$-IFD filtering mechanism, a heuristic sample selection mechanism that empirically stabilizes the optimization trajectory. By filtering extreme out-of-distribution samples, $Δ$-IFD prevents noise from dominating the gradients, ensuring updates remain within a safe proximal learning zone. Empirically, the NPD framework achieves a 8.1x speedup over on-policy baselines and outperforms SFT by 8.09%. Crucially, by effectively narrowing the exploration space for subsequent RL, our method enables openPangu-Embedded-1B to reach a state-of-the-art score of 68.73%, outperforming the substantially larger Qwen3-1.7B. Codes will be released soon.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the distribution mismatch problem in standard knowledge distillation for autoregressive models, where on-policy methods are effective but computationally expensive due to reliance on Reinforcement Learning. The authors propose Near-Policy Distillation (NPD), which asynchronously decouples student generation from training, enabling Supervised Fine-Tuning with sequence packing for efficiency. To mitigate policy lag and sample noise from asynchronous updates, NPD incorporates sparse student updates and a Δ-IFD filtering mechanism that removes extreme out-of-distribution samples, keeping updates within a safe proximal zone. Empirically, NPD achieves an 8.1x speedup over on-policy baselines and outperforms SFT by 8.09%, and when combined with subsequent RL, it enables openPangu-Embedded-1B to reach a state-of-the-art score of 68.73%, surpassing the larger Qwen3-1.7B model.
该论文针对自回归模型标准知识蒸馏中的分布不匹配问题，指出在线策略方法虽有效但依赖强化学习导致计算成本高。作者提出近策略蒸馏（NPD），通过异步解耦学生生成与训练，利用序列打包实现监督微调以提高效率。为应对异步更新带来的策略滞后和样本噪声，NPD集成稀疏学生更新和Δ-IFD过滤机制，剔除极端分布外样本，确保更新处于安全近端学习区域。实验表明，NPD相比在线策略基线实现8.1倍加速，并超越监督微调8.09%；结合后续强化学习后，使openPangu-Embedded-1B模型达到68.73%的先进水平，超越更大的Qwen3-1.7B模型。
AceGRPO: Adaptive Curriculum Enhanced Group Relative Policy Optimization for Autonomous Machine Learning Engineering
Authors: Yuzhu Cai, Zexi Liu, Xinyu Zhu, Cheng Wang, Yanfeng Wang, Siheng Chen
First: 2026-02-08T10:55:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T09:44:38+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Autonomous Machine Learning Engineering (MLE) requires agents to perform sustained, iterative optimization over long horizons. While recent LLM-based agents show promise, current prompt-based agents for MLE suffer from behavioral stagnation due to frozen parameters. Although Reinforcement Learning (RL) offers a remedy, applying it to MLE is hindered by prohibitive execution latency and inefficient data selection. Recognizing these challenges, we propose AceGRPO with two core components: (1) Evolving Data Buffer that continuously repurposes execution traces into reusable training tasks, and (2) Adaptive Sampling guided by a Learnability Potential function, which dynamically prioritizes tasks at the agent's learning frontier to maximize learning efficiency. Leveraging AceGRPO, our trained Ace-30B model achieves a 100% valid submission rate on MLE-Bench-Lite, approaches the performance of proprietary frontier models, and outperforms larger open-source baselines (e.g., DeepSeek-V3.2), demonstrating robust capability for sustained iterative optimization. Code is available at https://github.com/yuzhu-cai/AceGRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AceGRPO：面向自主机器学习工程的自适应课程增强组相对策略优化
自主机器学习工程（MLE）要求智能体在长时间跨度内进行持续、迭代的优化。尽管近期基于大语言模型的智能体展现出潜力，但当前用于MLE的提示驱动型智能体因参数冻结而面临行为停滞问题。虽然强化学习（RL）提供了解决方案，但将其应用于MLE受到执行延迟过高和数据选择效率低下的阻碍。针对这些挑战，我们提出AceGRPO，包含两个核心组件：（1）演化数据缓冲区，持续将执行轨迹转化为可复用的训练任务；（2）基于可学习性势函数的自适应采样，动态优先处理智能体学习前沿的任务，以最大化学习效率。借助AceGRPO，我们训练的Ace-30B模型在MLE-Bench-Lite上实现了100%的有效提交率，性能接近专有前沿模型，并超越了更大的开源基线模型（如DeepSeek-V3.2），展现出持续迭代优化的稳健能力。代码已开源：https://github.com/yuzhu-cai/AceGRPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses behavioral stagnation in LLM-based agents for Autonomous Machine Learning Engineering (MLE) by proposing AceGRPO, a reinforcement learning framework. It introduces an Evolving Data Buffer that reuses execution traces as training tasks and an Adaptive Sampling mechanism guided by a Learnability Potential function to prioritize tasks at the agent's learning frontier. The trained Ace-30B model achieves a 100% valid submission rate on MLE-Bench-Lite, approaching proprietary frontier model performance and outperforming larger open-source baselines like DeepSeek-V3.2, demonstrating robust iterative optimization capability.
该论文针对基于LLM的自主机器学习工程代理在长周期迭代优化中出现的参数冻结导致的行为停滞问题，提出了AceGRPO强化学习框架。其核心包括持续重用执行轨迹作为训练任务的演化数据缓冲区，以及通过可学习潜力函数动态优先选择学习前沿任务的适应性采样机制。训练后的Ace-30B模型在MLE-Bench-Lite上实现了100%的有效提交率，性能接近专有前沿模型，并超越了DeepSeek-V3.2等更大规模的开源基线，展现了强大的持续迭代优化能力。
Alternating Reinforcement Learning with Contextual Rubric Rewards: Beyond the Scalarization Strategy
Authors: Guangchen Lan, Lian Xiong, Xin Zhou, Hejie Cui, Yuwei Zhang, Mao Li, Zhenyu Shi, Besnik Fetahu, Lihong Li, Xian Li
First: 2026-03-04T04:18:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T09:27:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Rubric Rewards (RLRR) is a framework that extends conventional reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and verifiable rewards (RLVR) by replacing scalar preference signals with structured, multi-dimensional, contextual rubric-based evaluations. However, existing approaches in RLRR are limited to linearly compressing vector rewards into a scalar reward with a fixed weightings, which is sensitive to artificial score design and fails to capture correlations among reward dimensions. To overcome the limitations of reward aggregation, this work proposes Alternating Reinforcement Learning with Rubric Rewards (ARL-RR), a framework that eliminates the need for a fixed scalarization by optimizing one semantic rubric meta-class at a time. Theoretically, we show that reward aggregation induces a variance contraction effect, which helps explain the performance gains. We further introduce a lightweight, search-based adaptation procedure that selects the next meta-class dynamically based on task performance, enabling the policy to emphasize critical objectives and thereby improve the model performance. Empirically, our experiments on the HealthBench dataset with experts annotations demonstrate that ARL-RR uniformly outperforms scalarized methods in both model performance and training efficiency across different model scales (1.7B, 4B, 8B, and 14B).
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of Reinforcement Learning with Rubric Rewards (RLRR), which linearly compresses multi-dimensional rubric evaluations into a scalar reward, making it sensitive to fixed weightings and unable to capture correlations among reward dimensions. To overcome this, the authors propose Alternating Reinforcement Learning with Rubric Rewards (ARL-RR), a framework that optimizes one semantic rubric meta-class at a time, eliminating the need for fixed scalarization, and theoretically show that reward aggregation causes a variance contraction effect explaining performance gains. A lightweight, search-based adaptation procedure dynamically selects the next meta-class based on task performance. Experiments on the HealthBench dataset with expert annotations demonstrate that ARL-RR uniformly outperforms scalarized methods in both model performance and training efficiency across model scales of 1.7B, 4B, 8B, and 14B.
该论文针对基于评分标准的强化学习（RLRR）的局限性，即线性地将多维评分标准压缩为标量奖励，导致对固定权重敏感且无法捕捉奖励维度间的相关性。为此，作者提出了交替强化学习与评分标准奖励（ARL-RR）框架，通过每次优化一个语义评分元类来消除固定标量化的需求，并从理论上证明奖励聚合会导致方差收缩效应，从而解释性能提升。一种轻量级的基于搜索的自适应过程根据任务性能动态选择下一个元类。在HealthBench数据集上的专家标注实验表明，ARL-RR在1.7B、4B、8B和14B模型规模下，在模型性能和训练效率上均一致优于标量化方法。
Posterior Inference in Latent Space for Scalable Constrained Black-box Optimization
Authors: Kiyoung Om, Kyuil Sim, Taeyoung Yun, Hyeongyu Kang, Jinkyoo Park
First: 2025-07-01T06:55:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T09:04:12+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 14 figures, 6 tables. Equal contribution by Kiyoung Om, Kyuil Sim, and Taeyoung Yun
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Optimizing high-dimensional black-box functions under black-box constraints is a pervasive task in a wide range of scientific and engineering problems. These problems are typically harder than unconstrained problems due to hard-to-find feasible regions. In this work, we reformulate constrained black-box optimization as posterior inference, and perform this inference in the latent space of generative models. Our method iterates through two stages. First, we train flow-based models to capture the data distribution and surrogate models that predict both function values and constraint violations. Second, we cast the candidate selection problem as a posterior inference problem to effectively search for promising candidates that have high objective values while not violating the constraints. Concretely, we utilize outsourced diffusion models to amortize the sampling from the posterior distribution in the latent space of flow-based models, which can bypass the issue of mode collapse. We empirically demonstrate that our method achieves superior performance across synthetic and real-world tasks. Our code is available \href{https://github.com/umkiyoung/CiBO}{here}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：潜在空间中的后验推断用于可扩展的约束黑箱优化
在科学和工程问题的广泛领域中，优化高维黑箱函数并受黑箱约束是一项普遍任务。由于可行区域难以找到，这些问题通常比无约束问题更困难。在这项工作中，我们将约束黑箱优化重新表述为后验推断，并在生成模型的潜在空间中执行此推断。我们的方法迭代两个阶段。首先，我们训练基于流的模型以捕获数据分布，并训练预测函数值和约束违反的代理模型。其次，我们将候选选择问题视为后验推断问题，以有效搜索具有高目标值且不违反约束的有前途的候选者。具体来说，我们利用外部扩散模型来摊销从基于流模型的潜在空间中的后验分布采样，这可以绕过模式崩溃的问题。我们通过实验证明，我们的方法在合成和现实任务中均实现了优越的性能。我们的代码可在此处获取。

This paper addresses the challenge of optimizing high-dimensional black-box functions under black-box constraints, which is more difficult than unconstrained optimization due to the difficulty of finding feasible regions. The authors reformulate constrained black-box optimization as a posterior inference problem and perform this inference in the latent space of generative models. The method iterates through two stages: first, training flow-based models to capture data distribution and surrogate models for function values and constraint violations; second, casting candidate selection as posterior inference using outsourced diffusion models to sample from the posterior in the latent space, bypassing mode collapse. Empirical results show superior performance on both synthetic and real-world tasks.

asRoBallet: Closing the Sim2Real Gap via Friction-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Underactuated Spherical Dynamics
Authors: Fang Wan, Guangyi Huang, Tianyu Wu, Zishang Zhang, Bangchao Huang, Haoran Sun, Mingdong Chen, Chaoyang Song
First: 2026-04-27T18:51:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T09:03:16+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 9 figure, accepted for RSS2026. For Supplementary Videos, see https://bionicdl.ancorasir.com/?p=2238
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce asRoBallet, to the best of our knowledge, the first end-to-end reinforcement learning (RL) locomotion policy deployed on a humanoid ballbot hardware platform. Historically, ballbots have served as a canonical benchmark for underactuated and nonholonomic control, which are characterized by a reality gap in complex friction models for wheel-ball-floor interactions. While current literature demonstrates successful handling of 3D balancing with LQR and MPC, transitioning to actual hardware for a humanoid ballbot using RL is currently hindered by critical gaps in contact modeling, actuator latency & jitter, and safe hardware exploration. This study proposes a high-fidelity MuJoCo simulation that explicitly models the discrete roller mechanics of ETH-type omni-wheels, thereby capturing parasitic vibrations and contact discontinuities that have previously been ignored. We also developed a Friction-Aware Reinforcement Learning framework that achieves zero-shot Sim2Real transfer by mastering the coupled rolling, lateral, and torsional friction channels at the wheel-ball and ball-floor interfaces. We designed asRoBallet through subtractive reconfiguration, repurposing key components from an overconstrained quadruped and integrating them into a newly designed structural frame to achieve a robust research platform at low cost. We also developed a generalized iOS ecosystem that transforms consumer electronics into a low-latency interface, enabling a single operator to orchestrate expressive humanoid maneuvers via intuitive natural motion.
中文标题/摘要
标题：asRoBallet：基于摩擦感知强化学习的欠驱动球体动力学Sim2Real差距弥合
我们提出asRoBallet，据我们所知，这是首个部署在类人球机器人硬件平台上的端到端强化学习运动策略。历史上，球机器人一直是欠驱动和非完整控制的经典基准，其特点在于轮-球-地面相互作用的复杂摩擦模型中存在现实差距。虽然现有文献展示了使用LQR和MPC成功处理3D平衡，但将强化学习应用于类人球机器人的实际硬件目前仍受限于接触建模、执行器延迟与抖动以及安全硬件探索方面的关键差距。本研究提出了一种高保真MuJoCo仿真，显式建模ETH型全向轮的离散滚子力学，从而捕捉先前被忽略的寄生振动和接触不连续性。我们还开发了摩擦感知强化学习框架，通过掌握轮-球和球-地面接口处的耦合滚动、横向和扭转摩擦通道，实现了零样本Sim2Real迁移。我们通过减法重构设计了asRoBallet，重新利用过约束四足机器人的关键组件并将其集成到新设计的结构框架中，以低成本构建了稳健的研究平台。我们还开发了一个通用iOS生态系统，将消费电子产品转化为低延迟接口，使单个操作员能够通过直观的自然运动编排富有表现力的类人动作。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces asRoBallet, the first end-to-end reinforcement learning locomotion policy deployed on a humanoid ballbot hardware, motivated by the challenge of closing the sim-to-real gap caused by complex friction models in wheel-ball-floor interactions. The method proposes a high-fidelity MuJoCo simulation that explicitly models discrete roller mechanics of omni-wheels to capture parasitic vibrations and contact discontinuities, along with a Friction-Aware Reinforcement Learning framework that masters coupled rolling, lateral, and torsional friction channels for zero-shot Sim2Real transfer. The system is built via subtractive reconfiguration from an overconstrained quadruped and controlled through a generalized iOS ecosystem. Experimental results demonstrate successful zero-shot transfer of the learned policy to real hardware, enabling expressive humanoid maneuvers with low-latency control.

Correct Is Not Enough: Training Reasoning Planners with Executor-Grounded Rewards
Authors: Tianyang Han, Hengyu Shi, Junjie Hu, Xu Yang, Zhiling Wang, Junhao Su
First: 2026-05-05T15:24:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T08:57:08+00:00
Comments: 36 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has become a common way to improve explicit reasoning in large language models, but final-answer correctness alone does not reveal whether the reasoning trace is faithful, reliable, or useful to the model that consumes it. This outcome-only signal can reinforce traces that are right for the wrong reasons, overstate reasoning gains by rewarding shortcuts, and propagate flawed intermediate states in multi-step systems. To this end, we propose TraceLift, a planner-executor training framework that treats reasoning as a consumable intermediate artifact. During planner training, the planner emits tagged reasoning. A frozen executor turns this reasoning into the final artifact for verifier feedback, while an executor-grounded reward shapes the intermediate trace. This reward multiplies a rubric-based Reasoning Reward Model (RM) score by measured uplift on the same frozen executor, crediting traces that are both high-quality and useful. To make reasoning quality directly learnable, we introduce TRACELIFT-GROUPS, a rubric-annotated reason-only dataset built from math and code seed problems. Each example is a same-problem group containing a high-quality reference trace and multiple plausible flawed traces with localized perturbations that reduce reasoning quality or solution support while preserving task relevance. Extensive experiments on code and math benchmarks show that this executor-grounded reasoning reward improves the two-stage planner-executor system over execution-only training, suggesting that reasoning supervision should evaluate not only whether a trace looks good, but also whether it helps the model that consumes it. Our code is available at: https://github.com/MasaiahHan/TraceLift
中文标题/摘要
标题：正确还不够：使用执行器锚定奖励训练推理规划器
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已成为提升大语言模型显式推理能力的常见方法，但仅凭最终答案的正确性无法揭示推理轨迹是否忠实、可靠或对使用该模型的系统有用。这种仅依赖结果的信号可能强化“歪打正着”的轨迹，通过奖励捷径夸大推理增益，并在多步系统中传播有缺陷的中间状态。为此，我们提出TraceLift——一种将推理视为可消费中间产物的规划器-执行器训练框架。在规划器训练阶段，规划器输出带标签的推理过程；冻结的执行器将此推理转化为最终产物以供验证器反馈，同时执行器锚定奖励塑造中间轨迹。该奖励将基于评分标准的推理奖励模型得分与同一冻结执行器上的实测提升相乘，从而奖励既高质量又有用的轨迹。为使推理质量可直接学习，我们引入TRACELIFT-GROUPS——基于数学和代码种子问题构建的带评分标注的纯推理数据集。每个示例包含同一问题的分组：一条高质量参考轨迹与多条合理但有缺陷的轨迹，这些缺陷轨迹通过局部扰动降低推理质量或解决方案支持度，同时保持任务相关性。在代码和数学基准上的大量实验表明，这种执行器锚定的推理奖励能提升两阶段规划器-执行器系统相较于纯执行训练的性能，说明推理监督不仅应评估轨迹是否“看起来好”，还应评估它是否对使用该模型的系统有帮助。我们的代码已开源：https://github.com/MasaiahHan/TraceLift
Summary / 总结
The paper identifies that training reasoning planners in large language models using only final-answer correctness can reinforce flawed or unfaithful reasoning traces, as outcome-only rewards fail to capture intermediate reasoning quality. To address this, the authors propose TraceLift, a planner-executor framework where a frozen executor converts the planner's tagged reasoning into a final artifact for verifier feedback, and an executor-grounded reward multiplies a rubric-based Reasoning Reward Model score by the measured uplift on the executor. Experiments on code and math benchmarks demonstrate that this executor-grounded reasoning reward improves the two-stage system over execution-only training, showing that reasoning supervision should evaluate both trace quality and its utility to the consuming model.
该论文指出，仅使用最终答案正确性来训练大型语言模型中的推理规划器，可能会强化有缺陷或不忠实的推理轨迹，因为仅基于结果的奖励无法捕捉中间推理质量。为此，作者提出了TraceLift框架，其中冻结的执行器将规划器的标记推理转化为最终产物以供验证器反馈，而基于执行器的奖励将基于评分标准的推理奖励模型分数与执行器上的测量提升相乘。在代码和数学基准上的实验表明，这种基于执行器的推理奖励优于仅基于执行的训练，说明推理监督应同时评估轨迹质量及其对消费模型的实用性。
SOPE: Stabilizing Off-Policy Evaluation for Online RL with Prior Data
Authors: Carlo Romeo, Girolamo Macaluso, Alessandro Sestini, Andrew D. Bagdanov
First: 2026-05-07T08:32:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T08:32:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Incorporating prior data into online reinforcement learning accelerates training but typically forces a difficult trade-off between high computational costs and long, multi-stage training pipelines. While fixed-length stabilization phases are significantly more computationally efficient than static update schedules, they require task-dependent manual tuning, risking either the waste of prior knowledge or severe overfitting. To address this, we propose SOPE, an algorithm that uses an actor-aligned Off-Policy Policy Evaluation (OPE) signal as an automated early-stopping mechanism to dynamically control the length of offline training phases. By evaluating the critic on a held-out validation split under the current policy's action distribution, SOPE halts gradient updates exactly when out-of-distribution benefits saturate, eliminating the need for manual schedule tuning. Evaluated on 25 continuous control tasks from the Minari benchmark suite, SOPE improves baseline performance by up to 45.6% while reducing the required TFLOPs by up to 22x, thus balancing the tradeoff between sample and computational efficiency. These findings demonstrate that adaptive, evaluation-driven update schedules are more effective than relying on static, exhaustive update schedules.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces SOPE, an algorithm designed to stabilize off-policy evaluation for online reinforcement learning when incorporating prior data. The motivation stems from the difficulty of balancing computational costs and training efficiency in existing methods, which often require manual tuning of fixed-length stabilization phases that risk wasting prior knowledge or causing overfitting. SOPE addresses this by using an actor-aligned Off-Policy Policy Evaluation (OPE) signal as an automated early-stopping mechanism, dynamically controlling the length of offline training phases based on when out-of-distribution benefits saturate. Evaluated on 25 continuous control tasks from the Minari benchmark suite, SOPE improves baseline performance by up to 45.6% while reducing computational requirements (TFLOPs) by up to 22x, demonstrating that adaptive, evaluation-driven update schedules outperform static ones.
该论文提出了SOPE算法，旨在稳定在线强化学习中利用先验数据的离策略评估。其动机源于现有方法在平衡计算成本和训练效率上的困难，这些方法通常需要手动调整固定长度的稳定阶段，容易浪费先验知识或导致过拟合。SOPE通过使用与演员对齐的离策略策略评估（OPE）信号作为自动早停机制，动态控制离线训练阶段的长度，在分布外收益饱和时停止梯度更新。在Minari基准套件的25个连续控制任务上评估，SOPE将基线性能提升了最高45.6%，同时将计算需求（TFLOPs）降低了最高22倍，证明了自适应、评估驱动的更新方案优于静态方案。
Offline Reinforcement Learning for Rotation Profile Control in Tokamaks
Authors: Rohit Sonker, Hiro Josep Farre Kaga, Jiayu Chen, Andrew Rothstein, Ian Char, Ricardo Shousha, Egemen Kolemen, Jeff Schneider
First: 2026-05-07T08:26:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T08:26:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tokamaks remain leading candidates for achieving practical fusion energy, yet many important control problems inside these devices are still difficult or unsolved. One such challenge is controlling the plasma rotation profile, which strongly influences stability, confinement, and transport. While the average rotation can be controlled, controlling the full profile is challenging due to high dimensionality, response to multiple actuators and dependence on plasma condition. Learning-based control methods, such as reinforcement learning (RL), provide a potential solution to this challenging problem with ability to model complex interactions leading to effective multi-input multi-output control. However, learning such policies is challenging due to the lack of accurate simulators that can model the rotation profile dynamics. In this work, we investigate the use of offline RL and offline model-based RL algorithms for rotation profile control, training them solely on historical data from the DIII-D tokamak. Our final method uses probabilistic models of plasma dynamics to generate rollouts for RL training. We deploy this policy on the DIII-D Tokamak and observe promising real-world results. We conclude by highlighting key challenges and insights from training and deploying an RL policy on a complex physical device while using only limited past data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：托卡马克旋转剖面控制的离线强化学习
托卡马克仍是实现实用聚变能的主要候选装置，但其内部许多重要控制问题仍难以解决或尚未攻克。其中一项挑战是控制等离子体旋转剖面，该剖面强烈影响稳定性、约束和输运。虽然平均旋转可控，但由于高维度、多执行器响应及对等离子体条件的依赖，完整剖面的控制极具挑战性。基于学习的控制方法（如强化学习）通过建模复杂交互实现有效的多输入多输出控制，为此难题提供了潜在解决方案。然而，由于缺乏能精确建模旋转剖面动力学的模拟器，学习此类策略面临困难。本研究探索了使用离线强化学习和离线基于模型的强化学习算法进行旋转剖面控制，仅基于DIII-D托卡马克的历史数据训练模型。最终方法采用等离子体动力学的概率模型生成轨迹用于强化学习训练，并在DIII-D托卡马克上部署该策略，观察到有前景的实际结果。最后，我们总结了在仅使用有限历史数据的情况下，于复杂物理设备上训练和部署强化学习策略的关键挑战与见解。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of controlling the plasma rotation profile in tokamaks, a critical factor for stability and confinement in fusion energy devices, by proposing offline reinforcement learning (RL) methods. The motivation stems from the difficulty of modeling high-dimensional, multi-actuator dynamics with limited accurate simulators. The method employs offline RL and offline model-based RL, using probabilistic models of plasma dynamics trained solely on historical data from the DIII-D tokamak to generate rollouts for policy learning. The policy was deployed on the DIII-D tokamak, yielding promising real-world results, demonstrating the feasibility of learning-based control from limited past data while highlighting key challenges in training and deployment on complex physical devices.
该论文针对托卡马克中等离子体旋转剖面控制这一影响聚变装置稳定性和约束的关键难题，提出使用离线强化学习方法。其动机源于高维度、多执行器依赖的动力学难以建模且缺乏精确模拟器。方法采用离线强化学习和基于模型的离线强化学习，仅利用DIII-D托卡马克的历史数据训练等离子体动力学的概率模型，并生成轨迹用于策略学习。该策略在DIII-D托卡马克上部署后取得了有前景的实际结果，证明了在有限历史数据下基于学习的控制的可行性，同时总结了在复杂物理设备上训练和部署强化学习策略的关键挑战与经验。
Measuring Learning Progress via Gradient-Momentum Coupling
Authors: Samuel Blad, Martin Längkvist, Amy Loutfi
First: 2026-05-07T08:26:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T08:26:50+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 15 figures, preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Measuring learning progress is essential for curiosity-driven exploration in reinforcement learning, but widely used signals such as prediction error often fail to distinguish meaningful, learnable patterns from random noise. This paper proposes Gradient-Momentum Coupling (GMC), a signal derived from optimization dynamics that quantifies how useful each sample's gradient is for ongoing learning by measuring its per-parameter normalized absolute product with the momentum from previous gradients. By leveraging momentum's natural filtering of noise and oscillations, GMC identifies samples that contribute to ongoing parameter updates. Controlled experiments demonstrate noise robustness and emergent curriculum learning, with the signal prioritizing tasks by learning speed rather than difficulty. Experiments on MiniGrid suggest that replacing prediction error with GMC within existing curiosity-driven architectures can improve robustness to observation noise.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过梯度-动量耦合衡量学习进展
衡量学习进展对于强化学习中好奇心驱动的探索至关重要，但广泛使用的信号（如预测误差）往往难以区分有意义的可学习模式与随机噪声。本文提出梯度-动量耦合（GMC），这是一种源自优化动态的信号，通过测量每个样本梯度与先前梯度动量的逐参数归一化绝对乘积，量化该样本对持续学习的贡献。利用动量对噪声和振荡的自然过滤特性，GMC能够识别出对持续参数更新有贡献的样本。控制实验表明，该信号具有噪声鲁棒性和涌现式课程学习能力，能根据学习速度而非难度对任务进行优先级排序。在MiniGrid上的实验表明，在现有好奇心驱动架构中用GMC替代预测误差可提升对观测噪声的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem that traditional curiosity-driven exploration signals, such as prediction error, are often unreliable in distinguishing learnable patterns from random noise. The authors propose Gradient-Momentum Coupling (GMC), a signal derived from optimization dynamics that measures the per-parameter normalized absolute product of each sample's gradient with the momentum from previous gradients, thereby identifying samples that contribute to ongoing learning. Controlled experiments show that GMC is robust to noise and enables emergent curriculum learning by prioritizing tasks based on learning speed, and experiments on MiniGrid demonstrate that replacing prediction error with GMC improves robustness to observation noise in curiosity-driven architectures.
该论文针对传统好奇心驱动探索信号（如预测误差）常无法区分可学习模式与随机噪声的问题，提出基于优化动力学的梯度-动量耦合（GMC）信号。该方法通过计算每个样本梯度与先前梯度动量的逐参数归一化绝对乘积，量化样本对持续学习的贡献，利用动量对噪声和振荡的自然过滤能力识别有效样本。控制实验表明GMC具有噪声鲁棒性并能产生涌现课程学习，通过学习速度而非难度优先排序任务；在MiniGrid上的实验显示，用GMC替代预测误差可提升现有好奇心驱动架构对观测噪声的鲁棒性。
Frictional Q-Learning
Authors: Hyunwoo Kim, Hyo Kyung Lee
First: 2025-09-24T05:42:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T08:14:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Off-policy reinforcement learning suffers from extrapolation errors when a learned policy selects actions that are weakly supported in the replay buffer. In this study, we address this issue by drawing an analogy to static friction. From this perspective, the replay buffer is represented as a smooth, low-dimensional action manifold, where the support directions correspond to the tangential component, while the normal component captures the dominant first-order extrapolation error. This decomposition reveals an intrinsic anisotropy in value sensitivity that naturally induces a stability condition analogous to a friction threshold. To mitigate deviations toward unsupported actions, we propose Frictional Q-Learning, an off-policy algorithm that encodes supported actions as tangent directions using a contrastive variational autoencoder. We further show that an orthonormal basis of the orthogonal complement corresponds to normal components under mild local isometry assumptions. Empirical results on standard continuous-control benchmarks demonstrate robust, stable performance compared with baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：摩擦Q学习
离策略强化学习在学习策略选择重放缓冲区中支持较弱的动作时，会遭受外推误差。在本研究中，我们通过类比静摩擦来解决这一问题。从这一视角出发，重放缓冲区被表示为一个光滑的低维动作流形，其中支持方向对应切向分量，而法向分量捕获主要的一阶外推误差。这种分解揭示了价值敏感性中固有的各向异性，自然诱导出类似于摩擦阈值的稳定性条件。为了减轻向不支持动作的偏离，我们提出了摩擦Q学习，这是一种离策略算法，通过对比变分自编码器将支持动作编码为切向方向。我们进一步证明，在温和的局部等距假设下，正交补的标准正交基对应于法向分量。在标准连续控制基准上的实证结果表明，与基线相比，该方法具有稳健且稳定的性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses extrapolation errors in off-policy reinforcement learning, which occur when a learned policy selects actions poorly supported in the replay buffer. Drawing an analogy to static friction, the authors decompose the replay buffer into a smooth, low-dimensional action manifold, where support directions are tangential and extrapolation errors are normal, revealing an anisotropy in value sensitivity that suggests a friction-like stability condition. They propose Frictional Q-Learning, which uses a contrastive variational autoencoder to encode supported actions as tangent directions and leverages an orthonormal basis for normal components under local isometry. Empirical results on continuous-control benchmarks show robust and stable performance compared to baselines.
该论文针对离线策略强化学习中的外推误差问题，即当学习策略选择重放缓冲区中支持较弱的动作时产生的误差。通过类比静摩擦力，作者将重放缓冲区表示为平滑的低维动作流形，其中支持方向对应切向分量，外推误差对应法向分量，揭示了价值敏感性的内在各向异性，并自然导出一个类似摩擦阈值的稳定性条件。他们提出了摩擦Q学习算法，利用对比变分自编码器将支持动作编码为切向方向，并在局部等距假设下使用正交补空间的正交基表示法向分量。在标准连续控制基准上的实验结果表明，与基线相比，该算法具有鲁棒且稳定的性能。
Segment-Aligned Policy Optimization for Multi-Modal Reasoning
Authors: Lei Gao, Zhuoming Li, Mengxi Jia, Jiakang Yuan, Hongbo Sun, Hao Sun, Xuelong Li
First: 2026-05-02T08:47:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T08:09:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Existing reinforcement learning approaches for Large Language Models typically perform policy optimization at the granularity of individual tokens or entire response sequences. However, such formulations often misalign with the natural step-wise structure of reasoning processes, leading to suboptimal credit assignment and unstable training in multi-modal reasoning tasks. To bridge this gap, we propose Segment-Aligned Policy Optimization (SAPO), a novel reinforcement learning paradigm that treats coherent reasoning steps, rather than tokens or full sequences as fundamental units of policy update. SAPO introduces a step-wise Markov decision process abstraction over reasoning segments, accompanied by segment-level value estimation, advantage computation, and importance sampling mechanisms that are semantically aligned with reasoning boundaries. Experiments on representative reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that SAPO consistently outperforms token-level and sequence-level policy optimization methods, achieving significant accuracy improvements while exhibiting better training stability and value estimation consistency. Our work underscores the importance of aligning reinforcement learning updates with the intrinsic structure of reasoning, paving the way for more efficient and semantically grounded policy optimization in complex reasoning tasks. Codes and models will be released to ensure full reproducibility.
Summary / 总结
Existing reinforcement learning methods for large language models often perform policy optimization at the token or full-sequence level, which misaligns with the natural step-wise structure of reasoning in multi-modal tasks, leading to suboptimal credit assignment and unstable training. To address this, the authors propose Segment-Aligned Policy Optimization (SAPO), a novel paradigm that treats coherent reasoning steps as fundamental units for policy updates, incorporating step-wise Markov decision process abstraction, segment-level value estimation, advantage computation, and importance sampling. Experiments on representative reasoning benchmarks show that SAPO consistently outperforms token-level and sequence-level methods, achieving significant accuracy improvements with better training stability and value estimation consistency.
现有的针对大语言模型的强化学习方法通常在单个token或整个回复序列的粒度上进行策略优化，这与多模态推理任务中自然的逐步推理结构不匹配，导致信用分配不佳和训练不稳定。为解决这一问题，作者提出了段对齐策略优化（SAPO），这是一种新颖的强化学习范式，将连贯的推理步骤而非token或完整序列作为策略更新的基本单元，并引入了基于推理步骤的马尔可夫决策过程抽象、段级价值估计、优势计算和重要性采样机制。在代表性推理基准上的实验表明，SAPO始终优于token级和序列级的策略优化方法，在实现显著准确率提升的同时，展现出更好的训练稳定性和价值估计一致性。
AGPO: Asymmetric Group Policy Optimization for Verifiable Reasoning and Search Ads Relevance at JD
Authors: Yang Xu, Kun Yao, Yiming Deng, Zheng Fang, Kai Ming Ting, Ming Pang
First: 2026-05-07T08:00:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T08:00:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has demonstrated notable success in enhancing the reasoning performance of large language models (LLMs). However, recent studies reveal that while current RLVR methods improve sampling efficiency towards correct paths, they do not elicit fundamentally new reasoning patterns. Instead, the reasoning capability boundary of trained models often narrows compared to their base models, with base models achieving higher coverage at large sample sizes. In this work, we propose Asymmetric Group Policy Optimization (AGPO) to counteract this boundary shrinkage. AGPO adopts a negative-dominant reinforcement strategy to suppress incorrect reasoning paths, maintaining the base model's exploration capacity. For positive reinforcement, AGPO adopts a group advantage mechanism, which scales positive updates based on intra-group variance, allowing the model to focus on rare correct paths while suppressing updates from trivial paths. Our experiments on five mathematical benchmarks demonstrate that AGPO achieves state-of-the-art accuracy while consistently improving pass@$k$ performance at scale. In a large-scale industrial application for search ads relevance optimization, AGPO effectively enhances the quality of the data annotation, leading to substantial performance gains in downstream student models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AGPO：面向京东可验证推理与搜索广告相关性的非对称组策略优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在提升大语言模型（LLMs）推理性能方面已取得显著成功。然而，近期研究表明，当前RLVR方法虽能提高正确路径的采样效率，但并未激发根本性的新推理模式。相反，训练后模型的推理能力边界往往较基础模型收窄——在大样本量下，基础模型反而能实现更高的覆盖率。为应对这一边界收缩问题，本文提出非对称组策略优化（AGPO）。AGPO采用负向主导的强化策略抑制错误推理路径，从而保持基础模型的探索能力；在正向强化方面，AGPO引入组优势机制，根据组内方差缩放正向更新幅度，使模型聚焦于稀有正确路径，同时抑制平凡路径的更新。在五个数学基准上的实验表明，AGPO在实现最先进准确率的同时，持续提升大规模采样下的pass@$k$性能。在搜索广告相关性优化这一大规模工业应用中，AGPO有效提升了数据标注质量，进而为下游学生模型带来显著的性能增益。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Asymmetric Group Policy Optimization (AGPO) to address the issue of reasoning capability boundary shrinkage observed in existing Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods for large language models. AGPO employs a negative-dominant reinforcement strategy to suppress incorrect reasoning paths while preserving the base model's exploration capacity, and a group advantage mechanism for positive reinforcement that scales updates based on intra-group variance to focus on rare correct paths. Experiments on five mathematical benchmarks show that AGPO achieves state-of-the-art accuracy and consistently improves pass@k performance at scale, and in a large-scale industrial application for search ads relevance at JD, it enhances data annotation quality and downstream student model performance.
本文提出非对称组策略优化（AGPO）以解决现有基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法导致大语言模型推理能力边界收缩的问题。AGPO采用负向主导的强化策略抑制错误推理路径，同时保持基模型的探索能力，并通过组优势机制进行正向强化，根据组内方差缩放更新以聚焦于稀有正确路径。在五个数学基准上的实验表明，AGPO达到了最先进的准确率，并持续提升大规模下的pass@k性能；在京东搜索广告相关性优化的工业应用中，它有效提高了数据标注质量，并显著提升了下游学生模型的性能。
Long-Horizon Q-Learning: Accurate Value Learning via n-Step Inequalities
Authors: Armaan A. Abraham, Lucy Xiaoyang Shi, Chelsea Finn
First: 2026-05-07T07:47:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T07:47:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Off-policy, value-based reinforcement learning methods such as Q-learning are appealing because they can learn from arbitrary experience, including data collected by older policies or other agents. In practice, however, bootstrapping makes long-horizon learning brittle: estimation errors at later states propagate backward through temporal-difference (TD) updates and can compound over time. We propose long-horizon Q-learning (LQL), which introduces a principled backstop against compounding error when learning the optimal action-value function. LQL builds on a prior optimality tightening observation: any realized action sequence lower-bounds what the optimal policy can achieve in expectation, so acting optimally earlier should not be worse than following the observed actions for several steps before switching to optimal behavior. Our contribution is to turn this inequality into a practical stabilization mechanism for Q-learning by using a hinge loss to penalize violations of these bounds. Importantly, LQL computes these penalties using network outputs already produced for the TD error, requiring no auxiliary networks and no additional forward passes relative to Q-learning. When combined with multiple state-of-the-art methods on a range of online and offline-to-online benchmarks, LQL consistently outperforms both 1-step TD and n-step TD learning at similar runtime.
中文标题/摘要
标题：长视界Q学习：通过n步不等式实现精确值学习
离策略、基于值的强化学习方法（如Q学习）因其能够从任意经验（包括旧策略或其他智能体收集的数据）中学习而具有吸引力。然而，在实践中，自举法使得长视界学习变得脆弱：后期状态的估计误差通过时序差分更新向后传播，并可能随时间累积。我们提出长视界Q学习（LQL），它在学习最优动作值函数时引入了一种针对累积误差的原则性防御机制。LQL基于先前的最优性收紧观察：任何实际动作序列在期望上都是最优策略所能达到的下界，因此早期采取最优动作不应比跟随观察到的动作执行若干步后再切换至最优行为更差。我们的贡献在于通过使用铰链损失来惩罚这些界限的违反，从而将这一不等式转化为Q学习的实用稳定机制。重要的是，LQL利用已为TD误差生成的网络输出来计算这些惩罚，无需辅助网络，也无需相对于Q学习进行额外的前向传播。当与多种最先进方法结合应用于一系列在线和离线到在线基准测试时，LQL在相似运行时间下始终优于1步TD和n步TD学习。
Reward Shaping and Action Masking for Compositional Tasks using Behavior Trees and LLMs
Authors: Nicholas Potteiger, Ankita Samaddar, Taylor T. Johnson, Xenofon Koutsoukos
First: 2026-05-07T07:33:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T07:33:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Decomposing complex tasks into a sequence of simpler subtasks can improve learning efficiency for an autonomous agent. Reinforcement learning (RL) can be used to optimize agent policies to complete subtasks, but requires well-defined subtask rewards and benefits from action masking. Recent work uses large language models (LLMs) to automate reward shaping and action masking, however none of them fully address reactivity to subtask failure and modularity to varying objects for compositional tasks. To overcome these challenges, we develop masking reward behavior tree (MRBT), a symbolic structure used as a reactive and modular reward and action mask function. We design an MRBT template and derive logical specifications to construct and verify MRBTs for a sequence of object-interaction subtasks. Further, we develop an automated pipeline that uses an LLM to generate MRBTs robust to varying task objects, an SMT-solver to verify correctness of specifications, and a neurosymbolic RL loop to train agents on compositional tasks. Experiments demonstrate successful generation and refinement of five MRBTs, consistently improving training efficiency and task success rates over baselines and MRBTs without action masking. We further highlight three advantages of MRBTs: transferability, modularity, and verifiability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于行为树与大语言模型的组合任务奖励塑形与动作掩码
将复杂任务分解为一系列更简单的子任务可提升自主智能体的学习效率。强化学习可用于优化智能体策略以完成子任务，但需要明确定义的子任务奖励，并受益于动作掩码。近期研究利用大语言模型自动化奖励塑形与动作掩码，但均未充分解决组合任务中对子任务失败的响应性及针对不同对象的模块化问题。为克服这些挑战，我们提出掩码奖励行为树——一种作为响应式模块化奖励与动作掩码函数的符号结构。我们设计了MRBT模板并推导逻辑规范，以构建和验证面向对象交互子任务序列的MRBT。进一步开发自动化流水线：利用大语言模型生成对任务对象鲁棒的MRBT，通过SMT求解器验证规范正确性，并采用神经符号强化学习循环训练智能体完成组合任务。实验成功生成并优化了五个MRBT，相较于基线及无动作掩码的MRBT，持续提升了训练效率与任务成功率。我们进一步强调MRBT的三大优势：可迁移性、模块化与可验证性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of improving reinforcement learning efficiency for compositional tasks by automating reward shaping and action masking, while overcoming issues of reactivity to subtask failure and modularity with varying objects. The authors propose the masking reward behavior tree (MRBT), a symbolic structure that serves as a reactive and modular reward and action mask function, designed using an MRBT template and logical specifications. An automated pipeline leverages large language models to generate MRBTs robust to varying task objects, an SMT-solver to verify correctness, and a neurosymbolic RL loop for training. Experiments on five MRBTs show consistent improvements in training efficiency and task success rates over baselines, with additional benefits of transferability, modularity, and verifiability.
该论文针对组合任务中强化学习效率提升的挑战，通过自动化奖励塑形和动作掩码，同时解决子任务失败的响应性和不同对象的模块化问题。作者提出了掩码奖励行为树（MRBT），这是一种符号化结构，可作为响应式和模块化的奖励与动作掩码函数，并基于MRBT模板和逻辑规范进行设计。自动化流程利用大语言模型生成适应不同任务对象的MRBT，使用SMT求解器验证规范正确性，并通过神经符号强化学习循环进行训练。在五个MRBT上的实验表明，与基线相比，训练效率和任务成功率持续提升，并具有可迁移性、模块化和可验证性等额外优势。
A Measure-Theoretic Finite-Sample Theory for Adaptive-Data Fitted Q-Iteration
Authors: Manuel Haussmann, Mustafa Mert Çelikok, Melih Kandemir
First: 2026-05-07T07:26:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T07:26:58+00:00
Comments: preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While reinforcement learning (RL) promises to revolutionize the control of complex nonlinear robotic systems, a profound gap persists between the heuristic success of model-free off-policy deep RL and the underlying theory, which remains largely confined to tabular or linearizable settings. We identify the cause of this gap as an emergent isolation of three traditions: (i) measure-theoretic MDP foundations on general spaces limit their analysis to exact dynamic programming and ignore all error sources of a learning process; (ii) deterministic error propagation analysis addresses the approximation error via concentrability coefficients without a finite-sample analysis of the estimation error; and (iii) PAC generalization bounds characterize the estimation errors of simplified topologies. We bridge these traditions with a unified theoretical framework for fitted Q-iteration (FQI) on general measurable Borel spaces. Our main result provides a finite-sample, adaptive-data performance bound by chaining measure-theoretic probability with Bellman-operator contraction in Banach spaces. We prove that sequential Rademacher complexity controls Bellman-regression generalization under policy-dependent data collection. We further extend this analysis to provide the first cumulative, pathwise online regret guarantee for FQI in continuous spaces. These results lay the necessary foundations for the formal analysis of many modern deep RL algorithms.

标题：自适应数据拟合Q迭代的测度论有限样本理论
尽管强化学习有望彻底改变复杂非线性机器人系统的控制，但模型无关离策略深度RL的经验成功与其理论基础之间存在深刻鸿沟，后者仍主要局限于表格或可线性化场景。我们识别出这一鸿沟源于三种传统的孤立：（i）一般空间上的测度论MDP基础将其分析限制在精确动态规划，忽略了学习过程中的所有误差来源；（ii）确定性误差传播分析通过集中性系数处理近似误差，但缺乏对估计误差的有限样本分析；（iii）PAC泛化界刻画了简化拓扑的估计误差。我们通过一个统一的拟合Q迭代理论框架，在一般可测Borel空间上桥接了这些传统。我们的主要结果通过将测度论概率与Banach空间中的Bellman算子收缩相结合，提供了有限样本、自适应数据的性能界。我们证明序列Rademacher复杂度在策略依赖数据收集下控制Bellman回归泛化。我们进一步扩展这一分析，首次为连续空间中的FQI提供了累积的、路径依赖的在线遗憾保证。这些结果为许多现代深度RL算法的形式化分析奠定了必要基础。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the gap between heuristic success of model-free off-policy deep RL and its theoretical foundations, which are limited to tabular or linear settings. The analysis is extended to provide the first cumulative, pathwise online regret guarantee for FQI in continuous spaces, laying foundations for analyzing modern deep RL algorithms. Experimental results are not explicitly reported in this theoretical paper, but the framework is validated through rigorous mathematical proofs.

Sample-efficient LLM Optimization with Reset Replay
Authors: Zichuan Liu, Jinyu Wang, Lei Song, Jiang Bian
First: 2025-08-08T15:56:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T07:25:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advancements in LLM post-training, particularly through reinforcement learning and preference optimization, are key to boosting their reasoning capabilities. However, these methods often suffer from low sample efficiency and a susceptibility to primacy bias, a phenomenon where overfitting to initial experiences diminishes network plasticity and damages the learning process. To address these challenges, we introduce LLM optimization with Reset Replay (LoRR), a general and powerful plugin for enhancing sample efficiency in preference-based optimization. Its core mechanism enables high-replay training to maximize the utility of each data batch. To mitigate overfitting, LoRR orchestrates a periodic reset strategy that reuses the initial data and policy to maintain network plasticity, and further adopts a hybrid optimization objective to better exploit training data. Extensive experiments show that LoRR significantly boosts the performance of various preference optimization methods on both mathematical and general reasoning benchmarks. Notably, an iterative DPO framework augmented with LoRR achieves comparable performance on challenging math tasks, rivaling many complex or computationally expensive baselines. Our findings highlight that LoRR offers a practical and sample-efficient paradigm from limited offline data, unlocking greater performance with minimal changes to existing post-training workflows.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于重置回放的样本高效大语言模型优化

Discovering What You Can Control: Interventional Boundary Discovery for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jiaxin Liu, Anzhe Cheng, Paul Bogdan
First: 2026-03-18T20:26:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T07:22:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
When an RL agent's observations contain distractors driven by the same confounders as its true state, observational data alone cannot identify which dimensions the agent controls. In our benchmarks, even state-conditioned observational selectors can collapse when distractors mimic controllable state variables. We propose Interventional Boundary Discovery (IBD), which treats the agent's own action channel as a source of randomized interventions: randomizing actions implements an interventional contrast, and per-dimension two-sample tests with FDR correction produce a binary mask over observation dimensions. Across 12 continuous-control settings with up to 100 distractors, IBD matches oracle return in 11 of 12 settings, while observational baselines including mutual information, state-conditioned forward models, and gradient-based sensitivity often underperform simply passing the full observation to SAC.
中文标题/摘要
标题：发现可控因素：强化学习中的干预边界发现
当强化学习智能体的观测中包含与真实状态受相同混杂因素驱动的干扰项时，仅凭观测数据无法识别智能体控制哪些维度。在我们的基准测试中，即使基于状态条件的观测选择器在干扰项模仿可控状态变量时也可能失效。我们提出干预边界发现方法，将智能体自身的动作通道视为随机化干预源：随机化动作实现干预对比，通过带FDR校正的逐维双样本检验生成观测维度的二值掩码。在包含多达100个干扰项的12个连续控制场景中，IBD在11个场景中达到与理想回报相当的性能，而基于互信息、状态条件前向模型和梯度敏感性的观测基线方法往往不如直接将完整观测输入SAC算法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of reinforcement learning agents identifying controllable dimensions in observations when distractors are confounded with the true state, as observational methods fail under such conditions. The authors propose Interventional Boundary Discovery (IBD), which uses the agent's own actions as randomized interventions, applying per-dimension two-sample tests with FDR correction to produce a binary mask over observation dimensions. In experiments across 12 continuous-control settings with up to 100 distractors, IBD matches oracle return in 11 of 12 settings, outperforming observational baselines like mutual information and state-conditioned forward models.
该论文针对强化学习智能体在观测中存在与真实状态共享混杂因素的干扰物时，无法通过观测数据识别可控维度的问题。作者提出干预边界发现方法，将智能体自身的动作通道作为随机干预源，通过每维度的双样本检验和FDR校正生成观测维度的二值掩码。在12个包含多达100个干扰物的连续控制实验中，该方法在11个设置中达到与理想情况相当的回报，优于互信息、状态条件前向模型等观测基线方法。
Leveraging Analytic Gradients in Provably Safe Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tim Walter, Hannah Markgraf, Jonathan Külz, Matthias Althoff
Venue: IEEE Open Journal of Control Systems, vol. 4, pp. 463-481, 2025
First: 2025-06-02T13:35:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T07:15:27+00:00
Comments: 21 pages, 10 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The deployment of autonomous robots in safety-critical applications requires safety guarantees. Provably safe reinforcement learning is an active field of research that aims to provide such guarantees using safeguards. These safeguards should be integrated during training to reduce the sim-to-real gap. While there are several approaches for safeguarding sampling-based reinforcement learning, analytic gradient-based reinforcement learning often achieves superior performance from fewer environment interactions. However, there is no safeguarding approach for this learning paradigm yet. Our work addresses this gap by developing the first effective safeguard for analytic gradient-based reinforcement learning. We analyse existing, differentiable safeguards, adapt them through modified mappings and gradient formulations, and integrate them into a state-of-the-art learning algorithm and a differentiable simulation. Using numerical experiments on three control tasks, we evaluate how different safeguards affect learning. The results demonstrate safeguarded training without compromising performance. Additional visuals are provided at timwalter.github.io/safe-agb-rl.github.io.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在可证明安全的强化学习中利用解析梯度
在安全关键应用中部署自主机器人需要安全保证。可证明安全的强化学习是一个活跃的研究领域，旨在通过安全防护措施提供此类保证。这些防护措施应在训练期间集成，以减少模拟到现实的差距。尽管有几种方法用于保护基于采样的强化学习，但基于解析梯度的强化学习通常能从更少的环境交互中实现更优性能。然而，目前尚无针对这种学习范式的防护方法。我们的工作通过开发首个针对基于解析梯度的强化学习的有效防护措施来填补这一空白。我们分析了现有的可微分防护措施，通过修改映射和梯度公式对其进行调整，并将其集成到最先进的学习算法和可微分仿真中。通过在三个控制任务上进行数值实验，我们评估了不同防护措施对学习的影响。结果表明，防护训练在不影响性能的情况下得以实现。更多可视化内容请见timwalter.github.io/safe-agb-rl.github.io。

This paper addresses the lack of safeguarding methods for analytic gradient-based reinforcement learning, which is crucial for safety-critical autonomous robot deployment. The authors develop the first effective safeguard for this paradigm by analyzing existing differentiable safeguards, adapting them through modified mappings and gradient formulations, and integrating them into a state-of-the-art learning algorithm with differentiable simulation. Experimental results on three control tasks demonstrate that safeguarded training is achieved without compromising performance, effectively bridging the sim-to-real gap.
该论文针对分析梯度强化学习中缺乏安全防护方法的问题，这对于安全关键型自主机器人部署至关重要。作者通过分析现有的可微分安全防护机制，利用改进的映射和梯度公式进行适配，并将其集成到最先进的学习算法和可微分仿真中，开发了首个针对该范式的有效安全防护方法。在三个控制任务上的实验结果表明，安全防护训练在不影响性能的前提下得以实现，有效缩小了仿真与现实的差距。
Confidence is the key: how conformal prediction enhances the generative design of permeable peptides
Authors: Laura van Weesep, Sunay Chankeshwara, Leonardo De Maria, Florian David, Ola Engkvist, Gökçe Geylan
First: 2026-05-07T07:01:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T07:01:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative models coupled with reinforcement learning (RL), such as REINVENT and PepINVENT, have emerged as a powerful framework for de novo molecular design. During the ideation process these generative frameworks utilize various predictive models as part of the optimization objectives. However, the utility of the predictive models can be limited by their domain of applicability. When RL is used to explore the chemical space with predictive models, it can suggest molecules that lie outside the predictor's domain of applicability. As a result, the predictions may become less reliable, potentially steering designs into high reward but also high uncertainty chemical spaces. This is particularly pronounced for cyclic peptides which show therapeutic promise due to their modifiability and large interaction surfaces but are understudied compared to small molecules. While passive membrane permeation in cyclic peptides has attracted interest, identifying optimal permeable designs remains challenging yet crucial for targeting intracellular sites. We present an RL-guided generative framework that designs permeable cyclic peptides using an uncertainty-aware permeability predictor as the scoring component. To address predictive uncertainty, especially impacted by novel chemistry, we integrate conformal prediction (CP) as our uncertainty quantification method. CP assesses designs based on the calibrated model under a user-defined confidence level. We demonstrate that rewarding generated peptides with CP-informed predictions improves both reliability and efficiency of peptide optimization process. This also discourages exploration outside the predictor's applicability domain. This approach bridges the gap between predictive uncertainty and RL-guided exploration, showing how generative modelling and conformal prediction can be combined for the first time.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of unreliable predictions in reinforcement learning (RL)-guided generative design of permeable cyclic peptides, where RL exploration often suggests molecules outside the predictor's domain of applicability, leading to high-uncertainty chemical spaces. The authors propose integrating conformal prediction (CP) as an uncertainty quantification method into the RL framework, using a CP-informed permeability predictor to score generated peptides under a user-defined confidence level. Experimental results demonstrate that rewarding peptides with CP-informed predictions improves both the reliability and efficiency of the optimization process, effectively discouraging exploration beyond the predictor's applicability domain and marking the first combination of generative modeling with conformal prediction for molecular design.
该论文针对强化学习引导的渗透性环肽生成设计中预测不可靠的问题，即强化学习探索常导致分子超出预测器适用范围，进入高不确定性化学空间。作者提出将保形预测作为不确定性量化方法集成到强化学习框架中，利用保形预测校准的渗透性预测器在用户定义置信水平下对生成肽进行评分。实验结果表明，基于保形预测信息奖励生成肽可提高优化过程的可靠性和效率，有效抑制超出预测器适用范围的探索，首次将生成模型与保形预测结合用于分子设计。
Hardware-Aware Neural Feature Extraction for Resource-Constrained Devices
Authors: Francesco Tosini, Simone Pedroni, Christian Veronesi, Pietro Bartoli, Andrea Giudici, Marco Paracchini, Marco Marcon, Diana Trojaniello
Venue: CVPR
First: 2026-05-05T20:32:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T06:59:18+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted for publication at the IEEE Conference on Computer Vision and Pattern Recognition (CVPR) Workshops, 2026. \c{opyright}IEEE
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Visual SLAM is a core component of spatial computing systems, yet deploying learned local feature extractors on microcontroller-class hardware remains challenging due to memory, bandwidth, and quantization constraints. While modern neural descriptors provide strong robustness, their practical adoption is often hindered by system-level bottlenecks that are not captured by FLOP-based efficiency metrics. In this work, we introduce Gideon, a hardware-aware neural feature extractor explicitly designed for resource-constrained devices. Our approach combines relational knowledge distillation from a SuperPoint teacher with differentiable neural architecture search (DNAS) under strict memory and operator constraints. Unlike conventional design pipelines, we treat quantization stability and dynamic-range compactness as first-class objectives. We show that architectural choices such as replacing Batch Normalization with affine layers significantly improve INT8 robustness, and that descriptor dimensionality directly governs quantization resilience. Deployed on STM32N6, Gideon achieves 9.003 ms inference time (111 fps) while remaining below a 1.5 MB memory footprint. Remarkably, INT8 quantization induces negligible degradation and occasionally matches full-precision performance. These results demonstrate that robust learned feature extraction can be reconciled with embedded hardware constraints through holistic hardware-algorithm co-design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向资源受限设备的硬件感知神经特征提取
视觉SLAM是空间计算系统的核心组件，然而，由于内存、带宽和量化约束，在微控制器类硬件上部署学习型局部特征提取器仍然具有挑战性。虽然现代神经描述符提供了强大的鲁棒性，但其实际应用常受限于系统级瓶颈，而这些瓶颈无法通过基于FLOP的效率指标来捕捉。在这项工作中，我们引入了Gideon，一种专为资源受限设备设计的硬件感知神经特征提取器。我们的方法结合了来自SuperPoint教师的关系知识蒸馏与在严格内存和算子约束下的可微神经架构搜索（DNAS）。与传统设计流程不同，我们将量化稳定性和动态范围紧凑性视为首要目标。我们表明，诸如用仿射层替换批归一化等架构选择能显著提升INT8鲁棒性，并且描述符维度直接决定量化弹性。部署在STM32N6上，Gideon实现了9.003毫秒的推理时间（111帧/秒），同时内存占用低于1.5 MB。值得注意的是，INT8量化引起的性能退化可忽略不计，有时甚至与全精度性能相当。这些结果表明，通过整体的硬件-算法协同设计，鲁棒的学习型特征提取可以与嵌入式硬件约束相协调。

Transformers Provably Implement In-Context Reinforcement Learning with Policy Improvement
Authors: Haodong Liang, Lifeng Lai
First: 2026-05-07T06:50:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T06:50:49+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We investigate the ability of transformers to perform in-context reinforcement learning (ICRL), where a model must infer and execute learning algorithms from trajectory data without parameter updates. We show that a linear self-attention transformer block can provably implement policy-improvement methods, including semi-gradient SARSA and actor-critic, via explicit parameter constructions. Beyond existence, we design a teacher-mimicking training procedure, analyze its gradient-flow dynamics, and establish the first convergence guarantee in the ICRL literature: under suitable richness conditions on the training MDP distribution, gradient flow converges locally and exponentially to an optimal parameter manifold corresponding to the desired RL update. Empirically, training transformers on randomly generated tabular MDPs confirms these predictions: the learned models recover the parameter structure of our explicit constructions and, when deployed on unseen MDPs, deliver strong in-context control performance. Together, these results illuminate how transformer architectures internalize and execute classical reinforcement learning algorithms in context, bridging mechanistic understanding and training dynamics in ICRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Transformer可证明地通过策略改进实现上下文强化学习
我们研究了Transformer执行上下文强化学习（ICRL）的能力，即模型必须从轨迹数据中推断并执行学习算法，而无需参数更新。我们证明，通过显式参数构造，线性自注意力Transformer块可以可证明地实现策略改进方法，包括半梯度SARSA和演员-评论家算法。除了存在性证明，我们设计了一种教师模仿训练程序，分析了其梯度流动力学，并建立了ICRL文献中的首个收敛保证：在训练MDP分布满足适当丰富性条件下，梯度流局部且指数级收敛到对应于所需RL更新的最优参数流形。实验上，在随机生成的表格型MDP上训练Transformer证实了这些预测：学习到的模型恢复了我们显式构造的参数结构，并在未见过的MDP上部署时，提供了强大的上下文控制性能。这些结果共同阐明了Transformer架构如何在上下文中内化并执行经典强化学习算法，桥接了ICRL中的机制理解与训练动力学。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates how transformers can perform in-context reinforcement learning (ICRL), where models infer and execute learning algorithms from trajectory data without parameter updates. The authors show that a linear self-attention transformer block can provably implement policy-improvement methods like semi-gradient SARSA and actor-critic through explicit parameter constructions. They design a teacher-mimicking training procedure, analyze its gradient-flow dynamics, and establish the first convergence guarantee in ICRL literature, showing that gradient flow converges locally and exponentially to an optimal parameter manifold under suitable conditions. Empirically, training transformers on randomly generated tabular MDPs confirms these predictions, with learned models recovering the parameter structure of explicit constructions and delivering strong in-context control performance on unseen MDPs.
本文研究了Transformer如何执行上下文强化学习（ICRL），即模型从轨迹数据中推断并执行学习算法而无需参数更新。作者证明，线性自注意力Transformer块可以通过显式参数构造，可靠地实现策略改进方法，如半梯度SARSA和演员-评论家算法。他们设计了一种教师模仿训练程序，分析了其梯度流动力学，并建立了ICRL文献中的首个收敛保证，表明在适当条件下梯度流局部指数收敛到最优参数流形。实验上，在随机生成的表格型MDP上训练Transformer验证了这些预测，学习到的模型恢复了显式构造的参数结构，并在未见过的MDP上展现出强大的上下文控制性能。
Multi-Dimensional Behavioral Evaluation of Agentic Stock Prediction Systems Using LLM Judges with Closed-Loop Reinforcement Learning Feedback
Authors: Mohammad Al Ridhawi, Mahtab Haj Ali, Hussein Al Osman
First: 2026-05-07T06:31:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T06:31:34+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 2 figures, 8 tables. Short Communication submitted to Knowledge-Based Systems (Elsevier)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Agentic stock prediction systems make sequences of interdependent decisions (regime detection, pathway routing, reinforcement learning control) whose individual quality is hidden by aggregate metrics such as mean absolute percentage error (MAPE) or directional accuracy. We present a behavioral evaluation framework that addresses this gap. Behavioral traces logged at every autonomous decision point are grouped into five-day episodes and scored along six domain-specific dimensions (regime detection, routing, adaptation, risk calibration, strategy coherence, error recovery) by an ensemble of three large language model (LLM) judges (GPT 5.4, Claude 4.6 Opus, Gemini 3.1 Pro). Perturbation-based validation on 420 episodes yields targeted score drops of $-1.6$ to $-2.4$ on intended dimensions versus an average of $-0.32$ on the remaining five, with cross-model agreement up to Krippendorff's $α= 0.85$. The composite behavioral score, used here only for cross-episode reporting, correlates at $ρ= 0.72$ with realized 20-day Sharpe ratio from offline backtesting. Closing the loop, the framework converts deficient per-dimension scores into a credit-assigned penalty term added to the Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) reward. Three short fine-tuning cycles, all confined to the validation period, produce on the held-out 2017-2025 test period a one-day MAPE reduction from 0.61% to 0.54% (an 11.5% relative reduction; $p<0.001$, Cohen's $d=0.31$), a directional accuracy increase from 71% to 74%, and an 18% Sharpe ratio improvement (95% bootstrap CI [8.2%, 27.4%]), with gains concentrated in high-volatility episodes where the original system was most behaviorally deficient. Results are from offline backtesting and do not address effects specific to live deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型裁判与闭环强化学习反馈的智能股票预测系统多维度行为评估
智能股票预测系统会做出相互依赖的序列决策（状态检测、路径选择、强化学习控制），其个体质量被平均绝对百分比误差（MAPE）或方向准确率等聚合指标所掩盖。我们提出了一种行为评估框架来解决这一问题。在每个自主决策点记录的行为轨迹被分组为五天一个的片段，并由三个大语言模型（LLM）裁判（GPT 5.4、Claude 4.6 Opus、Gemini 3.1 Pro）组成的集成系统，按照六个特定领域维度（状态检测、路径选择、自适应、风险校准、策略一致性、错误恢复）进行评分。基于420个片段的扰动验证显示，目标维度的得分下降范围为-1.6至-2.4，而其余五个维度的平均下降为-0.32，跨模型一致性达到Krippendorff's α=0.85。复合行为得分（此处仅用于跨片段报告）与离线回测中实现的20天夏普比率的相关性为ρ=0.72。在闭环中，该框架将每个维度的不足得分转化为信用分配的惩罚项，添加到软演员-评论家（SAC）奖励中。三个简短的微调周期（均限于验证期内）在保留的2017-2025年测试期内，将一日MAPE从0.61%降至0.54%（相对降低11.5%；p<0.001，Cohen's d=0.31），方向准确率从71%提升至74%，夏普比率提高18%（95%自助法置信区间[8.2%, 27.4%]），收益集中在原始系统行为缺陷最严重的高波动片段。结果来自离线回测，未涉及实时部署特有的影响。
