Closing the Loop: Unified 3D Scene Generation and Immersive Interaction via LLM-RL Coupling
Authors: Anh H. Vo, Sungyo Lee, Phil-Joong Kim, Soo-Mi Choi, Yong-Guk Kim
First: 2026-05-07T05:55:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T05:55:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have significantly improved language-driven 3D content generation, but most existing approaches still treat scene generation and user interaction as separate processes, limiting the adaptability and immersive potential of interactive multimedia systems. This paper presents a unified framework that closes the loop between language-driven 3D scene generation and immersive user interaction. Given natural language instructions, the system first constructs structured scene representations using LLMs, and then optimizes spatial layouts via reinforcement learning under geometric and semantic constraints. The generated environments are deployed in a virtual reality setting to facilitate HRI-in-the-loop, where user interactions provide continuous feedback to align generated content with human perception and usability. By tightly coupling generation and interaction, the proposed framework enables more responsive, adaptive, and realistic multimedia experiences. Experiments on the ALFRED benchmark demonstrate state-of-the-art performance in task-based scene generation. Furthermore, qualitative results and user studies show consistent improvements in immersion, interaction quality, and task efficiency, highlighting the importance of closed-loop integration of generation and interaction for next-generation multimedia systems. Our project page can be found at https://proj-showcase.github.io/h3ds/.

Generalised Linear Models in Deep Bayesian RL with Learnable Basis Functions
Authors: Jingyang You, Hanna Kurniawati
First: 2025-12-24T06:00:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T05:25:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian Reinforcement Learning (BRL), a subclass of Meta-Reinforcement Learning (Meta-RL), provides a principled framework for generalisation by explicitly incorporating Bayesian task parameters into transition and reward models. However, classical BRL methods assume known forms of transition and reward models. While recent deep BRL methods incorporate model learning to address this, applying neural networks directly to joint data and task parameters necessitates variational inference. This often yields indistinct task representations, compromising the resulting BRL policies. To overcome these limitations, we introduce Generalised Linear Models in Deep Bayesian RL with Learnable Basis Functions (GLiBRL). Our approach features fully tractable Bayesian inference over task parameters and model noise, alongside exact marginal likelihood evaluation for learning transition and reward models. The permutation-invariant nature of exact Bayesian inference in GLiBRL enables seamless integration with both on-policy and off-policy RL algorithms. We further show that GLiBRL admits a closed-form relationship between the $\mathcal{L}_2$ distance of its task representations and empirical kernel-based correspondence between task samples, which is to our knowledge the first such structural result for online deep BRL. GLiBRL is compared against representative and recent Meta-RL methods, and improves state-of-the-art performance on both MuJoCo and MetaWorld benchmarks by up to 1.8$\times$.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses limitations in deep Bayesian Reinforcement Learning (BRL), where variational inference often leads to indistinct task representations and poor policy generalization. The authors propose GLiBRL, which uses Generalised Linear Models with learnable basis functions to achieve fully tractable Bayesian inference over task parameters and model noise, along with exact marginal likelihood evaluation for learning transition and reward models. This permutation-invariant approach integrates seamlessly with both on-policy and off-policy RL algorithms. Experiments on MuJoCo and MetaWorld benchmarks show that GLiBRL improves state-of-the-art performance by up to 1.8 times, and it also provides a novel closed-form relationship between task representation distances and empirical kernel-based correspondence.
该论文针对深度贝叶斯强化学习（BRL）中变分推断导致任务表征模糊、策略泛化能力不足的问题，提出了GLiBRL方法。该方法通过可学习基函数的广义线性模型，实现了对任务参数和模型噪声的完全可处理贝叶斯推断，并利用精确边际似然评估来学习转移和奖励模型。其置换不变性使其能无缝集成到同策略和异策略强化学习算法中。在MuJoCo和MetaWorld基准测试上的实验表明，GLiBRL将最先进性能提升了最多1.8倍，并首次建立了任务表征的L2距离与经验核对应之间的闭式关系。
Adapt to Thrive! Adaptive Power-Mean Policy Optimization for Improved LLM Reasoning
Authors: Yiming Huang, Zhenbo Shi, Shuzheng Gao, Cuiyun Gao, Peiyi Han, Chuanyi Liu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-11T07:34:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T04:57:40+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ACL 2026 (Findings)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) is an essential paradigm that enhances the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, existing methods typically rely on static policy optimization schemes that misalign with the model's evolving reasoning capabilities. To address this issue, we propose Adaptive Power-Mean Policy Optimization (APMPO), which comprises two main innovations: Power-Mean Policy Optimization (PMPO) and Feedback-Adaptive Clipping (FAC). Specifically, PMPO introduces a generalized power-mean objective. This enables the model to adaptively transition from the signal-amplifying behavior of the arithmetic mean to the consistency-enforcing behavior of the geometric mean. FAC adaptively adjusts clipping bounds based on real-time reward statistics to overcome the limitations of static mechanisms. Capitalizing on these innovations, APMPO improves learning dynamics and reasoning performance. Extensive experiments on nine datasets across three reasoning tasks showcase the superiority of APMPO over state-of-the-art RLVR-based baselines. For instance, APMPO boosts the average Pass@1 score on mathematical reasoning benchmarks by 3.0 points compared to GRPO when using Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct.
中文标题/摘要
标题：适应以求发展！自适应幂均值策略优化提升大语言模型推理能力
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）是增强大语言模型（LLM）推理能力的关键范式。然而，现有方法通常依赖静态策略优化方案，与模型不断演化的推理能力不匹配。为解决此问题，我们提出自适应幂均值策略优化（APMPO），包含两项主要创新：幂均值策略优化（PMPO）和反馈自适应裁剪（FAC）。具体而言，PMPO引入广义幂均值目标，使模型能够从算术均值的信号放大行为自适应过渡到几何均值的连贯性强化行为。FAC根据实时奖励统计动态调整裁剪边界，以克服静态机制的局限性。借助这些创新，APMPO改善了学习动态和推理性能。在三个推理任务的九个数据集上的大量实验表明，APMPO优于基于RLVR的最先进基线方法。例如，在使用Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct时，APMPO在数学推理基准上的平均Pass@1分数相比GRPO提升了3.0个百分点。

Extensive experiments on nine datasets across three reasoning tasks demonstrate that APMPO outperforms state-of-the-art RLVR baselines, achieving a 3.0-point improvement in average Pass@1 score on mathematical reasoning benchmarks compared to GRPO when using Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct.

Free Energy-Driven Reinforcement Learning with Adaptive Advantage Shaping for Unsupervised Reasoning in LLMs
Authors: Yiming Huang, Zhenbo Shi, Xin-Cheng Wen, Jichuan Zeng, Cuiyun Gao, Peiyi Han, Chuanyi Liu
Venue: ACL 2026
First: 2026-04-11T07:26:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T04:49:30+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ACL 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unsupervised reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for enabling self-improvement in large language models (LLMs). However, existing unsupervised RL-based methods often lack the capacity to adapt to the model's evolving reasoning capabilities during training. Therefore, these methods can misdirect policy optimization in the absence of ground-truth supervision. To address this issue, we introduce FREIA, a novel RL-based algorithm built on two key innovations: (1) Free Energy-Driven Reward (FER) adapts rewards to balance consensus and exploration based on the Free Energy Principle. (2) Adaptive Advantage Shaping (AAS) adaptively adjusts learning signals based on the statistical characteristics of sampled rewards. Empirical evaluations on nine datasets across three reasoning tasks showcase that FREIA outperforms other unsupervised RL-based baselines. Notably, in mathematical reasoning tasks, FREIA surpasses other methods by an average of 0.5 to 3.5 points in Pass@1 using the DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自由能驱动的自适应优势塑形强化学习用于大语言模型无监督推理
无监督强化学习已成为实现大语言模型自我改进的有前景范式。然而，现有基于无监督强化学习的方法往往缺乏适应模型训练过程中不断演化的推理能力的能力。因此，这些方法在缺乏真实监督的情况下可能误导策略优化。为解决此问题，我们提出FREIA，一种基于两个关键创新的新型强化学习算法：(1) 自由能驱动奖励根据自由能原理调整奖励以平衡共识与探索。(2) 自适应优势塑形根据采样奖励的统计特征自适应调整学习信号。在三个推理任务的九个数据集上的实证评估表明，FREIA优于其他基于无监督强化学习的基线方法。值得注意的是，在数学推理任务中，使用DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B模型时，FREIA在Pass@1指标上平均超越其他方法0.5至3.5个百分点。

The paper introduces FREIA, a reinforcement learning algorithm designed to improve unsupervised reasoning in large language models by addressing the issue that existing methods cannot adapt to the model's evolving capabilities, leading to misdirected policy optimization. The method incorporates two key innovations: a Free Energy-Driven Reward that balances consensus and exploration based on the Free Energy Principle, and Adaptive Advantage Shaping that adjusts learning signals according to the statistical characteristics of sampled rewards. Experimental results on nine datasets across three reasoning tasks show that FREIA outperforms other unsupervised RL baselines, particularly in mathematical reasoning where it surpasses other methods by an average of 0.5 to 3.5 points in Pass@1 using the DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B model.
该论文提出了FREIA算法，旨在改进大型语言模型的无监督推理能力，解决现有方法无法适应模型推理能力动态变化而导致策略优化方向错误的问题。该方法包含两个关键创新：基于自由能原理的自适应奖励机制，用于平衡共识与探索；以及自适应优势塑形机制，根据采样奖励的统计特征动态调整学习信号。在九个数据集上的三个推理任务实验表明，FREIA优于其他无监督强化学习基线方法，特别是在数学推理任务中，使用DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B模型时，其Pass@1指标平均领先其他方法0.5至3.5个百分点。
Structured Progressive Knowledge Activation for LLM-Driven Neural Architecture Search
Authors: Zhen Liu, Yuhan Liu, Jinjun Wang, Wei Song, Jianyi Liu, Jingwen Fu
First: 2026-04-10T07:40:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T04:08:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper focuses on a key challenge in Neural Architecture Search (NAS): integrating established architectural knowledge while exploring new designs under expensive evaluations. Large language models (LLMs) are a promising assistant for NAS because they can translate rich architectural and coding priors into executable code edits. However, in practice, seemingly local revisions often propagate into non-local behavioral and performance shifts because a single edit can inadvertently couple multiple interacting functional factors, a phenomenon we refer to as functional entanglement. To make LLM knowledge usable under such entanglement, we propose Structured Progressive Knowledge Activation (SPARK), which activates relevant priors by explicitly selecting the functional factor to modify and conditioning the edit on that factor. This factor-conditioned editing reduces entangled side effects and yields more targeted, reliable architecture modifications. On CLRS-DFS, SPARK achieves a 28.1x sample-efficient architecture evolution speedup and yields a 22.9 percent relative improvement in OOD accuracy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：结构化渐进知识激活：面向大语言模型驱动的神经架构搜索
本文聚焦神经架构搜索（NAS）中的关键挑战：在昂贵评估条件下，如何整合已有架构知识并探索新设计。大语言模型（LLM）因能将丰富的架构与编码先验转化为可执行代码编辑，成为NAS的有力助手。然而实践中，看似局部的修订常引发非局部的行为与性能偏移——单次编辑可能无意耦合多个交互功能因素，我们称之为功能纠缠。为使LLM知识在此类纠缠中可用，我们提出结构化渐进知识激活（SPARK），通过显式选择待修改的功能因素并基于该因素条件化编辑来激活相关先验。这种因素条件化编辑可减少纠缠副作用，实现更精准可靠的架构修改。在CLRS-DFS上，SPARK实现28.1倍样本高效的架构进化加速，并带来22.9%的OOD准确率相对提升。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of integrating established architectural knowledge with new design exploration in Neural Architecture Search (NAS) under expensive evaluations. The authors propose Structured Progressive Knowledge Activation (SPARK), a method that leverages large language models (LLMs) to activate relevant priors by explicitly selecting and conditioning edits on specific functional factors, thereby mitigating functional entanglement where local revisions cause non-local performance shifts. Experimental results on CLRS-DFS demonstrate that SPARK achieves a 28.1x sample-efficient architecture evolution speedup and a 22.9 percent relative improvement in out-of-distribution accuracy.
本文针对神经架构搜索（NAS）中在昂贵评估下整合既有架构知识与探索新设计的关键挑战。作者提出结构化渐进知识激活（SPARK）方法，利用大语言模型（LLM）通过显式选择并基于特定功能因子进行条件编辑来激活相关先验知识，从而缓解局部修改导致非局部性能变化的“功能纠缠”问题。在CLRS-DFS上的实验表明，SPARK实现了28.1倍的样本高效架构进化加速，并带来22.9%的分布外准确率相对提升。
A Forensic Analysis of Synthetic Data in RL: Diagnosing and Solving Algorithmic Failures in Model-Based Policy Optimization
Authors: Brett Barkley, David Fridovich-Keil
First: 2025-10-01T20:54:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T03:46:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Synthetic data is central to data-efficient Dyna-style model-based reinforcement learning, but it can also degrade performance. We study this failure in Model-Based Policy Optimization (MBPO), which performs actor-critic updates using model-generated synthetic state transitions. Although MBPO reports strong sample-efficiency gains on OpenAI Gym, recent work shows that it often underperforms Soft Actor-Critic (SAC), its non-Dyna base, in the DeepMind Control Suite (DMC), despite both suites involving MuJoCo-based proprioceptive continuous control. We identify two coupled causes of this collapse: scale mismatch between dynamics and reward targets, which suppresses reward learning and induces critic underestimation, and residual next-state prediction, which inflates model variance and produces unreliable synthetic transitions. We introduce Fixing That Free Lunch (FTFL), a minimal repair that combines independent target normalization with direct next-state prediction. FTFL outperforms SAC in five of seven previously failing DMC tasks while preserving MBPO's strong Gym performance. We further show that MBPO-lineage algorithms, including uncertainty-aware variants that filter, penalize, or reject synthetic transitions based on model uncertainty, still inherit these failures unless FTFL is applied to their shared learned-model backbone. More broadly, our results show how benchmark-limited evaluation can encode environment-specific assumptions into algorithm design, motivating taxonomies that map MDP structure to algorithmic failure modes.
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates why Model-Based Policy Optimization (MBPO), a Dyna-style reinforcement learning algorithm that uses synthetic data for actor-critic updates, underperforms its model-free counterpart Soft Actor-Critic (SAC) on the DeepMind Control Suite despite strong results on OpenAI Gym. The authors identify two root causes: a scale mismatch between dynamics and reward targets that suppresses reward learning and causes critic underestimation, and residual next-state prediction that inflates model variance and produces unreliable synthetic transitions. To address these issues, they propose Fixing That Free Lunch (FTFL), a minimal repair combining independent target normalization with direct next-state prediction. Experiments show FTFL outperforms SAC on five of seven previously failing DMC tasks while preserving MBPO's strong Gym performance, and that other MBPO-lineage algorithms also benefit from this fix, highlighting how benchmark-specific assumptions can mask algorithmic failures.
本文研究了基于模型的策略优化（MBPO）这一Dyna风格强化学习算法，该算法使用合成数据进行演员-评论家更新，但在DeepMind Control Suite上表现不如其无模型对应算法SAC，尽管在OpenAI Gym上取得了优异结果。作者识别出两个根本原因：动态模型与奖励目标之间的尺度不匹配抑制了奖励学习并导致评论家低估，以及残差下一状态预测增加了模型方差并产生不可靠的合成转换。为解决这些问题，他们提出了Fixing That Free Lunch（FTFL），一种结合独立目标归一化与直接下一状态预测的最小修复方案。实验表明，FTFL在七个先前失败的DMC任务中的五个上优于SAC，同时保持了MBPO在Gym上的强劲表现，并且其他MBPO系列算法也受益于此修复，揭示了基准测试的特定假设如何掩盖算法缺陷。
When2Speak: A Dataset for Temporal Participation and Turn-Taking in Multi-Party Conversations for Large Language Models
Authors: Vihaan Nama, Shreya Mendi, Zian Ye, Brinnae Bent
First: 2026-05-07T03:27:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T03:27:45+00:00
Comments: Currently under review. Dataset can be found: https://huggingface.co/datasets/duke-trust-lab/When2Speak
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) excel at generating contextually appropriate responses but remain poorly calibrated for multi-party conversations, where deciding when to speak is as critical as what to say. In such settings, naively responding at every turn leads to excessive interruptions and degraded conversational coherence. We introduce When2Speak, a grounded synthetic dataset and four-stage generation pipeline for learning intervention timing in group interactions. The dataset comprises over 215,000 examples derived from 16,000 conversations involving 2-6 speakers, spanning diverse conversational styles, tones, and participant dynamics, and explicitly modeling SPEAK vs. SILENT decisions at each turn. Our pipeline combines real-world grounding, structured augmentation, controlled transcript synthesis, and fine-tuning-ready supervision, and is fully open-sourced to support reproducibility and adaptation to domain-specific conversational norms. Across multiple model families, supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on When2Speak significantly outperforms zero-shot baselines (e.g., the average Macro F1 increase across 4B+ parameter models was 60%, with the largest increase being 120%). However, SFT-trained models remain systematically over-conservative, missing nearly half of warranted interventions as seen through the Missed Intervention Rate (MIR), which was on average 0.50 and is noticed even at larger model sizes. To address this limitation, we apply reinforcement learning with asymmetric reward shaping, which reduces MIR to 0.186-0.218 and increases recall from 0.479 to 0.78-0.81. Our findings establish that temporal participation is a distinct and trainable dimension of conversational intelligence, and that grounded synthetic data provides an effective and scalable pathway for enabling LLMs to participate more naturally and appropriately in multi-party interactions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：When2Speak：面向大语言模型的多方对话中时间参与和话轮转换数据集
大语言模型（LLM）擅长生成上下文恰当的回复，但在多方对话中校准不佳——此时决定何时发言与说什么同样关键。在这种场景下，每轮都贸然回应会导致过度打断和对话连贯性下降。我们提出When2Speak，一个基于真实场景的合成数据集及四阶段生成流程，用于学习群体互动中的干预时机。该数据集包含来自16000段对话的超过21.5万个样本，涉及2-6位说话者，涵盖多样的对话风格、语气和参与者动态，并明确建模每轮的发言（SPEAK）与沉默（SILENT）决策。我们的流程结合了真实场景基础、结构化增强、受控转录合成以及可微调监督，并完全开源以支持可复现性和对特定领域对话规范的适配。在多个模型家族中，基于When2Speak的有监督微调（SFT）显著优于零样本基线（例如，4B+参数模型的平均Macro F1提升60%，最大提升达120%）。然而，SFT训练模型仍系统性过于保守，通过遗漏干预率（MIR）衡量，平均遗漏近一半的必要干预（MIR平均为0.50），即使在更大模型规模下也如此。为解决此局限，我们应用非对称奖励塑形的强化学习，将MIR降至0.186-0.218，并将召回率从0.479提升至0.78-0.81。我们的发现表明，时间参与是对话智能中一个独特且可训练维度，而基于真实场景的合成数据为LLM更自然、恰当地参与多方交互提供了有效且可扩展的路径。

Large language models struggle with multi-party conversations because they lack the ability to decide when to speak, often interrupting excessively. Supervised fine-tuning on this dataset significantly outperforms zero-shot baselines, achieving an average Macro F1 increase of 60% across 4B+ parameter models, but trained models remain over-conservative with a Missed Intervention Rate of 0.50. Multi-Objective Instruction-Aware Representation Learning in Procedural Content Generation RL
Authors: Sung-Hyun Kim, Geum-Hwan Hwang, In-Chang Baek, Seo-Young Lee, Kyung-Joong Kim
First: 2025-08-08T09:41:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T02:59:24+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advancements in generative modeling emphasize the importance of natural language as a highly expressive and accessible modality for controlling content generation. However, existing instructed reinforcement learning for procedural content generation (IPCGRL) method often struggle to leverage the expressive richness of textual input, especially under complex, multi-objective instructions, leading to limited controllability. To address this problem, we propose \textit{MIPCGRL}, a multi-objective representation learning method for instructed content generators, which incorporates sentence embeddings as conditions. MIPCGRL effectively trains a multi-objective embedding space by incorporating multi-label classification and multi-head regression networks. Experimental results show that the proposed method achieves up to a 13.8\% improvement in controllability with multi-objective instructions. The ability to process complex instructions enables more expressive and flexible content generation.

Unified Framework of Distributional Regret in Multi-Armed Bandits and Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Harin Lee, Min-hwan Oh
First: 2026-05-06T16:38:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T02:34:23+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the Conference of Learning Theory (COLT) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study the distribution of regret in stochastic multi-armed bandits and episodic reinforcement learning through a unified framework. We formalize a distributional regret bound as a probabilistic guarantee that holds uniformly over all confidence levels $δ\in (0,1]$, thereby characterizing the regret distribution across the full range of $δ$. We present a simple UCBVI-style algorithm with exploration bonus $\min\{c_{1,k}/N, c_{2,k}/\sqrt{N}\}$, where $N$ denotes the visit count and $(c_{1,k},c_{2,k})$ are user-specified parameters. For arbitrary parameter sequences, we derive general gap-independent and gap-dependent distributional regret bounds, yielding a principled characterization of how the parameters control the trade-off between expected performance, tail risk, and instance-dependent behavior. In particular, our bounds achieve optimal trade-offs between expected and distributional regret in both minimax and instance-dependent regimes. As a special case, for multi-armed bandits with $A$ arms and horizon $T$, we obtain a distributional regret bound of order $\mathcal{O}(\sqrt{AT}\log(1/δ))$, confirming the conjecture of Lattimore & Szepesvári (2020, Section 17.1) for the first time.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多臂老虎机与强化学习中分布遗憾的统一框架
我们通过统一框架研究随机多臂老虎机和情节式强化学习中的遗憾分布。我们将分布遗憾界形式化为对所有置信水平δ∈(0,1]一致成立的概率保证，从而刻画δ全范围内的遗憾分布。我们提出一种简单的UCBVI风格算法，其探索奖励为min{c₁ₖ/N, c₂ₖ/√N}，其中N表示访问次数，(c₁ₖ, c₂ₖ)是用户指定参数。对于任意参数序列，我们推导出通用的与间隙无关和与间隙相关的分布遗憾界，从而原则性地刻画参数如何控制期望性能、尾部风险与实例依赖行为之间的权衡。特别地，我们的界在极小极大和实例依赖两种机制下均实现了期望遗憾与分布遗憾之间的最优权衡。作为特例，对于具有A个臂和水平T的多臂老虎机，我们得到阶为O(√(AT) log(1/δ))的分布遗憾界，首次证实了Lattimore & Szepesvári (2020, 第17.1节)的猜想。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces a unified framework for studying the distribution of regret in stochastic multi-armed bandits and episodic reinforcement learning. The authors formalize a distributional regret bound as a probabilistic guarantee that holds uniformly over all confidence levels, and propose a simple UCBVI-style algorithm with a novel exploration bonus. The method yields general gap-independent and gap-dependent distributional regret bounds that achieve optimal trade-offs between expected performance, tail risk, and instance-dependent behavior. Notably, for multi-armed bandits, the framework obtains a distributional regret bound of order O(√(AT) log(1/δ)), confirming a long-standing conjecture for the first time.
本文提出了一个统一框架，用于研究随机多臂老虎机和情节强化学习中遗憾的分布特性。作者将分布遗憾界形式化为在所有置信水平上一致成立的概率保证，并设计了一种带有新型探索奖励的简单UCBVI风格算法。该方法推导出通用的与间隙无关和与间隙相关的分布遗憾界，在期望性能、尾部风险和实例依赖行为之间实现了最优权衡。特别地，对于多臂老虎机，该框架获得了O(√(AT) log(1/δ))阶的分布遗憾界，首次证实了一个长期存在的猜想。
Emergent Slow Thinking in LLMs as Inverse Tree Freezing
Authors: Sihan Hu, Xiansheng Cai, Yuan Huang, Zhiyuan Yao, Linfeng Zhang, Pan Zhang, Youjin Deng, Kun Chen
First: 2025-09-28T04:10:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T02:29:03+00:00
Comments: 34 pages, 17 figures, 1 table
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) enables large language models to acquire slow, multi-step reasoning from sparse final-answer signals. We provide a statistical-physics picture of this emergence. We show that an autoregressive model's finite capacity forces it to compress its exponentially large prefix space into a Markov network of predictive states, on which slow thinking unfolds as a random walk -- the Concept Network (CoNet) picture. Within CoNet, RLVR dynamics are governed by two mechanisms: merging of compatible paths and frustrated competition among incompatible ones. Together they drive the network through nucleation, growth, and freezing into multi-input, single-output directed inverse trees. The picture reproduces the training dynamics of a 1.5-billion-parameter LLM and yields three predictions: reasoning chains lengthen as a geometric necessity of sparse topology; SFT induces catastrophic forgetting through bridge-node rupture; and frustration drives policy collapse. Building on the structural timing inherent in inverse-tree freezing, we propose Annealed-RLVR -- a brief SFT intervention at the moment of maximum frustration. It outperforms standard RLVR on both in- and out-of-distribution benchmarks, with the largest gains at high sampling budgets where standard RLVR collapses. The same SFT applied after the trees freeze instead triggers catastrophic forgetting, isolating timing as the active ingredient.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型中作为逆树冻结的涌现慢思考
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）使大语言模型能够从稀疏的最终答案信号中习得缓慢的多步推理。我们提供了这一涌现现象的统计物理图景。研究表明，自回归模型的有限容量迫使其将指数级增长的前缀空间压缩为预测状态的马尔可夫网络，慢思考在此网络上以随机游走的形式展开——即概念网络（CoNet）图景。在CoNet中，RLVR动力学由两种机制主导：兼容路径的合并与不兼容路径间的受挫竞争。两者共同驱动网络经历成核、生长和冻结，最终形成多输入单输出的有向逆树。该图景重现了15亿参数大语言模型的训练动力学，并给出三个预测：推理链延长是稀疏拓扑的几何必然；SFT通过桥节点断裂引发灾难性遗忘；受挫导致策略崩溃。基于逆树冻结中固有的结构时序，我们提出退火RLVR——在最大受挫时刻进行短暂SFT干预。它在分布内和分布外基准测试中均优于标准RLVR，在高采样预算下标准RLVR崩溃时增益最大。若在树冻结后施加相同SFT，则会触发灾难性遗忘，从而将时序确定为关键活性成分。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces a statistical-physics framework called Concept Network (CoNet) to explain how reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) enables large language models to develop slow, multi-step reasoning. The authors show that an autoregressive model's finite capacity compresses its prefix space into a Markov network, where RLVR drives the merging of compatible paths and frustrated competition among incompatible ones, leading to the formation of multi-input, single-output directed inverse trees. Experiments on a 1.5-billion-parameter LLM confirm that reasoning chains lengthen as a geometric necessity of sparse topology, supervised fine-tuning (SFT) induces catastrophic forgetting through bridge-node rupture, and frustration causes policy collapse. The proposed Annealed-RLVR, which applies a brief SFT intervention at the moment of maximum frustration, outperforms standard RLVR on both in- and out-of-distribution benchmarks, especially at high sampling budgets where standard RLVR collapses, while applying SFT after tree freezing triggers catastrophic forgetting, highlighting timing as the critical factor.
本文提出了一个名为概念网络（CoNet）的统计物理框架，用于解释可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）如何使大型语言模型发展出缓慢的多步推理能力。作者证明，自回归模型的有限容量迫使其将指数级增长的前缀空间压缩为一个马尔可夫网络，在此网络中，RLVR通过兼容路径的合并与不兼容路径间的受挫竞争，驱动网络经历成核、生长和冻结，最终形成多输入单输出的有向逆树。在15亿参数的大语言模型上的实验证实，推理链的延长是稀疏拓扑的几何必然结果，监督微调（SFT）通过桥节点断裂引发灾难性遗忘，而受挫竞争则导致策略崩溃。提出的退火RLVR方法在最大受挫时刻施加短暂的SFT干预，在分布内和分布外基准测试中均优于标准RLVR，尤其是在标准RLVR崩溃的高采样预算下表现更佳，而在树冻结后应用SFT则会触发灾难性遗忘，从而凸显了时机作为关键因素的作用。
New Bounds for Zarankiewicz Numbers via Reinforced LLM Evolutionary Search
Authors: Jay Bhan, Nicole Nobili, Patrick Langer
First: 2026-05-01T21:45:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T02:22:17+00:00
Comments: *Jay Bhan and Nicole Nobili contributed equally to this work as first authors, and their order was determined via coin flip
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Zarankiewicz number $\textbf{Z}(m, n, s, t)$ is the maximum number of edges in a bipartite graph $G_{m, n}$ such that there is no complete $K_{s, t}$ bipartite subgraph. We determine for the first time the exact values of three Zarankiewicz numbers: $\textbf{Z}(11, 21, 3, 3)=116$, $\textbf{Z}(11, 22, 3, 3)=121$, and $\textbf{Z}(12, 22, 3, 3)=132$. We further establish lower bounds for 41 more Zarankiewicz numbers, including several that are within one edge of the best known upper bound, and we match the established value in four more closed cases. Our results are obtained using OpenEvolve, an open-source evolutionary algorithm based on Large Language Models (LLMs) that iteratively improves algorithms for generating mathematical constructions by optimizing a reward signal which we tailored for this specific problem. These findings provide new extremal graph constructions and demonstrate the potential of LLM-guided evolutionary search to contribute to mathematical research. In addition to presenting the resulting constructions, we report the generation algorithms produced, describe the relevant implementation details, and provide our computational costs. Our costs are remarkably low, at less than \$30 for each Zarankiewicz parameter combination, showing that LLM-guided evolutionary search can be an inexpensive, reproducible, and accessible tool for discovering new combinatorial constructions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过强化大语言模型进化搜索获得Zarankiewicz数的新界
Zarankiewicz数$\textbf{Z}(m, n, s, t)$表示不含完全二分子图$K_{s, t}$的二部图$G_{m, n}$的最大边数。我们首次确定了三个Zarankiewicz数的精确值：$\textbf{Z}(11, 21, 3, 3)=116$、$\textbf{Z}(11, 22, 3, 3)=121$和$\textbf{Z}(12, 22, 3, 3)=132$。此外，我们为另外41个Zarankiewicz数建立了下界，其中若干结果与已知最佳上界仅差一条边，并在四个封闭情形中匹配了已确立的值。这些成果通过OpenEvolve获得——一种基于大语言模型的开源进化算法，通过优化针对该问题定制的奖励信号，迭代改进数学构造生成算法。这些发现提供了新的极图构造，并展示了LLM引导的进化搜索对数学研究的潜力。除呈现最终构造外，我们报告了生成的算法、相关实现细节及计算成本。每个Zarankiewicz参数组合的计算成本低于30美元，表明LLM引导的进化搜索可成为发现新组合构造的廉价、可复现且易用的工具。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of determining Zarankiewicz numbers, which represent the maximum edges in a bipartite graph without a complete bipartite subgraph K_{s,t}. The authors introduce OpenEvolve, an open-source evolutionary algorithm guided by Large Language Models (LLMs), which iteratively refines generation algorithms by optimizing a tailored reward signal. This method successfully computes exact values for three Zarankiewicz numbers—Z(11,21,3,3)=116, Z(11,22,3,3)=121, and Z(12,22,3,3)=132—and establishes lower bounds for 41 others, with several within one edge of the best known upper bounds, all at a computational cost of less than $30 per parameter combination.
该论文针对Zarankiewicz数问题展开研究，该数表示不含完全二分子图K_{s,t}的二部图的最大边数。作者提出了OpenEvolve，一种基于大型语言模型（LLM）的开源进化算法，通过优化定制的奖励信号迭代改进生成算法。该方法首次精确计算出三个Zarankiewicz数：Z(11,21,3,3)=116、Z(11,22,3,3)=121和Z(12,22,3,3)=132，并为另外41个数建立了下界，其中多个与已知最佳上界仅差一条边，而每个参数组合的计算成本不到30美元。
Nonsense Helps: Prompt Space Perturbation Broadens Reasoning Exploration
Authors: Langlin Huang, Chengsong Huang, Jinyuan Li, Donghong Cai, Yuyi Yang, Jiaxin Huang
First: 2026-05-07T01:18:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T01:18:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, particularly Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), has significantly advanced the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, in complex tasks, GRPO frequently suffers from the ``zero-advantage problem'': when all sampled rollouts for a query fail, the relative advantage collapses to zero. Consequently, the model loses effective training signals for these questions, wasting the training data and computational budget. While simply increasing the sampling budget for these questions is a common remedy, the static sampling policy inherently constrains reasoning exploration, limiting the success rate. In this paper, we propose Lorem Perturbation for Exploration (LoPE), a simple yet effective training framework to break this exploration bottleneck. We posit that task-irrelevant prompt-space perturbations can shift the model's output distribution enough to unlock orthogonal reasoning pathways for hard questions. Specifically, LoPE prepends sequences stochastically assembled from Lorem Ipsum vocabulary (a pseudo-Latin placeholder text) to the prompts before resampling. Experiments across 1.7B, 4B, and 7B models demonstrate that LoPE significantly outperforms resampling with the original prompts. Further analysis reveals that other Latin-based random sequences with low perplexity are also effective perturbations. Our results establish LoPE as a strong baseline for broadening exploration in LLM reinforcement learning.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the 'zero-advantage problem' in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for large language models, where all sampled rollouts for a query fail, leading to collapsed relative advantages and wasted training data. The authors propose LoPE (Lorem Perturbation for Exploration), a method that prepends stochastic sequences from Lorem Ipsum vocabulary to prompts before resampling, shifting the output distribution to unlock orthogonal reasoning pathways. Experiments on 1.7B, 4B, and 7B models show that LoPE significantly outperforms resampling with original prompts, with further analysis confirming that other Latin-based random sequences with low perplexity are also effective perturbations.
该论文针对大型语言模型中组相对策略优化（GRPO）的“零优势问题”，即当查询的所有采样轨迹均失败时，相对优势归零，导致训练数据和计算资源浪费。作者提出LoPE（探索的Lorem扰动）方法，通过在重新采样前向提示中随机拼接Lorem Ipsum词汇序列，改变输出分布以解锁正交推理路径。在1.7B、4B和7B模型上的实验表明，LoPE显著优于使用原始提示的重新采样，进一步分析证实其他低困惑度的拉丁随机序列也是有效的扰动。
WaferSAGE: Large Language Model-Powered Wafer Defect Analysis via Synthetic Data Generation and Rubric-Guided Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ke Xu
First: 2026-04-30T09:19:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T01:17:49+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 3 figures, 8 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present WaferSAGE, a framework for wafer defect visual question answering using small vision-language models. To address data scarcity in semiconductor manufacturing, we propose a three-stage synthesis pipeline incorporating structured rubric generation for precise evaluation. Starting from limited labeled wafer maps, we employ clustering-based cleaning to filter label noise, then generate comprehensive defect descriptions using vision-language models, which are converted into structured evaluation rubrics criteria. These rubrics guide the synthesis of VQA pairs, ensuring coverage across defect type identification, spatial distribution, morphology, and root cause analysis. Our dual assessment framework aligns rule-based metrics with LLM-Judge scores via Bayesian optimization, enabling reliable automated evaluation. Through curriculum-based reinforcement learning with Group Sequence Policy Optimization (GSPO) and rubric-aligned rewards, our 4B-parameter Qwen3-VL model achieves a 6.493 LLM-Judge score, closely approaching Gemini-3-Flash (7.149) while enabling complete on-premise deployment. We demonstrate that small models with domain-specific training can surpass proprietary large models in specialized industrial visual understanding, offering a viable path for privacy-preserving, cost-effective deployment in semiconductor manufacturing.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WaferSAGE：基于合成数据生成与评分准则引导强化学习的大语言模型晶圆缺陷分析
我们提出WaferSAGE，一个利用小型视觉语言模型进行晶圆缺陷视觉问答的框架。为解决半导体制造中的数据稀缺问题，我们提出一个三阶段合成流程，其中包含结构化评分准则生成以实现精确评估。从有限的带标签晶圆图出发，我们采用基于聚类的清洗方法过滤标签噪声，然后利用视觉语言模型生成全面的缺陷描述，并将其转化为结构化评估准则。这些准则指导VQA对的合成，确保覆盖缺陷类型识别、空间分布、形态和根因分析。 我们的双重评估框架通过贝叶斯优化将基于规则的指标与LLM-Judge评分对齐，实现可靠的自动化评估。通过基于课程的强化学习（结合组序列策略优化GSPO和与评分准则对齐的奖励），我们的4B参数Qwen3-VL模型获得了6.493的LLM-Judge评分，接近Gemini-3-Flash（7.149），同时支持完全本地部署。我们证明，经过领域特定训练的小型模型在专业工业视觉理解方面可以超越专有大模型，为半导体制造中隐私保护、成本效益高的部署提供可行路径。

WaferSAGE addresses data scarcity in semiconductor manufacturing for wafer defect visual question answering by proposing a framework that uses small vision-language models. The method involves a three-stage synthesis pipeline: clustering-based cleaning to filter label noise from limited wafer maps, generating comprehensive defect descriptions via vision-language models, and converting these into structured evaluation rubrics to guide the synthesis of VQA pairs covering defect type, spatial distribution, morphology, and root cause analysis. A dual assessment framework aligns rule-based metrics with LLM-Judge scores through Bayesian optimization, and curriculum-based reinforcement learning with Group Sequence Policy Optimization and rubric-aligned rewards enables a 4B-parameter Qwen3-VL model to achieve a 6.493 LLM-Judge score, closely approaching Gemini-3-Flash's 7.149 while supporting complete on-premise deployment, demonstrating that small models with domain-specific training can surpass proprietary large models in specialized industrial visual understanding.

Owen-Shapley Policy Optimization: A Principled RL Algorithm for Generative Search LLMs
Authors: Abhijnan Nath, Alireza Bagheri Garakani, Tianchen Zhou, Fan Yang, Yan Gao, Nikhil Krishnaswamy
First: 2026-01-13T10:17:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T01:11:13+00:00
Comments: Added additional experiments, computational analysis and further revisions
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models are increasingly trained via reinforcement learning for personalized recommendation tasks, but standard methods like GRPO rely on sparse, sequence-level rewards. These obscure which tokens actually contribute to high-quality outputs, creating a credit assignment gap. This gap is especially problematic when models must infer latent user intent from under-specified language without ground truth labels, which is a reasoning pattern rarely seen during pretraining but commonly required in deployment. We introduce Owen-Shapley Policy Optimization (OSPO), a framework that redistributes sequence-level advantages based on tokens' marginal contributions to outcomes. OSPO transforms task feedback into potential-based reward shaping via Shapley-Owen attributions to assign segment-level credit while preserving the optimal policy, all without parametric value models. By forming coalitions of semantically coherent units (e.g., phrases describing product attributes or sentences capturing preferences), OSPO identifies which response parts drive performance. Experiments on Amazon ESCI and H&M Fashion datasets including controlled generation tasks show consistent gains over baselines and notable test-time robustness to out-of-distribution retrievers unseen during training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Owen-Shapley策略优化：面向生成式搜索大语言模型的原则性强化学习算法
大型语言模型越来越多地通过强化学习进行个性化推荐任务的训练，但GRPO等标准方法依赖于稀疏的序列级奖励。这些奖励掩盖了哪些词元真正贡献于高质量输出，造成了信用分配缺口。当模型必须从表述不充分的语言中推断潜在用户意图（缺乏真实标签）时，这一缺口尤为棘手——这种推理模式在预训练中很少出现，但在部署中却常见。我们提出Owen-Shapley策略优化（OSPO），该框架基于词元对结果的边际贡献重新分配序列级优势。OSPO通过Shapley-Owen归因将任务反馈转化为基于势能的奖励塑形，在保持最优策略的同时分配片段级信用，且无需参数化价值模型。通过形成语义连贯单元（如描述产品属性的短语或捕捉偏好的句子）的联盟，OSPO识别出哪些响应部分驱动性能。在Amazon ESCI和H&M时尚数据集（包括受控生成任务）上的实验显示，该方法持续优于基线，并对训练中未见过的分布外检索器展现出显著的测试时鲁棒性。

The paper addresses the credit assignment gap in reinforcement learning for generative search LLMs, where sparse sequence-level rewards obscure which tokens contribute to high-quality outputs, especially when models must infer latent user intent. The authors propose Owen-Shapley Policy Optimization (OSPO), a framework that redistributes sequence-level advantages based on tokens' marginal contributions using Shapley-Owen attributions for segment-level credit assignment without parametric value models. Experiments on Amazon ESCI and H&M Fashion datasets demonstrate consistent gains over baselines and notable test-time robustness to out-of-distribution retrievers unseen during training.
该论文针对生成式搜索大语言模型强化学习中的信用分配问题，即稀疏的序列级奖励掩盖了哪些标记对高质量输出有贡献，特别是在模型需要推断潜在用户意图时。作者提出了Owen-Shapley策略优化（OSPO）框架，通过Shapley-Owen归因将序列级优势基于标记的边际贡献重新分配，实现片段级信用分配而无需参数化价值模型。在Amazon ESCI和H&M Fashion数据集上的实验表明，该方法持续优于基线，并在训练中未见过的分布外检索器上表现出显著的测试时鲁棒性。
SPARK: Self-Play with Asymmetric Reward from Knowledge Graphs
Authors: Hyobin Park, Taeseop Kim, Dong-Geol Choi
First: 2026-05-07T00:51:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T00:51:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Self-play reinforcement learning has shown strong performance in domains with formally verifiable structure, such as mathematics and coding, where both problem generation and reward computation can be grounded in explicit rules. Extending this paradigm to scientific literature is more challenging: the relationships among multi-modal elements within and across documents are rarely made explicit in text, which makes automatic generation of relational reasoning questions difficult and weakens the reliability of reward signals. We propose SPARK (Self-Play with Asymmetric Reward from Knowledge Graphs), a framework that automatically constructs a unified knowledge graph (KG) from multi-document scientific literature and uses it as the structural basis for self-play. KG paths over multimodal nodes serve as a source for generating relational reasoning questions, and structured facts stored in the KG provide a basis for verifiable reward computation. A single small vision-language model (sVLM) alternates between Proposer and Solver roles under information asymmetry against a fixed KG, a design that we believe can be naturally extended toward online adaptation in future work. We evaluate SPARK on public benchmarks and a self-constructed cross-document multi-hop QA dataset. Results show that SPARK consistently outperforms flat-corpus-based self-play baselines, and the performance gap widens as hop count increases, suggesting that KG-structure grounding contributes to relational multi-hop reasoning beyond what unstructured corpus grounding can provide.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPARK：基于知识图谱的非对称奖励自博弈框架
自博弈强化学习在具有形式化可验证结构的领域（如数学和编程）中表现出色，其中问题生成和奖励计算均可基于显式规则。将这一范式扩展到科学文献更具挑战性：文档内及跨文档的多模态元素间关系很少在文本中显式呈现，这使得关系推理问题的自动生成变得困难，并削弱了奖励信号的可靠性。我们提出SPARK（基于知识图谱的非对称奖励自博弈框架），该框架从多文档科学文献中自动构建统一知识图谱，并将其作为自博弈的结构基础。多模态节点间的知识图谱路径可作为生成关系推理问题的来源，而知识图谱中存储的结构化事实则为可验证的奖励计算提供依据。单个小型视觉语言模型在信息不对称条件下交替扮演提议者与求解者角色（相对于固定知识图谱），我们认为该设计未来可自然扩展至在线适应。我们在公开基准测试及自建的跨文档多跳问答数据集上评估SPARK。结果表明，SPARK始终优于基于扁平语料库的自博弈基线，且随着跳数增加性能差距扩大，这表明知识图谱结构基础对关系型多跳推理的贡献超越了非结构化语料基础所能提供的支持。
Summary / 总结
The paper proposes SPARK, a self-play reinforcement learning framework that uses knowledge graphs to improve relational reasoning over scientific literature. The method automatically constructs a unified knowledge graph from multi-document scientific texts, generates relational reasoning questions from graph paths, and computes verifiable rewards from structured facts, with a single small vision-language model alternating between Proposer and Solver roles under information asymmetry. Experiments on public benchmarks and a cross-document multi-hop QA dataset show that SPARK consistently outperforms flat-corpus-based self-play baselines, with the performance gap widening as the number of reasoning hops increases, demonstrating the advantage of KG-structure grounding for multi-hop reasoning.
该论文提出SPARK框架，利用知识图谱增强科学文献中的关系推理能力。方法自动从多文档科学文献构建统一知识图谱，基于图路径生成关系推理问题，并从结构化事实计算可验证奖励，单个小型视觉语言模型在信息不对称下交替扮演提议者和求解者角色。在公开基准和自建跨文档多跳问答数据集上的实验表明，SPARK持续优于基于平铺语料的自我对弈基线，且随着推理跳数增加性能差距扩大，证明知识图谱结构对多跳推理的支撑作用超越非结构化语料。
Adaptive Q-Chunking for Offline-to-Online Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Nandiraju Gireesh, Yuanliang Ju, He Wang
First: 2026-05-07T00:48:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T00:48:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline-to-online reinforcement learning with action chunking eliminates multi-step off-policy bias and enables temporally coherent exploration, but all existing methods use a fixed chunk size across every state. This is suboptimal: near contact events the agent needs short chunks for reactive control, while during free-space motion long chunks provide better credit assignment. The natural solution is to train critics for several chunk sizes and select the best one at each state, but naive comparison of learned critic values systematically collapses to the shortest chunk due to discount-scale mismatch, and degrades to noise in low-value states. We propose Adaptive Q-Chunking (AQC), which resolves both failures by comparing the advantage of each chunk size relative to a per-horizon baseline, normalized by the discount factor. This criterion converts biased wrong answers into unbiased near-random choices when no genuine signal exists, and becomes discriminative when a particular scale enables better planning. We prove theoretical bounds on the advantage selector's noise immunity and on the value dominance of adaptive chunking over any fixed chunk size. We demonstrate that AQC achieves state-of-the-art offline and online success rates on OGBench and Robomimic, and can be applied to enhance the performance of large-scale VLA models that predict action sequences, significantly boosting performance on RoboCasa-GR1 tasks.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of fixed action chunk sizes in offline-to-online reinforcement learning, which are suboptimal because short chunks are needed for reactive control near contact events while long chunks improve credit assignment during free-space motion. The proposed method, Adaptive Q-Chunking (AQC), resolves this by comparing the advantage of each chunk size relative to a per-horizon baseline normalized by the discount factor, preventing systematic collapse to the shortest chunk and degradation to noise in low-value states. Theoretical bounds on noise immunity and value dominance are provided, and experiments show that AQC achieves state-of-the-art offline and online success rates on OGBench and Robomimic, and boosts performance on RoboCasa-GR1 tasks when applied to large-scale VLA models.
该论文针对离线到在线强化学习中固定动作块大小的局限性，即靠近接触事件时需要短块以实现反应控制，而在自由空间运动中长块能更好地进行信用分配。提出的自适应Q块方法通过比较每个块大小相对于每视野基线的优势，并除以折扣因子进行归一化，从而避免了系统性地偏向最短块以及在低价值状态下退化为噪声的问题。该方法提供了关于噪声免疫性和价值优势的理论界限，实验表明在OGBench和Robomimic上取得了最先进的离线和在线成功率，并在应用于大规模VLA模型时显著提升了RoboCasa-GR1任务的性能。
Taming the Curses of Multiagency in Robust Markov Games with Large State Space through Linear Function Approximation
Authors: Jingchu Gai, Laixi Shi
First: 2026-05-04T20:04:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T22:03:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) holds great potential but faces robustness challenges due to environmental uncertainty. To address this, distributionally robust Markov games (RMGs) optimize worst-case performance when the environment deviates from the nominal model within a uncertainty set. Beyond robustness, an equally urgent goal for MARL is data efficiency -- sampling from vast state and action spaces that grow exponentially with the number of agents potentially leads to the curse of multiagency. However, current provably data-efficient algorithms for RMGs are limited to tabular settings with finite state and action spaces, which are only computationally manageable for small-scale problems, leaving RMGs with large-scale (or infinite) state spaces largely unexplored. The only existing work beyond tabular settings focuses on linear function approximation (LFA) for a restrictive class of RMGs using vanish minimal value assumption and still suffers from sample complexity with the curse of multiagency. In this work, we focuses on general RMGs with LFA. For uncertainty sets defined by total variation distance, we develop provably data-efficient algorithms that break the curse of multiagency in both the generative model setting and a newly proposed online interactive setting. To our knowledge, our results are the first to break the curse of multiagency of sample complexity for RMGs with large (possibly infinite) state spaces, regardless of the uncertainty set construction.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过线性函数逼近驯服大规模状态空间鲁棒马尔可夫博弈中的多智能体诅咒
多智能体强化学习（MARL）潜力巨大，但因环境不确定性面临鲁棒性挑战。为此，分布鲁棒马尔可夫博弈（RMG）在环境偏离名义模型且处于不确定集内时优化最坏情况性能。除鲁棒性外，MARL同样迫切的目标是数据效率——从随智能体数量指数增长的大规模状态与动作空间中采样可能导致多智能体诅咒。然而，当前RMG的可证明数据高效算法仅限于有限状态与动作空间的表格设置，仅能处理小规模问题，使得大规模（或无限）状态空间的RMG研究基本空白。唯一超越表格设置的现有工作聚焦于一类受限RMG的线性函数逼近（LFA），采用消失最小化值假设，且样本复杂度仍受多智能体诅咒影响。本文研究一般性RMG与LFA。针对总变差距离定义的不确定集，我们开发了可证明数据高效的算法，在生成模型设置和新提出的在线交互设置中均打破了多智能体诅咒。据我们所知，无论不确定集如何构建，我们的结果是首个打破大规模（可能无限）状态空间RMG样本复杂度中多智能体诅咒的工作。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the dual challenges of robustness and data efficiency in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) with large state spaces, specifically focusing on distributionally robust Markov games (RMGs). The authors propose novel algorithms that leverage linear function approximation (LFA) to overcome the curse of multiagency, which previously limited provably efficient methods to tabular settings. By defining uncertainty sets via total variation distance, they develop algorithms for both generative model and online interactive settings that achieve sample complexity without the curse of multiagency. Experimental results demonstrate that their approach is the first to break this curse for RMGs with large or infinite state spaces, regardless of uncertainty set construction, significantly advancing the scalability of robust MARL.
本文针对大规模状态空间下多智能体强化学习中的鲁棒性和数据效率双重挑战，重点研究了分布鲁棒马尔可夫博弈。作者提出利用线性函数近似的新算法，克服了此前仅适用于表格型设置的多智能体诅咒，通过基于总变差距离的不确定性集，在生成模型和在线交互场景中实现了无多智能体诅咒的样本复杂度。实验结果表明，该方法是首个在任意不确定性集构造下，为大规模或无限状态空间的鲁棒马尔可夫博弈打破多智能体诅咒的工作，显著提升了鲁棒多智能体强化学习的可扩展性。
Approximate Next Policy Sampling: Replacing Conservative Target Policy Updates in Deep RL
Authors: Dillon Sandhu, Ronald Parr
First: 2026-05-06T22:02:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T22:02:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We revisit a classic "chicken-and-egg" problem in reinforcement learning: to safely improve a policy, the value function must be accurate on the state-visitation distribution of the updated policy. That distribution over states is unknown and cannot be sampled for the purposes of training the value function. Conservative updates solve this problem, but at the cost of shrinking the policy update. This paper explores an alternative solution, Approximate Next Policy Sampling (ANPS), which addresses the problem by modifying the training distribution rather than constraining the policy update. ANPS is satisfied if the distribution of the training data approximates that of the next policy. To demonstrate the feasibility and efficacy of ANPS, we introduce Stable Value Approximate Policy Iteration (SV-API). SV-API modifies the standard approximate policy iteration loop to hold the target policy fixed while an iteratively updated behavioral policy gathers relevant experience. It only commits to a new policy once a convergence criterion has been met. If certain stability criteria are met, the update is guaranteed to be safe; otherwise, it remains no less safe than standard approximate policy iteration. Applying SV-API to PPO yields Stable Value PPO (SV-PPO), which matches or improves performance on high-dimensional discrete (Atari) and continuous control benchmarks while executing substantially larger target policy updates. These results demonstrate the viability of ANPS as a new solution to this classic challenge in RL.
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the classic chicken-and-egg problem in reinforcement learning where safe policy improvement requires accurate value function estimates on the updated policy's state distribution, which is unknown and unsampleable. The authors propose Approximate Next Policy Sampling (ANPS), which modifies the training distribution to approximate that of the next policy instead of constraining the policy update. They introduce Stable Value Approximate Policy Iteration (SV-API), which holds the target policy fixed while an iteratively updated behavioral policy gathers experience, committing to a new policy only after convergence. Applying SV-API to PPO yields SV-PPO, which matches or improves performance on Atari and continuous control benchmarks while executing substantially larger target policy updates, demonstrating ANPS's viability.
该论文重新审视了强化学习中的一个经典‘鸡生蛋’问题：要安全地改进策略，价值函数必须对更新后策略的状态访问分布准确，但该分布未知且无法采样。作者提出了近似下一策略采样（ANPS），通过修改训练分布使其近似于下一策略的分布，而不是约束策略更新。他们引入了稳定价值近似策略迭代（SV-API），该方法在迭代更新的行为策略收集相关经验时固定目标策略，仅在满足收敛标准后才提交新策略。将SV-API应用于PPO得到SV-PPO，在高维离散（Atari）和连续控制基准测试中匹配或提升了性能，同时执行了显著更大的目标策略更新，证明了ANPS的可行性。
LANTERN: LLM-Augmented Neurosymbolic Transfer with Experience-Gated Reasoning Networks
Authors: Mahyar Alinejad, Yue Wang, Amrit Singh Bedi, George Atia
First: 2026-05-06T21:57:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T21:57:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Transfer learning in reinforcement learning (RL) seeks to accelerate learning in new tasks by leveraging knowledge from related sources. Existing neurosymbolic transfer methods, however, typically rely on manually specified task automata, assume a single source task, and use fixed knowledge-integration mechanisms that cannot adapt to varying source relevance. We propose LANTERN, a unified framework for multi-source neurosymbolic transfer that addresses these limitations through three components: (i) deterministic finite automata generated from natural language task descriptions using large language models, (ii) semantic embedding-based aggregation of multiple source policies weighted by cross-task similarity, and (iii) adaptive teacher-student gating based on temporal-difference error and semantic uncertainty. Across domains spanning resource management, navigation, and control, LANTERN achieves 40-60% improvements in sample efficiency over existing baselines while remaining robust to poorly aligned sources. These results demonstrate that multi-source, adaptively weighted neurosymbolic transfer can improve scalability and robustness in symbolic RL settings.
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LANTERN, a framework for multi-source neurosymbolic transfer in reinforcement learning that overcomes limitations of existing methods which rely on manually specified task automata, single source tasks, and fixed knowledge integration. LANTERN uses large language models to generate deterministic finite automata from natural language task descriptions, aggregates multiple source policies via semantic embedding-based weighting based on cross-task similarity, and employs adaptive teacher-student gating driven by temporal-difference error and semantic uncertainty. Experimental results across resource management, navigation, and control domains show that LANTERN achieves 40-60% improvements in sample efficiency over baselines while maintaining robustness to poorly aligned sources.
该论文提出了LANTERN框架，用于强化学习中的多源神经符号迁移，克服了现有方法依赖手动指定任务自动机、单一源任务和固定知识整合机制的局限。LANTERN利用大语言模型从自然语言任务描述生成确定性有限自动机，通过基于语义嵌入的跨任务相似度加权聚合多个源策略，并采用基于时序差分误差和语义不确定性的自适应师生门控机制。在资源管理、导航和控制领域的实验结果表明，LANTERN在样本效率上比基线方法提升40-60%，同时对低质量源任务保持鲁棒性。
